Got it — no code, no plan, no project outline. Just the inspiration map.

Here's a 360° view of real companies doing parts of what you're describing, organized by layer:



Client Portal \& Agency Operations Layer

Vendasta — white-label platform for agencies managing SMB clients, with multi-tier access (agency → client → location)

GoHighLevel — all-in-one agency platform with sub-account structure, white-labeling, and client portals

Clientjoy — CRM built specifically for agencies to manage clients, proposals, and onboarding

Plutio — agency workspace with client portals, project tracking, and role-based access

Bonsai Agency — client portal, contracts, onboarding, and task management for freelancers and agencies



Reporting \& Analytics Dashboard Layer

AgencyAnalytics — multi-client dashboards pulling SEO, social, ads, and web data with white-label client access

DashThis — automated marketing reporting for agencies, per-client dashboards

Whatagraph — cross-channel marketing reports with client-sharing and white-label options

Databox — KPI dashboards pulling from HubSpot, GA, and other tools with team/client sharing

Reportz — white-label reporting for digital agencies



Social Media Monitoring Layer (without Meta API)

Sprout Social — social analytics, listening, and performance tracking across platforms

Metricool — social analytics with competitor benchmarking and scheduling, lighter API dependency

Pallyy — social media management with analytics per brand/account

Brand24 — social listening and mention tracking by domain/brand name



HubSpot-Native or HubSpot-Adjacent Layer

Syncari — data orchestration and HubSpot sync layer for RevOps teams

Operations Hub (HubSpot) — native RevOps layer inside HubSpot, which is a direct comp for part of your tooling

Breadcrumbs.io — lead scoring and revenue attribution built on top of HubSpot data

Coefficient — pulls HubSpot data into Google Sheets/Excel for live client reporting



Training Academy \& LMS Layer

Trainual — SOPs and training platform for SMBs, with role-based access and progress tracking

LearnWorlds — white-label LMS with video courses, quizzes, and certificates

Teachable / Thinkific — course delivery with student progress tracking and completion certificates

TalentLMS — multi-tenant LMS with branching (like your partner/client hierarchy)

Northpass (now Gainsight PX Academy) — customer education platform inside SaaS products



Digital Certificate \& Credential Layer

Credly — digital badge and certificate issuance after course completion

Accredible — certificate generation tied to LMS completion, shareable on LinkedIn/social



Benchmark \& Industry Comparison Layer

Klipfolio — business metrics with industry benchmarking views

Databox Benchmarks — HubSpot-connected benchmarks by industry/company size

Visible.vc — investor-facing metrics with benchmark overlays for SaaS companies



Multi-Tenant SaaS Infrastructure Closest to Your Full Vision

Vendasta (again — worth studying deeply, most similar full-stack structure)

GoHighLevel (closest in spirit to what you're building end-to-end)

White Label Suite — white-label tools specifically for HubSpot agencies

Gemini reply

This is a comprehensive vision for a RevOps "Operating System" that bridges the gap between high-level consultancy and technical implementation. To give you the "360-degree" view you requested for inspiration, here are the companies and platforms that lead the world in the specific layers of your proposed software:

1\. The "Data Engine" \& Full-Funnel Visibility (Stages 1–4)

For the tracking of sessions, conversions, and the transition from MQL to SQL to Opportunity, these companies have mastered the "GTM Engineering" visualization:

HockeyStack: They are currently the gold standard for "Unified GTM Data." They track every touchpoint from the first website session to the final deal without requiring complex manual tagging. They excel at the "Conversion Rate" and "Industry Benchmark" views you described.

Factors.ai: Excellent for Stage 1 and 2 (View \& Subscribe). They focus heavily on "Account-Based" signals and website deanonymization, showing exactly which companies are visiting and how they move through the funnel.

Clay: For your Stage 2 (Social/Scraping) and Stage 3 (Lead enrichment), Clay is the "programmable engine" of choice. They allow you to build custom scrapers and waterfalls to find data (like social media impressions or LinkedIn activity) without relying solely on traditional APIs.

2\. The "Customer Portal" \& Layered Access (Admin/Manager/Employee)

For the 3-layer access and the "View only/Comment" functionality you mentioned for Ops Solutions:

Arrows.to: This is a HubSpot-native onboarding platform. It allows you to create customer-facing "plans" where you can share progress, upload documents, and set tasks. It’s a great example of how to make a CRM-driven project feel like a high-end SAAS experience for the client.

Dock: They specialize in "Digital Sales Rooms" and "Client Portals." Their logic for "View only" versus "Collaborator" access is very similar to what you are describing for your Admin/Manager/Employee layers.

3\. The "Academy" \& Sequential Training (Courses \& Certificates)

For the training material, sequential locking, and automated certificate generation using templates:

Skilljar: A leader in "Customer Education" platforms. They handle the "Sequential Learning" path perfectly—meaning a user cannot skip ahead until the previous step is finished.

Northpass (by Gainsight): This is built for scale. It allows you to provide different "learning paths" based on the customer’s plan (e.g., Video vs. Doc only) and provides deep analytics on who is actually completing the training.

Trainual: While internal-focused, their UI for "tips, tricks, and day-to-day guidelines" is the benchmark for making complex processes easy for an "Employee" level user to follow.

4\. The "HubSpot Enhancement" \& Audit Layer (Before/After)

For showing the "Enhancements" and "Before/After" snapshots of a HubSpot portal:

Supered: They provide "Process Overlays" directly inside HubSpot. This is a great inspiration for your "tips and tricks" tab, as they show the user how to do their work while they are inside the CRM.

RevOps.io: Though focused on the "Deal Desk," their ability to show a "History of Changes" and "Audit Trail" is a strong reference for your "Before/After" enhancement documentation.

Summary of the "Ops Solutions" SaaS Advantage

The companies above each do one part of your plan. Your unique advantage is the Unified Layer:

The Architect View: You (Mostafa) see the tokens and technical health.

The Action Layer: The customer sees the funnel progress.

The Education Layer: The employee learns how to use the "GTM Engine" you built.

I have reviewed your background as a Revenue Operations Manager with a Six Sigma Green Belt and your shift toward specialized "Vibe Coding" and custom reporting. This software is the logical evolution of your current consultancy.

Does one of these specific layers (The Data Engine, The Academy, or the HubSpot Audit) feel like the most critical "First Step" to build in Lovable?

Deepseek reply

Based on your detailed request and the search results, I have compiled a comprehensive market analysis and a 360-degree view of potential solutions. This information is intended to help you explore the competitive landscape and plan your next steps without generating any code or project plans at this time.



\---



\### 🏢 Category 1: Direct Competitors / Near Exact Matches



This category includes platforms designed to solve the specific problem of a HubSpot consultant or RevOps manager providing a client-facing portal.



\*   \*\*Noloco\*\*: This is a strong direct match. It allows you to build a fully customized \*\*partner portal\*\* on top of your HubSpot data. Key features include a secure, branded interface where clients can log in to \*\*access documentation, track deals, and communicate with internal teams\*\*. It supports multi-tier permissions (Admin, Agent, Client) and can streamline client onboarding by automating data capture.

\*   \*\*PartnerPortal.io\*\*: This is a dedicated \*\*PRM (Partner Relationship Management)\*\* platform. While it focuses on managing resellers, the core concept of a self-serve portal for partners to track deals and access resources is directly applicable to your need.

\*   \*\*Bripes (formerly ProRequests)\*\*: This is a \*\*white-label client portal software\*\* built specifically for agencies to manage projects, communications, and billing all in one place. Its focus on agency infrastructure and the ability for clients to log in and view updates makes it a close parallel to your vision.

\*   \*\*Introw\*\*: Billed as the "#1 Partner Portal on top of HubSpot and Salesforce," this platform specializes in launching a personalized portal for managing partners and resellers.



\### 🧩 Category 2: Core Functional Components (Your Tech Stack Inspirations)



This category breaks down the major features you've described and identifies companies that excel in each area. This will help you think about building your solution as an integration of best-in-class tools.



\#### 1. Multi-Tier Permissions \& Client Reporting



This is the foundation of your client access and data visibility feature.



\*   \*\*SpaceGo\*\*: A white-label ready platform that includes contracts, e-signatures, project tracking, and file sharing, all with a \*\*custom domain\*\*.

\*   \*\*ZenOps (built on Softr)\*\*: This is a perfect example of what can be built. It features an admin dashboard to manage clients and projects, and it provides \*\*employee-specific logins\*\* to view assigned tasks, as well as \*\*client-facing portals\*\* for project updates.

\*   \*\*Closely\*\*: This platform emphasizes a \*\*white-label client portal\*\* where clients see only your branding and have controlled access to campaigns and reports.

\*   \*\*AgencyAnalytics\*\*: A leading tool for agencies to monitor client metrics. It can integrate with various data sources, including \*\*Matomo for website analytics\*\*, to create automated, branded reports for clients.



\#### 2. Training Academy \& LMS (Learning Management System)



This addresses your need for a white-labeled academy to train client teams and issue certificates.



\*   \*\*LearnWorlds\*\*: A powerful, white-label LMS that allows you to launch \*\*fully branded academies\*\* for clients. It offers robust certification features, including the ability to create "Program Paths" that group courses into a learning journey that issues a certificate upon completion.

\*   \*\*CYPHER Learning\*\*: Offers a strong \*\*multi-tenant architecture\*\*, which means you can create and manage \*\*multiple branded portals\*\* for different clients under a single account. This is ideal for an agency model.

\*   \*\*WorkRamp\*\*: Known for its "Embedded Learning Cloud," which allows you to \*\*white-label and embed\*\* their LMS functionality directly within your platform, providing a seamless experience.



\#### 3. Analytics \& Reporting (Web Analytics \& Lead Funnel)



This covers your needs for website analytics, form tracking, and visualizing the MQL → SQL → Opportunity journey.



\*   \*\*Pendo\*\*: Provides a clear definition and method for tracking web analytics, including \*\*visitors, sessions, and conversion rates\*\* across web apps.

\*   \*\*LeadSources.io\*\*: Tracks the \*\*full path a lead takes across multiple sessions\*\* before submitting a form, providing crucial attribution data that can be sent directly into a CRM.

\*   \*\*Dataflo\*\*: This platform specializes in integrating with HubSpot to visualize key \*\*funnel metrics like MQL to SQL conversion rate\*\* in a single dashboard.

\*   \*\*Bizminer\*\*: A comprehensive database that provides \*\*industry benchmarks and key performance indicators\*\* for thousands of industries, which can be used to benchmark your clients' performance.

\*   \*\*Salesloft\*\*: Publishes the \*\*"Revenue Team Benchmark Report,"\*\* which establishes standards for sales cycle activities across different geographies, job titles, and industries.



\#### 4. Social Media Monitoring (No API)



This directly addresses your request for a way to track social media activity without using official APIs.



\*   \*\*EmbedSocial\*\*: A social listening platform that \*\*automatically detects and collects posts\*\* mentioning a brand across social media platforms without requiring manual tracking.

\*   \*\*Pendulum\*\*: Employs proprietary solutions to uncover brand mentions not just in metadata but also \*\*within the actual transcripts and visual content\*\* of posts, going beyond what traditional API-based tools can do.

\*   \*\*ForumScout\*\*: A free social listening tool that scans platforms like Reddit, Twitter, and LinkedIn to \*\*track brand mentions, competitor activity, and industry conversations\*\*.



\#### 5. Certification Generator \& Social Sharing



This is for the feature that generates a personalized certificate for a user and allows them to share it on social media.



\*   \*\*Virtualbadge.io\*\*: Optimized for social media sharing, this platform allows recipients to \*\*share certificates on their LinkedIn profile or other social feeds\*\* with a couple of clicks, turning them into brand ambassadors.

\*   \*\*Certifier\*\*: A comprehensive certificate maker that allows you to \*\*track credential engagement, including social media shares and referrals\*\*.

\*   \*\*Sertifier (for Tutor LMS)\*\*: Enables students to \*\*share certificates and badges on social platforms\*\* with one click, with a strong emphasis on white-labeling to showcase your brand.



\### 🗺️ Category 3: Broader Ecosystem (Platforms \& Open Source)



This category looks at the underlying platforms and open-source projects that could accelerate development.



\#### No-Code / Low-Code Builders



Given your mention of \*\*Lovable and Supabase\*\*, this is the most direct path to building a custom solution.



\*   \*\*Lovable \& Supabase Combo\*\*: This is a proven stack for building a \*\*SaaS-style dashboard\*\* with secure login and client-specific data environments. You can create a central admin panel to manage all clients and give each client a private dashboard. \*\*Row Level Security (RLS) in Supabase\*\* is the key to ensuring "Client A never sees Client B's data". This approach is explicitly offered as a service on freelance platforms, confirming its viability.



\#### Open Source Projects



\*   \*\*AgencyOS\*\*: An open-source "operating system" for digital agencies built with \*\*Nuxt and Directus\*\*. It's designed to be "100% hackable" and provides a strong foundation for a custom agency management solution.



\### 🧭 Strategic 360-Degree Option Set



Here is a strategic breakdown of the three main paths you can take, as requested:



\*\*Option 1: Build a Custom Solution\*\*

\*   \*\*Description\*\*: Develop your own platform from scratch or using a builder like \*\*Lovable + Supabase\*\*. This gives you 100% control over features, data, and user experience.

\*   \*\*Pros\*\*:

&#x20;   \*   \*\*Full Customization\*\*: Every feature will work exactly as you envision.

&#x20;   \*   \*\*Complete Ownership\*\*: You own the code, the data, and the platform.

&#x20;   \*   \*\*Potential for a New SaaS\*\*: You could eventually turn this into a standalone product for other RevOps consultants.

\*   \*\*Cons\*\*:

&#x20;   \*   \*\*Significant Time Investment\*\*: This will take the longest to plan, build, and test.

&#x20;   \*   \*\*High Upfront Effort\*\*: You'll need to manage development, security, and infrastructure (even with Supabase).



\*\*Option 2: Integrate Existing Best-of-Breed Tools\*\*

\*   \*\*Description\*\*: Use a central hub (like \*\*Noloco\*\*) and integrate it with other specialized tools for LMS (\*\*LearnWorlds\*\*), analytics (\*\*AgencyAnalytics\*\*), and certifications (\*\*Virtualbadge.io\*\*).

\*   \*\*Pros\*\*:

&#x20;   \*   \*\*Fastest to Market\*\*: You can have a professional-looking system running quickly.

&#x20;   \*   \*\*Leverage Expertise\*\*: You benefit from the continuous innovation of established platforms.

&#x20;   \*   \*\*Lower Technical Risk\*\*: You're not reinventing the wheel for complex features like LMS or analytics.

\*   \*\*Cons\*\*:

&#x20;   \*   \*\*Higher Monthly Costs\*\*: You'll be paying for multiple software subscriptions.

&#x20;   \*   \*\*Potential for Disjointed Experience\*\*: Clients might have to navigate between different interfaces or subdomains.



\*\*Option 3: Hybrid Approach (MVP + Platform)\*\*

\*   \*\*Description\*\*: Start by building a \*\*Minimum Viable Product (MVP)\*\* using \*\*Lovable + Supabase\*\* that focuses on your \*core differentiators\*—the client portal with multi-tier permissions and the HubSpot audit snapshots. For complex but non-core features (like the full LMS), use a \*\*white-label embedded solution\*\* (like \*\*WorkRamp's Embedded Learning Cloud\*\*) that integrates seamlessly into your MVP.

\*   \*\*Pros\*\*:

&#x20;   \*   \*\*Balanced Approach\*\*: Get to market faster with a custom, branded core experience.

&#x20;   \*   \*\*Focus on Your "Secret Sauce"\*\*: Your unique value isn't in building an LMS from scratch; it's in the overall consulting workflow.

&#x20;   \*   \*\*Scalable\*\*: You can gradually replace the integrated tools with your own custom-built modules over time.

\*   \*\*Cons\*\*:

&#x20;   \*   \*\*Requires Careful Scoping\*\*: You need to clearly define the boundaries of your MVP.

&#x20;   \*   \*\*Integration Management\*\*: You'll still need to manage the connection between your core app and the embedded third-party tools.



Take your time to review this information. The options above provide a spectrum of paths forward, from building a fully custom solution to integrating a suite of powerful existing tools. Let me know when you're ready to discuss the next steps.

\# 🚀 Ops Solutions SaaS Platform — Implementation Plan

\### \*RevOps Operating System for HubSpot Consultants \& Their Clients\*



\*\*Prepared for:\*\* Mostafa Ali | \*\*Company:\*\* Ops Solutions | \*\*Stack:\*\* Lovable + Supabase + HubSpot API + Gemini

\## 📐 1. Technical Architecture Overview



```

┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐

│                    FRONTEND (Lovable)                │

│  • React/Next.js PWA with responsive design          │

│  • White-label theming engine (logo/colors per org) │

│  • Role-based UI rendering (SuperAdmin→Employee)     │

│  • Sequential course player + certificate generator  │

└─────────────┬───────────────────────────────────────┘

&#x20;             │ HTTPS / WebSocket

┌─────────────▼───────────────────────────────────────┐

│                 BACKEND (Supabase)                   │

│  • PostgreSQL database with Row Level Security (RLS)│

│  • Auth: Supabase Auth + OAuth (HubSpot, Google)    │

│  • Storage: Supabase Storage for certs/media/docs   │

│  • Edge Functions: Webhooks, scrapers, AI triggers  │

└─────┬──────────────┬──────────────┬────────────────┘

&#x20;     │              │              │

┌─────▼────┐ ┌──────▼─────┐ ┌─────▼────────┐

│HubSpot API│ │Gemini API  │ │Scraper Service│

│• Tokens  │ │• Cert gen  │ │• Social posts│

│• Objects │ │• Content   │ │• No Meta API │

│• Webhooks│ │• Templates │ │• Puppeteer   │

└──────────┘ └────────────┘ └──────────────┘

```



\---



\## 👥 2. User Role Matrix \& Permission Logic



| Role | Scope | Permissions | UI Access |

|------|-------|-------------|-----------|

| \*\*Super Admin\*\* (Mostafa) | Global | ✅ Create/Edit/Delete companies, users, courses, templates<br>✅ View all analytics, logs, tokens<br>✅ Impersonate any user<br>✅ Manage billing/plans | Full admin panel + all customer views |

| \*\*Ops Employee\*\* (Your team) | Assigned companies | ✅ View/edit assigned customer data<br>✅ Submit updates, comments, audits<br>✅ Upload training materials<br>❌ Cannot delete companies or see other employees' assignments | Dashboard filtered to assigned companies |

| \*\*Customer Admin\*\* | Single company | ✅ View all progress, analytics, training<br>✅ Manage their employees (invite, assign roles)<br>✅ Comment on updates<br>❌ Cannot edit HubSpot config or see other customers | Branded client portal (white-label) |

| \*\*Customer Manager\*\* | Single company, assigned teams | ✅ View assigned employees' progress<br>✅ View analytics for their team<br>✅ Comment on updates<br>❌ Cannot invite users or change company settings | Filtered portal view |

| \*\*Customer Employee\*\* | Single company, assigned content | ✅ Complete assigned courses<br>✅ View personal progress \& certificates<br>✅ View updates shared with them<br>❌ Cannot see analytics or other users | Minimal training + update view |



\### 🔐 Permission Logic (Supabase RLS Pattern)

```sql

\-- Example: updates table RLS policy

CREATE POLICY "Ops employees see assigned companies"

ON updates FOR SELECT

USING (

&#x20; company\_id IN (

&#x20;   SELECT company\_id FROM employee\_assignments 

&#x20;   WHERE employee\_id = auth.uid()

&#x20; )

);



CREATE POLICY "Customer Admins see their company"

ON updates FOR SELECT

USING (

&#x20; company\_id = (

&#x20;   SELECT company\_id FROM customer\_users 

&#x20;   WHERE user\_id = auth.uid() AND role = 'admin'

&#x20; )

);

```



\---



\## 🗄️ 3. Core Database Schema (Supabase)



\### 🏢 Companies \& Users

```sql

companies (

&#x20; id UUID PK,

&#x20; name TEXT,

&#x20; website\_url TEXT,

&#x20; logo\_url TEXT, -- auto-fetched via scraper

&#x20; industry TEXT,

&#x20; employee\_count INT,

&#x20; locations JSONB,

&#x20; hubspot\_portal\_id TEXT,

&#x20; hubspot\_access\_token TEXT, -- encrypted

&#x20; hubspot\_refresh\_token TEXT, -- encrypted

&#x20; plan\_tier TEXT, -- 'basic', 'pro', 'enterprise'

&#x20; branding\_config JSONB, -- {primary\_color, secondary\_color, accent\_color}

&#x20; created\_at TIMESTAMPTZ

)



users (

&#x20; id UUID PK, -- Supabase auth ID

&#x20; email TEXT UNIQUE,

&#x20; full\_name TEXT,

&#x20; role TEXT CHECK (role IN ('super\_admin', 'ops\_employee', 'customer\_admin', 'customer\_manager', 'customer\_employee')),

&#x20; company\_id UUID FK REFERENCES companies(id),

&#x20; assigned\_companies UUID\[] REFERENCES companies(id), -- for ops employees

&#x20; manager\_id UUID REFERENCES users(id), -- for customer employees

&#x20; created\_at TIMESTAMPTZ

)

```



\### 📊 Analytics \& Funnel Tracking

```sql

funnel\_stages (

&#x20; id UUID PK,

&#x20; company\_id UUID FK,

&#x20; stage\_name TEXT CHECK (stage\_name IN ('view', 'subscribe', 'lead', 'mql', 'sql', 'opportunity', 'customer')),

&#x20; count INT,

&#x20; conversion\_rate DECIMAL,

&#x20; benchmark\_industry TEXT,

&#x20; benchmark\_region TEXT,

&#x20; benchmark\_value DECIMAL,

&#x20; last\_updated TIMESTAMPTZ

)



form\_submissions (

&#x20; id UUID PK,

&#x20; company\_id UUID FK,

&#x20; form\_name TEXT,

&#x20; form\_url TEXT,

&#x20; submission\_count INT,

&#x20; leads\_with\_owner INT,

&#x20; leads\_without\_owner INT,

&#x20; source TEXT, -- 'online', 'offline', 'import'

&#x20; created\_at TIMESTAMPTZ

)



social\_metrics (

&#x20; id UUID PK,

&#x20; company\_id UUID FK,

&#x20; platform TEXT, -- 'linkedin', 'twitter', 'facebook'

&#x20; profile\_url TEXT,

&#x20; posts\_count INT,

&#x20; impressions\_estimate INT, -- via scraper

&#x20; last\_scraped TIMESTAMPTZ

)

```

```sql
&#x20; description TEXT,

&#x20; plan\_access TEXT\[] CHECK (plan\_access <@ ARRAY\['basic', 'pro', 'enterprise']),

&#x20; is\_sequential BOOLEAN DEFAULT true,

&#x20; created\_at TIMESTAMPTZ

)



modules (

&#x20; id UUID PK,

&#x20; course\_id UUID FK,

&#x20; title TEXT,

&#x20; order\_index INT,

&#x20; content\_type TEXT CHECK (content\_type IN ('doc', 'video', 'quiz')),

&#x20; content\_url TEXT, -- Supabase Storage or external link

&#x20; is\_locked\_until\_prev\_complete BOOLEAN DEFAULT true,

&#x20; duration\_minutes INT

)



enrollments (

&#x20; user\_id UUID FK,

&#x20; course\_id UUID FK,

&#x20; progress\_percent DECIMAL,

&#x20; completed\_at TIMESTAMPTZ,

&#x20; UNIQUE(user\_id, course\_id)

)



certificate\_templates (

&#x20; company\_id UUID FK,

&#x20; template\_name TEXT,

&#x20; gemini\_prompt\_template TEXT, -- for AI generation

&#x20; fields\_config JSONB -- {first\_name, last\_name, course\_name, date}

)



certificates (

&#x20; generated\_at TIMESTAMPTZ,

&#x20; shared\_on\_social BOOLEAN DEFAULT false

)

```

\---



\## 🔌 4. Integration Strategy



\### 🔄 HubSpot Integration

| Feature | Implementation |

|---------|---------------|

| \*\*OAuth Flow\*\* | Supabase Edge Function handles `/oauth/authorize` → store tokens encrypted (pgcrypto) |

| \*\*Token Refresh\*\* | Cron job (Supabase pg\_cron) refreshes tokens 1 hour before expiry |

| \*\*Data Sync\*\* | Webhooks from HubSpot → Supabase Edge Function → upsert to `funnel\_stages`, `form\_submissions` |

| \*\*Object Access\*\* | Use HubSpot API scopes: `crm.objects.contacts.read`, `automation`, `reports` |

| \*\*Security\*\* | Tokens encrypted at rest; never exposed to frontend; all calls via Edge Functions |



\### 🕷️ Social Scraper Service (No Meta API)

```python

\# Pseudo-code for Edge Function (Python/Deno)

async def scrape\_social\_metrics(company\_url: str, platform: str):

&#x20;   if platform == 'linkedin':

&#x20;       # Use Puppeteer/Playwright to fetch public company page

&#x20;       # Extract: follower count, recent posts count, engagement estimates

&#x20;       # Store in social\_metrics table

&#x20;   elif platform == 'twitter':

&#x20;       # Use nitter.net scraper (no API key needed)

&#x20;   # Rate limiting: max 1 scrape per company per 24h

&#x20;   # Fallback: if scraper fails, use cached data + flag as "estimated"

```



\### 🤖 Gemini Certificate Generation

```python

\# Edge Function trigger: when enrollment.completed\_at is set

async def generate\_certificate(enrollment\_id: str):

&#x20;   # Fetch template + user data

&#x20;   prompt = template.gemini\_prompt\_template.format(

&#x20;       first\_name=user.full\_name.split()\[0],

&#x20;       last\_name=user.full\_name.split()\[-1],

&#x20;       course\_name=course.title,

&#x20;       date=datetime.now().strftime("%B %d, %Y")

&#x20;   )

&#x20;   # Call Gemini API to generate image with text overlay

&#x20;   image\_url = await gemini.generate\_image(prompt, template.background\_image\_url)

&#x20;   # Upload to Supabase Storage, update certificates table

&#x20;   # Generate shareable link (signed URL with expiry)

&#x20;   # Send notification to manager/admin/ops

```

\## 🧩 5. Feature Modules Breakdown



\### 🏠 Module 1: Company Onboarding \& Branding

\- \[ ] Auto-fetch logo via scraper (Clearbit API fallback)

\- \[ ] Branding config: primary/secondary/accent colors → applied to customer portal CSS variables

\- \[ ] HubSpot token setup wizard (OAuth flow + test connection)



\### 📈 Module 2: Analytics Dashboard

\- \[ ] Funnel visualization: View → Subscribe → Lead → MQL → SQL → Opportunity → Customer

\- \[ ] Benchmark overlay: fetch industry/region benchmarks from Bizminer API or cached dataset

\- \[ ] Form attribution table: filter by form name, source, owner assignment

\- \[ ] "Recommendations" panel: if conversion rate < benchmark → show actionable tips



\### 🎯 Module 3: Social \& Lead Monitoring

\- \[ ] Social scraper scheduler (cron job per company)

\- \[ ] Lead source tracker: online forms vs offline imports vs manual entry

\- \[ ] "Unassigned leads" alert for Customer Admins



\### 🎓 Module 4: Academy Engine

\- \[ ] Sequential module player: disable next module until current is marked complete

\- \[ ] Content types: embedded PDF viewer, video player (Supabase Storage), quiz component

\- \[ ] Certificate generator: Gemini API + template system + social share buttons (LinkedIn, Twitter)



\### 🔍 Module 5: HubSpot Audit \& Enhancements

\- \[ ] Before/after image uploader with side-by-side comparison viewer

\- \[ ] Audit checklist template (properties, workflows, pipelines, reports)

\- \[ ] "Enhancement log" timeline visible to customer roles per permission config



\### 💬 Module 6: Updates \& Collaboration

\- \[ ] Rich text editor for updates (Tiptap)

\- \[ ] Role/user selector for visibility (multi-select dropdown with search)

\- \[ ] Comment threading with @mentions + email notifications

\- \[ ] Internal vs customer-visible comment toggle

\---



\## 🔐 7. Security \& Compliance



| Area | Implementation |

|------|---------------|

| \*\*Data Isolation\*\* | Supabase RLS on every table; `company\_id` in every query |

| \*\*Token Security\*\* | HubSpot tokens encrypted with `pgcrypto`; decrypted only in Edge Functions |

| \*\*Auth\*\* | Supabase Auth + JWT; optional SSO for enterprise customers |

| \*\*File Storage\*\* | Supabase Storage with signed URLs; virus scan on upload (ClamAV Edge Function) |

| \*\*Audit Logs\*\* | Log all admin actions (token changes, user invites) to `audit\_logs` table |

| \*\*GDPR/CCPA\*\* | Data export/delete endpoints per user; cookie consent banner |



\---



\## 📡 8. API Endpoints Structure (Edge Functions)



```

POST /api/v1/hubspot/connect          # Start OAuth flow

POST /api/v1/hubspot/webhook          # Handle HubSpot webhooks

GET  /api/v1/analytics/funnel/:companyId

POST /api/v1/social/scrape/:companyId # Trigger manual scrape

POST /api/v1/certificates/generate/:enrollmentId

POST /api/v1/notifications/completion # Send completion alerts

GET  /api/v1/companies/:id/branding   # Fetch white-label config

```

\## 🚀 10. Deployment \& DevOps



| Step | Tool | Command/Config |

|------|------|---------------|

| \*\*1. Supabase Setup\*\* | Supabase CLI | `supabase init` → `supabase link` → `supabase db push` |

| \*\*2. Edge Functions\*\* | Supabase Functions | `supabase functions new <name>` → deploy via CLI |

| \*\*3. Lovable Project\*\* | Lovable.dev | Import Figma → connect to Supabase project |

| \*\*4. Environment Vars\*\* | Supabase Dashboard | `HUBSPOT\_CLIENT\_ID`, `GEMINI\_API\_KEY`, `SCRAPER\_PROXY` |

| \*\*5. CI/CD\*\* | GitHub Actions | Auto-deploy Edge Functions on push to `main` |

| \*\*6. Monitoring\*\* | Supabase Logs + Sentry | Track errors, slow queries, auth failures |

\### USER

we can use it as intergation like arrow with hbuspot or toher CRM to let the agents who use hubspot guide them like arrow ?







\### ASSISTANT

Yes, Mostafa — absolutely. Integrating your platform \*\*inside HubSpot (like Arrows.to)\*\* is not only possible, it's a high-impact differentiator for your RevOps consulting model.



Below is a clear breakdown of \*\*how to embed Ops Solutions guidance directly into HubSpot\*\*, ranked by effort vs. impact, with technical options you can implement in Lovable + Supabase.



\---



\## 🎯 Goal: "Arrows-Style" In-CRM Guidance for Your Clients



> \*"When a sales agent opens a Contact/Deal in HubSpot, they see a contextual sidebar from Ops Solutions showing:  

> • Their assigned training progress  

> • Audit recommendations for this record  

> • Next operational step (e.g., 'Update lifecycle stage')  

> • Quick link to complete a micro-course"\*



\---



\## 🔧 Integration Options (Ranked)



\### ✅ Option 1: HubSpot UI Extensions (Recommended — Native \& Scalable)

\*\*What it is\*\*: Official HubSpot framework to embed custom React components directly into CRM record pages (Contact, Company, Deal, Ticket).



| Feature | Implementation |

|---------|---------------|

| \*\*Where it appears\*\* | Right sidebar of any CRM object page |

| \*\*Tech stack\*\* | React + HubSpot UI Extensions SDK + Supabase API |

| \*\*Auth\*\* | OAuth 2.0 via HubSpot private app (tokens stored encrypted in Supabase) |

| \*\*Data flow\*\* | Extension fetches user's progress/tasks from your Supabase backend using `hubspot\_user\_id` |

| \*\*Permissions\*\* | Respects HubSpot user roles + your platform's RLS policies |



\*\*Example UI in HubSpot\*\*:

```

\[Ops Solutions Panel]

✓ Welcome, Ahmed!  

🎓 Training: "Lead Qualification Basics" — 2/3 modules complete  

💡 Recommendation: Add "Company Size" property to this contact  

➕ Next Step: Update lifecycle stage → "Marketing Qualified"  

\[Complete Micro-Task] \[View Full Academy]

```



\*\*Effort\*\*: Medium (3-5 days for MVP extension)  

\*\*Impact\*\*: High — feels native, zero context-switching for users



🔗 Docs: \[HubSpot UI Extensions Guide](https://developers.hubspot.com/docs/ui-extensions)



\---



\### ✅ Option 2: HubSpot Tasks + Webhooks Sync (Fastest MVP)

\*\*What it is\*\*: Push guided steps from your platform → HubSpot Tasks object. When user completes task in HubSpot, webhook updates your system.



| Feature | Implementation |

|---------|---------------|

| \*\*Where it appears\*\* | HubSpot Tasks tab (native) |

| \*\*Tech stack\*\* | Supabase Edge Functions + HubSpot Tasks API + Webhooks |

| \*\*Auth\*\* | Same OAuth flow; no UI injection needed |

| \*\*Data flow\*\* | Your platform creates Task → HubSpot API → assigned to user → completion webhook → update Supabase |

| \*\*Permissions\*\* | Uses HubSpot's native task assignment + visibility |



\*\*Example Workflow\*\*:

1\. Ops employee flags: "Contact missing industry property"  

2\. Your system creates HubSpot Task: "Add industry to \[Contact Name]"  

3\. Agent sees task in their HubSpot inbox  

4\. Agent completes task → webhook triggers → your platform marks step complete + unlocks next training module



\*\*Effort\*\*: Low (1-2 days)  

\*\*Impact\*\*: Medium — leverages native UX, but less "wow" than embedded sidebar



🔗 Docs: \[HubSpot Tasks API](https://developers.hubspot.com/docs/api/crm/tasks)



\---



\### ⚙️ Option 3: Chrome Extension Companion (CRM-Agnostic)

\*\*What it is\*\*: Browser extension that detects HubSpot (or Salesforce/Zoho) URLs and overlays your guidance UI.



| Feature | Implementation |

|---------|---------------|

| \*\*Where it appears\*\* | Floating widget or sidebar overlay on CRM pages |

| \*\*Tech stack\*\* | React + Chrome Extensions Manifest V3 + Supabase API |

| \*\*Auth\*\* | Supabase session token stored in extension storage |

| \*\*Data flow\*\* | Extension reads URL → extracts record ID → fetches guidance from your backend |

| \*\*Permissions\*\* | Works across any CRM; no vendor approval needed |



\*\*Pros\*\*:  

\- Works for clients on Salesforce, Zoho, etc.  

\- No HubSpot app review process  

\- Can inject contextual tooltips/walkthroughs  



\*\*Cons\*\*:  

\- Requires user to install extension  

\- Slightly less "polished" than native extensions  



\*\*Effort\*\*: Medium-High (4-7 days)  

\*\*Impact\*\*: High for multi-CRM consultancies



\---



\### 🚫 Option 4: iFrame Embed via Custom Code (Not Recommended for Production)

\*\*What it is\*\*: Add your platform as an `<iframe>` in HubSpot via custom code module or page injection.



| Issue | Why Avoid |

|-------|-----------|

| \*\*Security\*\* | iFrames can be blocked by CSP policies; token leakage risk |

| \*\*UX\*\* | Clunky scrolling, mobile-unfriendly, no native styling |

| \*\*Maintenance\*\* | Breaks if HubSpot changes DOM structure |

| \*\*Approval\*\* | Won't pass HubSpot App Marketplace review |



→ Only use for internal prototyping, not client-facing.



\---



\## 🔄 Bidirectional Sync Architecture (Supabase + HubSpot)



```mermaid

graph LR

&#x20;   A\[Ops Solutions Platform] <--> B\[Supabase Edge Functions]

&#x20;   B <--> C\[HubSpot API]

&#x20;   C <--> D\[HubSpot UI: Tasks/Extensions]

&#x20;   

&#x20;   E\[User completes task in HubSpot] --> F\[Webhook to Edge Function]

&#x20;   F --> G\[Update Supabase: enrollment progress]

&#x20;   G --> H\[Trigger: unlock next module / notify manager]

&#x20;   

&#x20;   I\[Ops employee adds recommendation] --> J\[Create HubSpot Task via API]

&#x20;   J --> K\[Task appears in agent's HubSpot inbox]

```



\### 🔐 Critical Security Notes:

1\. \*\*Never expose Supabase keys to frontend\*\* — all HubSpot API calls go through Edge Functions

2\. \*\*Encrypt HubSpot tokens\*\* using `pgcrypto` in Supabase

3\. \*\*Validate record ownership\*\* — ensure user can only see guidance for records they own in HubSpot

4\. \*\*Rate limit API calls\*\* — HubSpot has strict limits (100 req/10s per app)



\---



\## 🧩 Sample Data Model Additions (Supabase)



```sql

\-- Link HubSpot users to your platform users

hubspot\_user\_mappings (

&#x20; id UUID PK,

&#x20; platform\_user\_id UUID FK REFERENCES users(id),

&#x20; hubspot\_user\_id TEXT, -- HubSpot's internal user ID

&#x20; hubspot\_portal\_id TEXT,

&#x20; oauth\_access\_token TEXT, -- encrypted

&#x20; oauth\_refresh\_token TEXT, -- encrypted

&#x20; token\_expires\_at TIMESTAMPTZ,

&#x20; UNIQUE(hubspot\_user\_id, hubspot\_portal\_id)

)



\-- Guidance steps that can be pushed to HubSpot

guidance\_steps (

&#x20; id UUID PK,

&#x20; company\_id UUID FK,

&#x20; title TEXT,

&#x20; description TEXT,

&#x20; hubspot\_object\_type TEXT CHECK (type IN ('contact', 'company', 'deal', 'ticket')),

&#x20; trigger\_condition JSONB, -- e.g., {property: "lifecyclestage", equals: "lead"}

&#x20; action\_type TEXT CHECK (action IN ('task', 'notification', 'training\_unlock')),

&#x20; training\_module\_id UUID FK REFERENCES modules(id),

&#x20; created\_at TIMESTAMPTZ

)



\-- Track completion of in-CRM guidance

guidance\_completions (

&#x20; id UUID PK,

&#x20; step\_id UUID FK,

&#x20; hubspot\_user\_id TEXT,

&#x20; hubspot\_record\_id TEXT, -- the contact/deal ID where action was taken

&#x20; completed\_at TIMESTAMPTZ,

&#x20; source TEXT CHECK (source IN ('hubspot\_task', 'ui\_extension', 'chrome\_extension'))

)

```

|-------|------|----------|

| \*\*Phase 1 (MVP)\*\* | Tasks + Webhooks sync | Week 1-2 |

\## 💡 Pro Tips for Mostafa



1\. \*\*Start with Tasks sync\*\* — delivers immediate value with minimal code, validates the workflow with clients.

2\. \*\*Use your existing AI Diagnose App\*\* as the "brain" — feed HubSpot record data to it, return recommendations to display in-extension.

3\. \*\*White-label the extension\*\* — use the company's branding config (colors/logo) so it feels like their internal tool.

4\. \*\*Add Arabic support early\*\* — no major competitor offers in-CRM guidance in Arabic; huge differentiator for your MENA clients.

5\. \*\*Track "guidance adoption" as a KPI\*\* — measure how many recommended steps users complete → proves ROI to clients.

4\. DATABASE SCHEMA (Supabase / PostgreSQL)

4.1 companies

CREATE TABLE companies (

&#x20; id              UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen\_random\_uuid(),

&#x20; name            TEXT NOT NULL,

&#x20; website         TEXT,

&#x20; domain          TEXT,

&#x20; industry        TEXT,

&#x20; employee\_count  TEXT,         -- e.g. '50-200'

&#x20; country         TEXT,

&#x20; region          TEXT,

&#x20; logo\_url        TEXT,         -- auto-fetched via Clearbit/Logo.dev

&#x20; plan            TEXT DEFAULT 'basic', -- basic | pro | enterprise

&#x20; hubspot\_token   TEXT,         -- encrypted private app token

&#x20; status          TEXT DEFAULT 'active',

&#x20; created\_by      UUID REFERENCES auth.users(id),

&#x20; created\_at      TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT now(),

&#x20; updated\_at      TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT now()

);



4.2 profiles (extends auth.users)

CREATE TABLE profiles (

&#x20; id              UUID PRIMARY KEY REFERENCES auth.users(id),

&#x20; full\_name       TEXT,

&#x20; email           TEXT,

&#x20; avatar\_url      TEXT,

&#x20; role            TEXT NOT NULL,  -- superadmin | ops\_employee | client\_admin | client\_manager | client\_employee

&#x20; company\_id      UUID REFERENCES companies(id),

&#x20; manager\_id      UUID REFERENCES profiles(id), -- for client\_employee → manager link

&#x20; is\_active       BOOLEAN DEFAULT true,

&#x20; created\_at      TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT now()

);



4.3 updates (change log / announcements)

CREATE TABLE updates (

&#x20; id              UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen\_random\_uuid(),

&#x20; company\_id      UUID REFERENCES companies(id),

&#x20; title           TEXT NOT NULL,

&#x20; content         TEXT,

&#x20; category        TEXT,          -- hubspot | process | training | general

&#x20; visibility      TEXT\[],        -- \['client\_admin','client\_manager'] or \['all']

&#x20; visible\_to\_users UUID\[],       -- specific user IDs if targeted

&#x20; before\_image\_url TEXT,

&#x20; after\_image\_url  TEXT,

&#x20; created\_by      UUID REFERENCES profiles(id),

&#x20; created\_at      TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT now()

);



4.4 update\_comments

CREATE TABLE update\_comments (

&#x20; id              UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen\_random\_uuid(),

&#x20; update\_id       UUID REFERENCES updates(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,

&#x20; user\_id         UUID REFERENCES profiles(id),

&#x20; content         TEXT NOT NULL,

&#x20; created\_at      TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT now()

);



4.5 analytics\_snapshots

CREATE TABLE analytics\_snapshots (

&#x20; id              UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen\_random\_uuid(),

&#x20; company\_id      UUID REFERENCES companies(id),

&#x20; snapshot\_date   DATE DEFAULT CURRENT\_DATE,

&#x20; stage           TEXT,          -- visitor | subscriber | lead | mql | sql | opportunity | customer

&#x20; metric\_key      TEXT,          -- sessions, conversions, form\_submissions, etc.

&#x20; metric\_value    NUMERIC,

&#x20; source          TEXT,          -- hubspot | manual | scraped

&#x20; created\_at      TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT now()

);



4.6 forms\_tracking

CREATE TABLE forms\_tracking (

&#x20; id              UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen\_random\_uuid(),

&#x20; company\_id      UUID REFERENCES companies(id),

&#x20; form\_name       TEXT,

&#x20; form\_type       TEXT,          -- lead\_1 | lead\_2 | subscriber\_1 | etc.

&#x20; total\_submissions INT DEFAULT 0,

&#x20; with\_owner      INT DEFAULT 0,

&#x20; without\_owner   INT DEFAULT 0,

&#x20; offline\_count   INT DEFAULT 0,

&#x20; hubspot\_form\_id TEXT,

&#x20; last\_synced     TIMESTAMPTZ,

&#x20; created\_at      TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT now()

);



4.7 social\_snapshots

CREATE TABLE social\_snapshots (

&#x20; id              UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen\_random\_uuid(),

&#x20; company\_id      UUID REFERENCES companies(id),

&#x20; platform        TEXT,          -- linkedin | instagram | twitter | facebook

&#x20; followers       INT,

&#x20; posts\_count     INT,

&#x20; avg\_engagement  NUMERIC,

&#x20; snapshot\_date   DATE DEFAULT CURRENT\_DATE,

&#x20; source\_url      TEXT,

&#x20; created\_at      TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT now()

);



4.8 courses

CREATE TABLE courses (

&#x20; id              UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen\_random\_uuid(),

&#x20; title           TEXT NOT NULL,

&#x20; description     TEXT,

&#x20; thumbnail\_url   TEXT,

&#x20; order\_index     INT DEFAULT 0,

&#x20; plan\_required   TEXT DEFAULT 'basic',  -- basic | pro | enterprise

&#x20; content\_type    TEXT DEFAULT 'both',   -- doc | video | both

&#x20; is\_published    BOOLEAN DEFAULT false,

&#x20; created\_by      UUID REFERENCES profiles(id),

&#x20; created\_at      TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT now()

);



4.9 course\_modules

CREATE TABLE course\_modules (

&#x20; id              UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen\_random\_uuid(),

&#x20; course\_id       UUID REFERENCES courses(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,

&#x20; title           TEXT NOT NULL,

&#x20; order\_index     INT DEFAULT 0,

&#x20; doc\_url         TEXT,          -- Lovable academy doc URL

&#x20; video\_url       TEXT,

&#x20; duration\_mins   INT,

&#x20; is\_locked       BOOLEAN DEFAULT true  -- unlocked when previous is complete

);



4.10 course\_progress

CREATE TABLE course\_progress (

&#x20; id              UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen\_random\_uuid(),

&#x20; user\_id         UUID REFERENCES profiles(id),

&#x20; course\_id       UUID REFERENCES courses(id),

&#x20; module\_id       UUID REFERENCES course\_modules(id),

&#x20; company\_id      UUID REFERENCES companies(id),

&#x20; completed       BOOLEAN DEFAULT false,

&#x20; completed\_at    TIMESTAMPTZ,

&#x20; UNIQUE(user\_id, module\_id)

);



4.11 certificates

CREATE TABLE certificates (

&#x20; id              UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen\_random\_uuid(),

&#x20; user\_id         UUID REFERENCES profiles(id),

&#x20; company\_id      UUID REFERENCES companies(id),

&#x20; course\_id       UUID REFERENCES courses(id),

&#x20; issued\_at       TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT now(),

&#x20; certificate\_url TEXT,          -- generated image URL stored in Supabase Storage

&#x20; share\_token     TEXT UNIQUE DEFAULT gen\_random\_uuid()::TEXT

);



4.12 enhancements (before/after HubSpot work)

CREATE TABLE enhancements (

&#x20; id              UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen\_random\_uuid(),

&#x20; company\_id      UUID REFERENCES companies(id),

&#x20; area            TEXT,          -- workflows | pipelines | properties | reports | sequences | etc.

&#x20; title           TEXT NOT NULL,

&#x20; description     TEXT,

&#x20; before\_image\_url TEXT,

&#x20; after\_image\_url  TEXT,

&#x20; created\_by      UUID REFERENCES profiles(id),

&#x20; created\_at      TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT now()

);



4.13 industry\_benchmarks

CREATE TABLE industry\_benchmarks (

&#x20; id              UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen\_random\_uuid(),

&#x20; industry        TEXT,

&#x20; region          TEXT,

&#x20; stage           TEXT,

&#x20; metric\_key      TEXT,

&#x20; benchmark\_value NUMERIC,

&#x20; source          TEXT,

&#x20; updated\_at      TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT now()

);



Row Level Security — Key Rules

\-- Companies: only visible to members assigned to that company

ALTER TABLE companies ENABLE ROW LEVEL SECURITY;

CREATE POLICY company\_isolation ON companies

&#x20; USING (

&#x20;   id IN (SELECT company\_id FROM profiles WHERE id = auth.uid())

&#x20;   OR EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM profiles WHERE id = auth.uid() AND role IN ('superadmin','ops\_employee'))

&#x20; );



\-- Apply similar RLS to all tables with company\_id

\-- Profiles: users can only see teammates in their own company

\-- Updates: filtered by visibility array or visible\_to\_users

\-- Courses/Progress: filtered by company plan

6\. FEATURE MODULES — DETAILED SPECS



MODULE 1: Auth \& Onboarding

Use Supabase Auth (email/password)

Invite flow: OPS sends invite link → user lands on /invite/\[token] → sets password → profile created with pre-assigned role + company\_id

On first login show onboarding modal:

SUPERADMIN: "Add your first company"

CLIENT\_ADMIN: "Welcome to \[Company Name] workspace"

Session middleware in middleware.ts reads role from profile, redirects accordingly



MODULE 2: Company Management (OPS side)

Page: /ops/companies

Grid of company cards showing: logo, name, industry, employee count, plan badge, status

"Add Company" button → drawer form with fields:

Company name, website/domain, industry (dropdown), employee count range, country, region

Plan selector: Basic | Pro | Enterprise

HubSpot Private App Token (encrypted at rest using Supabase Vault)

On domain entry → auto-fetch company logo via https://logo.dev/\[domain] or Clearbit

Each card links to company detail page

Page: /ops/companies/\[id]

Tabs: Overview | Team | Analytics | Updates | Enhancements | Academy

OPS-specific controls: edit token, change plan, manage team, impersonate (view as client)



MODULE 3: Analytics Dashboard (5 Stages)

All data pulls from HubSpot API using the company's stored token + analytics\_snapshots table as cache.

Stage 1 — Visitors

Sessions, unique visitors, bounce rate, top pages

Source: Google Analytics embed OR HubSpot traffic analytics API

Chart: Line chart (last 30/60/90 days)

KPI cards: Total Sessions | Avg Session Duration | Conversion Rate

Stage 2 — Subscribers (Social)

Social media stats per platform: followers, post count, avg engagement

Source: Domain scraper (no Meta API) — scrape public social profiles by domain

Platforms: LinkedIn, Instagram, Twitter/X, Facebook

Display: Platform cards with logo, metric numbers, last updated timestamp

Manual override: OPS or CLIENT\_ADMIN can manually input/update numbers

Stage 3 — Leads (Forms)

Pull all HubSpot forms via API

For each form show: name, total submissions, with owner %, without owner %, offline submissions

Allow OPS to label each form (Lead Form 1, Subscriber Form 2, etc.)

"Add Form" button to manually track additional forms

Source attribution chart: organic | paid | referral | direct | offline

Stage 4 — MQL

Contact lifecycle stage breakdown

MQL count, conversion rate from Lead → MQL

Breakdown by:

Inbound (form submissions)

Offline (manual/import)

Source channel

Contacts with/without owner donut chart

Compare vs industry benchmark (from industry\_benchmarks table)

Stage 5 — Pipeline (SQL → Opportunity → Customer)

Deal stages pipeline view

Conversion rates: MQL→SQL, SQL→Opp, Opp→Customer

Avg conversion time per stage

Revenue metrics: projected vs closed

Benchmark overlay by industry + region

Recommendation engine: if conversion rate < benchmark → show inline tip/sequence suggestion



MODULE 4: Updates \& Change Log

OPS posts updates, clients read and comment.

Create Update (OPS only):

Title, content (rich text), category selector

Visibility: All roles | Specific roles | Specific users (multi-select, like HubSpot dashboard share)

Upload before/after images (optional)

Company selector (which client this is for)

Client View:

Feed of updates filtered by their visibility

Each card: title, date, category badge, content, before/after images if present

Comment box below each update

Unread badge on sidebar



MODULE 5: Enhancements (Before/After HubSpot Work)

OPS side:

Add enhancement: area (Workflows / Pipelines / Properties / Reports / Sequences / Custom), title, description, before image, after image

Tag to company

Client side:

Gallery view of enhancements grouped by area

Before/After image toggle (slide or side-by-side)

Accessible to CLIENT\_ADMIN and CLIENT\_MANAGER



MODULE 6: Academy (Training + Certificates)

Content Management (OPS side)

Create courses with: title, thumbnail, description, plan required, content type (Doc | Video | Both)

Add modules inside each course (ordered, locked by default)

Each module has: doc URL (Lovable academy link), video URL, order index

Publish/unpublish toggle

Learning Experience (Client side)

Course list shows only courses matching company plan

Sequential lock: module N+1 unlocked only after N is marked complete

Doc mode: iframe embed of Lovable academy doc

Video mode: embedded video player

Plan-based gating: Basic → Doc only | Pro/Enterprise → Doc + Video

Certificate Generation

Triggered when all modules in a course are complete

Template stored in Supabase Storage

Inject: user first name, last name, course name, completion date, Mostafa's signature image

Generate as PNG using Canvas API (server-side via Supabase Edge Function)

Store generated certificate in Supabase Storage under /certificates/\[company\_id]/\[user\_id]/\[course\_id].png

Display in user profile + shareable link /share/certificate/\[share\_token]

Download button + "Share on LinkedIn" button

Notifications on Completion

Notify CLIENT\_MANAGER (if assigned)

Notify CLIENT\_ADMIN

Notify SUPERADMIN via Supabase notification or email



MODULE 7: Team Management

OPS side (/ops/employees):

List of OPS team members

Invite new OPS employee

Assign OPS employee to specific companies

Client side (/client/\[companyId]/team):

CLIENT\_ADMIN sees all users in company

CLIENT\_MANAGER sees only assigned employees

Invite new user (within allowed role range)

Resend invite, deactivate user



MODULE 8: Intro Video \& Owner Branding

First login for any client user → modal with Mostafa's intro video (URL from Supabase config)

Video auto-plays, can be dismissed after 10 seconds

Stored as seen\_intro: boolean in profiles

Ops can update the intro video URL from settings panel



7\. HUBSPOT INTEGRATION

Per-Company Token Architecture

// lib/hubspot/client.ts

import { createClient } from '@/lib/supabase/server'



export async function getHubspotClient(companyId: string) {

&#x20; const supabase = createClient()

&#x20; const { data } = await supabase

&#x20;   .from('companies')

&#x20;   .select('hubspot\_token')

&#x20;   .eq('id', companyId)

&#x20;   .single()



&#x20; if (!data?.hubspot\_token) throw new Error('No HubSpot token')



&#x20; return {

&#x20;   baseUrl: 'https://api.hubapi.com',

&#x20;   headers: {

&#x20;     Authorization: `Bearer ${data.hubspot\_token}`,

&#x20;     'Content-Type': 'application/json'

&#x20;   }

&#x20; }

}



Key HubSpot Endpoints Used

Data

Endpoint

Contacts by lifecycle stage

GET /crm/v3/objects/contacts with lifecyclestage filter

Deals by stage

GET /crm/v3/objects/deals

Forms list

GET /marketing/v3/forms

Form submissions

GET /form-integrations/v1/submissions/forms/{formId}

Traffic analytics

GET /analytics/v2/reports/totals/daily

Contact owner

GET /crm/v3/owners





8\. SOCIAL SCRAPER (No Meta API)

// lib/scrapers/socialScraper.ts

// Uses a headless fetch approach for public data



export async function scrapeSocialProfile(platform: string, handle: string) {

&#x20; // Strategy: fetch public embed/oembed endpoints

&#x20; // LinkedIn: use li.scraper or people data labs free tier

&#x20; // Instagram: use public embed endpoint instagram.com/\[handle]/embed

&#x20; // Twitter/X: use nitter.net or syndication.twitter.com embed

&#x20; // Facebook: use graph.facebook.com/\[page]?fields=fan\_count (public pages only)

&#x20; 

&#x20; // Primary: https://api.microlink.io?url=https://instagram.com/\[handle]

&#x20; // Fallback: manual entry by OPS team

}



Note for Claude Code: Use https://api.microlink.io as the primary scraping engine — it supports LinkedIn, Instagram, Twitter, Facebook public pages without needing API keys for basic metadata. Store results in social\_snapshots table. Schedule refresh via Supabase Edge Function cron (daily).



9\. LOGO AUTO-FETCH

// lib/scrapers/logoFetcher.ts

export async function fetchCompanyLogo(domain: string): Promise<string | null> {

&#x20; // Primary: https://img.logo.dev/\[domain]?token=pk\_YOUR\_TOKEN\&size=128

&#x20; // Fallback: https://logo.clearbit.com/\[domain]

&#x20; // Fallback 2: https://www.google.com/s2/favicons?domain=\[domain]\&sz=128

&#x20; // If all fail: return null, show initials avatar

}





10\. CERTIFICATE GENERATOR

// lib/certificates/generateCertificate.ts

// Supabase Edge Function — runs server-side



import { createCanvas, loadImage } from 'canvas'



export async function generateCertificate({

&#x20; firstName, lastName, courseName, completionDate, templateUrl

}) {

&#x20; const canvas = createCanvas(1200, 850)

&#x20; const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d')

&#x20; 

&#x20; // Load template background

&#x20; const template = await loadImage(templateUrl)

&#x20; ctx.drawImage(template, 0, 0, 1200, 850)

&#x20; 

&#x20; // Inject name

&#x20; ctx.font = 'bold 52px Sora'

&#x20; ctx.fillStyle = '#425b76'

&#x20; ctx.textAlign = 'center'

&#x20; ctx.fillText(`${firstName} ${lastName}`, 600, 420)

&#x20; 

&#x20; // Inject course name

&#x20; ctx.font = '28px DM Sans'

&#x20; ctx.fillStyle = '#333333'

&#x20; ctx.fillText(courseName, 600, 490)

&#x20; 

&#x20; // Inject date

&#x20; ctx.font = '22px DM Sans'

&#x20; ctx.fillStyle = '#8a9bb0'

&#x20; ctx.fillText(completionDate, 600, 540)

&#x20; 

&#x20; return canvas.toBuffer('image/png')

}





11\. RECOMMENDATION ENGINE

Simple rule-based engine in lib/utils/benchmarks.ts:

export function getRecommendations(metrics: CompanyMetrics, benchmarks: Benchmark\[]) {

&#x20; const recommendations = \[]

&#x20; 

&#x20; // Example rules

&#x20; if (metrics.leadToMql < benchmarks.leadToMql \* 0.8) {

&#x20;   recommendations.push({

&#x20;     area: 'Lead Scoring',

&#x20;     issue: 'Lead to MQL rate is 20% below industry average',

&#x20;     action: 'Review lead scoring model and qualification criteria',

&#x20;     urgency: 'high'

&#x20;   })

&#x20; }

&#x20; 

&#x20; if (metrics.formsWithoutOwner > 0.3) {

&#x20;   recommendations.push({

&#x20;     area: 'Lead Routing',

&#x20;     issue: 'More than 30% of form submissions have no owner assigned',

&#x20;     action: 'Set up lead rotation workflows in HubSpot',

&#x20;     urgency: 'medium'

&#x20;   })

&#x20; }

&#x20; 

&#x20; return recommendations

}

15\. KEY CONSTRAINTS FOR CLAUDE CODE

Never expose HubSpot tokens to the client — all HubSpot calls go through Next.js API routes or Supabase Edge Functions

Row Level Security must be on for all tables — no client ever sees another client's data

Role check in both middleware AND component level — use RoleGate.tsx wrapper component

Plan-based content gating — academy content checks company.plan before rendering

All images/certificates stored in Supabase Storage — never in public CDN without auth

Certificate share link is public but contains only name + course + date — no company data

Supabase Vault for HubSpot token encryption at rest

Use shadcn/ui for all base components, customized with the brand tokens above

Fonts: Load Sora + DM Sans from Google Fonts in layout.tsx

All forms use React Hook Form + Zod validation

17\. HUBSPOT UI EXTENSION — AGENT GUIDANCE CARD

Overview

This is a native HubSpot CRM card that lives inside Contact, Deal, and Company records. Agents using HubSpot see a panel called "OPS Guidance" that shows them the next recommended action based on the current lifecycle stage of that record.

Visibility is plan-gated: the card only activates for companies whose plan allows it. Agents do not need to leave HubSpot. Everything renders inline inside the CRM.



How It Works (Architecture)

HubSpot CRM Record (Contact / Deal)

&#x20; └── OPS Guidance Card (UI Extension)

&#x20;       └── Calls your Next.js API route

&#x20;             └── Reads lifecycle stage from HubSpot record context

&#x20;                   └── Queries Supabase for matching guidance steps

&#x20;                         └── Checks company plan (show or hide)

&#x20;                               └── Returns guidance to the card



The card receives the HubSpot record context automatically (contact ID, deal stage, associated company ID). It uses that to look up the right guidance from your platform.



New Database Tables

17.1 lifecycle\_guidance

CREATE TABLE lifecycle\_guidance (

&#x20; id              UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen\_random\_uuid(),

&#x20; stage           TEXT NOT NULL,

&#x20; -- visitor | subscriber | lead | mql | sql | opportunity | customer | churned

&#x20; title           TEXT NOT NULL,

&#x20; description     TEXT,

&#x20; action\_label    TEXT,           -- e.g. "Enroll in Welcome Sequence"

&#x20; action\_type     TEXT,           -- tip | task | sequence | alert | academy\_link

&#x20; academy\_module\_id UUID REFERENCES course\_modules(id),

&#x20; order\_index     INT DEFAULT 0,

&#x20; plan\_required   TEXT DEFAULT 'basic',  -- basic | pro | enterprise

&#x20; is\_active       BOOLEAN DEFAULT true,

&#x20; created\_by      UUID REFERENCES profiles(id),

&#x20; created\_at      TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT now()

);



17.2 guidance\_completions

CREATE TABLE guidance\_completions (

&#x20; id              UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen\_random\_uuid(),

&#x20; hubspot\_user\_id TEXT NOT NULL,   -- HubSpot agent user ID

&#x20; hubspot\_record\_id TEXT NOT NULL, -- contact or deal ID

&#x20; guidance\_id     UUID REFERENCES lifecycle\_guidance(id),

&#x20; company\_id      UUID REFERENCES companies(id),

&#x20; completed\_at    TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT now(),

&#x20; UNIQUE(hubspot\_user\_id, hubspot\_record\_id, guidance\_id)

);



17.3 hubspot\_app\_installs

CREATE TABLE hubspot\_app\_installs (

&#x20; id              UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen\_random\_uuid(),

&#x20; company\_id      UUID REFERENCES companies(id),

&#x20; hubspot\_portal\_id TEXT NOT NULL,

&#x20; access\_token    TEXT,            -- encrypted via Supabase Vault

&#x20; refresh\_token   TEXT,            -- encrypted

&#x20; token\_expires\_at TIMESTAMPTZ,

&#x20; installed\_at    TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT now(),

&#x20; is\_active       BOOLEAN DEFAULT true,

&#x20; UNIQUE(hubspot\_portal\_id)

);





Plan Gating Logic

// lib/hubspot/extensionGate.ts



export function canSeeGuidanceCard(companyPlan: string): boolean {

&#x20; // Basic: card visible but shows only 1 tip per stage (teaser)

&#x20; // Pro: full guidance steps per stage

&#x20; // Enterprise: full guidance + sequence recommendations + academy links

&#x20; const planOrder = { basic: 1, pro: 2, enterprise: 3 }

&#x20; return planOrder\[companyPlan] >= 1  // all plans see it, content differs

}



export function getGuidanceLimit(companyPlan: string): number {

&#x20; if (companyPlan === 'enterprise') return 999   // unlimited

&#x20; if (companyPlan === 'pro') return 5             // up to 5 steps per stage

&#x20; return 1                                        // basic: 1 tip only (upsell hook)

}



For Basic plan the card shows 1 step + a locked state with "Upgrade to Pro to unlock all guidance steps" — this is your in-HubSpot upsell moment.



HubSpot Public App Setup (Steps for Claude Code)

Create a HubSpot Developer Account at developers.hubspot.com

Create a new Public App under your developer portal

Configure scopes needed:

&#x20;crm.objects.contacts.readcrm.objects.deals.readcrm.objects.companies.readoauth





Set OAuth redirect URI to:

&#x20;https://app.opsolutionss.com/api/hubspot/oauth/callback





Enable UI Extensions under the app settings

Deploy the card extension pointing to:

&#x20;https://app.opsolutionss.com/hubspot-extension







New API Routes (Next.js)

app/

├── api/

│   └── hubspot/

│       ├── oauth/

│       │   ├── install/route.ts        # Redirect to HubSpot OAuth

│       │   └── callback/route.ts       # Handle token exchange + save to DB

│       ├── guidance/route.ts           # Card calls this to get steps

│       └── complete/route.ts           # Mark a guidance step done

└── hubspot-extension/

&#x20;   └── page.tsx                        # The UI Extension React component





guidance/route.ts Logic

// app/api/hubspot/guidance/route.ts

// Called by the UI Extension card with: portalId, recordId, lifecycleStage



export async function GET(req: Request) {

&#x20; const { searchParams } = new URL(req.url)

&#x20; const portalId     = searchParams.get('portalId')

&#x20; const stage        = searchParams.get('lifecycleStage') // from HubSpot record context

&#x20; const hubspotUserId = searchParams.get('userId')



&#x20; // 1. Look up company by portalId in hubspot\_app\_installs

&#x20; // 2. Get company plan

&#x20; // 3. Get guidance steps for this stage, filtered by plan limit

&#x20; // 4. Get already-completed steps for this user + record

&#x20; // 5. Return steps with completed flags



&#x20; return Response.json({ steps, companyPlan, completedIds })

}





UI Extension Card — Component Spec

File: app/hubspot-extension/page.tsx

The card renders inside HubSpot. It uses the @hubspot/ui-extensions-sdk package. Layout:

┌─────────────────────────────────────┐

│  🧭 OPS Guidance                    │

│  Stage: MQL  ──────────────── Pro   │

├─────────────────────────────────────┤

│  ✅ Verify contact owner assigned   │

│  ✅ Check lead source is captured   │

│  ▶  Enroll in MQL nurture sequence  │  ← current step (highlighted)

│  🔒 Review scoring model fit        │  ← next step (locked until above done)

│  🔒 Schedule discovery call         │

├─────────────────────────────────────┤

│  \[Mark as Done]   \[Open Academy →]  │

└─────────────────────────────────────┘



Visual rules:

Completed steps: checkmark, muted color, struck through

Current step: accent color (#ff7a59), arrow icon, bold

Locked steps: lock icon, greyed out

Plan upgrade prompt (Basic only): banner below steps



OAuth Install Flow

When a HubSpot admin installs your app from the marketplace or via install link:

They land on your install page: https://app.opsolutionss.com/hubspot/install

They are redirected to HubSpot OAuth consent screen

After approval, HubSpot redirects to your callback with code

Your callback:

Exchanges code for access\_token + refresh\_token

Identifies the portalId

Looks up matching company in your DB by hubspot\_token or portal ID

Saves tokens to hubspot\_app\_installs

Redirects to success page

The UI Extension card is now live for all agents in that portal

Connection Between Portal and HubSpot Card

When an agent marks a guidance step as done in HubSpot:

It writes to guidance\_completions in Supabase

The client portal (/client/\[companyId]/analytics) shows aggregate completion stats

CLIENT\_MANAGER can see how many steps their agents have completed per stage

SUPERADMIN (Mostafa) sees this across all companies

This closes the loop: you build the guidance in your portal, agents execute it in HubSpot, progress flows back into your portal for client visibility.

Gimini plan



Yes, that is a highly effective way to differentiate this SaaS. Integrating your "guidelines" and "academy" directly where the agents work (inside HubSpot) is known as Contextual Enablement. Instead of making agents leave the CRM to go to your portal, you bring the portal's intelligence to them. Here is how that works technically and strategically to achieve an "Arrows-like" or "Supered-like" experience:

1\. The Technical "How-To"

To guide agents directly inside the CRM, there are three primary paths:

HubSpot UI Extensions (The Native Way): HubSpot now allows developers to build custom cards and tabs directly in the middle or right-hand sidebar of a record (Deal, Contact, or Company). You can display your "Steps and Tricks" or "Next Actions" right there.

Custom CRM Cards: You can use your Supabase data to feed a "Card" in HubSpot. For example, if an agent is on a Deal, the card could show: "Training Status: 50% Complete. Watch 'How to move to SQL' to proceed."

Chrome Extension (The Overlay Way): This is how tools like Supered or Spekit work. By building a companion Chrome Extension for your SaaS, you can place "floating bubbles" or sidebar overlays on top of any CRM (HubSpot, Salesforce, etc.) without needing a deep native integration for every feature.

2\. The "In-CRM" Feature Set

To replicate the value of Arrows for agent guidance, your SaaS would focus on these specific functionalities:

Playbook Overlays: When an agent opens a specific stage (e.g., "Discovery"), a sidebar from your SaaS appears with the specific Doc materials or Video tips you uploaded for that stage.

The "Required Action" Sync: Just as Arrows syncs task completion to HubSpot properties, your SaaS can update a HubSpot "Property" once an employee completes a video in your Academy. This can then trigger a "Next Step" in the CRM.

Audit Alerts: If your AI Diagnosis app detects an error (e.g., a missing field or a stalled deal), a notification can pop up directly in the CRM record via the integration, telling the agent exactly what to fix.

3\. Comparison of Guidance Styles

To help you choose the right direction, here is how the "Inner-CRM" guidance market is currently split:

Feature Style

Key Inspiration

How it Works

Task-Based

Arrows

Shows a clear checklist of what the agent or customer needs to do next.

Knowledge-Based

Spekit / Supered

Provides "just-in-time" learning snippets (videos/docs) when the user hovers over a button.

Data-Based

Gong / Clari

Analyzes the record and gives a "Health Score" or "Warning" if the deal looks risky.



4\. Strategic "Wildcard" Idea: The "Co-Pilot" View

Instead of just a portal, you could build a "Shared Command Center":

The Left Side: The actual HubSpot Record.

The Right Side (Your SaaS): The Academy training, the Before/After proof, and the "Expert Recommendations" specific to that deal.

This makes your software feel less like a "separate website" and more like an "Advanced Operating Layer" sitting on top of the CRM.

Would you like to focus the initial build on a HubSpot-native "UI Extension," or would you prefer the flexibility of a "Chrome Extension" that can work on any CRM?





Deepseek plan 

Absolutely. You can build a deep integration where your platform guides users directly inside HubSpot, just like Arrows does. In fact, by combining HubSpot's native "UI Extensions" with your existing architecture, your solution will be uniquely positioned to provide both \*\*process guidance\*\* and \*\*strategic analytics\*\* in one place.



This is how to make it happen, using the same technical methods that Arrows and other top-tier apps use:



\### 🚀 Your Platform, Inside HubSpot: The Key Integration Points



You can embed your entire experience inside HubSpot, right where your clients' teams are already working. This eliminates the friction of switching between tabs.



\*   \*\*Embed via UI Extensions (Custom CRM Cards)\*\*: HubSpot provides a framework called \*\*UI Extensions\*\*. This lets you build custom React-based cards that can be placed in the right sidebar or as a new tab on any HubSpot record (Contacts, Deals, Tickets, etc.). This is the \*\*exact method Arrows uses\*\* to let users manage their onboarding plans without leaving HubSpot. Your entire Ops OS dashboard—with its unique funnel views, training checklists, and "before/after" snapshots—can be presented directly in the HubSpot interface.



\*   \*\*Launch Workflows from HubSpot Records\*\*: You can design your system so that a user, looking at a new Deal in HubSpot, could click a button in your custom card to instantly launch a pre-built Ops OS implementation plan. That plan could then pull data from the Deal record (like company size or product tier) to dynamically show or hide specific tasks.



\*   \*\*Powerful Two-Way Data Sync\*\*: The integration isn't just about what users see. It's about data flow. Your platform will use HubSpot APIs to:

&#x20;   1.  \*\*Read Data\*\*: Pull deal stage, contact properties, and lifecycle stage to power your dashboards.

&#x20;   2.  \*\*Write Data\*\*: Push data back to HubSpot. For example, when a user completes a training course in your Academy, you can update a "Training Completed" property on their Contact record in HubSpot. This can then trigger HubSpot workflows and reports.



\### 📈 A Smarter Guidance Layer: Your Unique Advantage



While tools like Arrows are excellent for guided processes, your vision for Ops OS creates a much more powerful and personalized experience. You can go beyond static checklists by integrating \*\*analytics and AI\*\*.



\*   \*\*Personalized In-App Guidance\*\*: By combining with a tool like \*\*Userflow\*\* or \*\*VisualSP\*\*, you can trigger specific, step-by-step walkthroughs \*inside HubSpot\* based on a user's activity. For instance, if a sales rep's MQL-to-SQL conversion rate is low, your platform could automatically launch a guided checklist that shows them exactly how to properly score and convert a lead in HubSpot.



\*   \*\*AI-Powered Recommendations\*\*: This is where your "AI diagnosis" app becomes a true differentiator. Your system can analyze their HubSpot data, identify a bottleneck (e.g., deals are stalling in the "Demo Scheduled" stage), and then surface a contextual recommendation within your HubSpot CRM card. It could suggest a relevant training course from your Academy, a new email template, or a change to their deal workflow—all from within their daily workspace.



\### 🛠️ The Implementation Path: From MVP to Full Integration



Here’s a phased, practical roadmap to building this integration using your existing stack (Lovable + Supabase).



1\.  \*\*Core HubSpot Integration (Immediate)\*\*: Start by building the data pipeline. Use a Supabase Edge Function to securely handle OAuth and fetch data from HubSpot's APIs. You can then present this data in a custom dashboard on your own platform—this is a great MVP to demonstrate the value of the analytics layer to clients.



2\.  \*\*Build a Private App with UI Extensions (Next Step)\*\*: This is the step that puts you "inside" HubSpot. You'll need to create a HubSpot Developer Account and build a "Private App". For the front-end, you can develop a simple custom CRM card using React, which you can then deploy. This card can fetch and display data from your Supabase backend using API calls. There are open-source examples on GitHub to help you get started.



3\.  \*\*Full Integration \& User Experience (Future)\*\*: This is the complete vision. In this phase, you would:

&#x20;   \*   Build out the full Ops OS dashboard to be embeddable in HubSpot tabs.

&#x20;   \*   Add interactive features like commenting, before/after image galleries, and the full Academy experience.

&#x20;   \*   Implement AI-driven recommendations that analyze the CRM data and present actionable insights to users.



\### 💡 Strategic Inspiration



Your vision of combining guidance with intelligence is already being validated by the market.



\*   \*\*Arrows\*\* proves there is massive demand for embedding a collaborative, guided workflow directly onto CRM records.

\*   \*\*AdoptionHub\*\* validates the need for tools that train and enforce unique processes \*inside\* HubSpot.



Your advantage is in creating a system that is not just a to-do list, but a \*\*data-driven coach for the GTM team\*\*, uniquely blending implementation, enablement, and performance visibility.



This approach elevates your platform from a simple integration to an intelligent layer on top of the CRM, making you an indispensable partner for your clients. If you want to dive deeper into the specifics of building a UI Extension or setting up the OAuth flow, just let me know.
