Below is a clear breakdown of \*\*how to embed Ops Solutions guidance directly into HubSpot\*\*, ranked by effort vs. impact, with technical options you can implement in Lovable + Supabase.



\---



\## 🎯 Goal: "Arrows-Style" In-CRM Guidance for Your Clients



> \*"When a sales agent opens a Contact/Deal in HubSpot, they see a contextual sidebar from Ops Solutions showing:  

> • Their assigned training progress  

> • Audit recommendations for this record  

> • Next operational step (e.g., 'Update lifecycle stage')  

> • Quick link to complete a micro-course"\*



\---



\## 🔧 Integration Options (Ranked)



\### ✅ Option 1: HubSpot UI Extensions (Recommended — Native \& Scalable)

\*\*What it is\*\*: Official HubSpot framework to embed custom React components directly into CRM record pages (Contact, Company, Deal, Ticket).



| Feature | Implementation |

|---------|---------------|

| \*\*Where it appears\*\* | Right sidebar of any CRM object page |

| \*\*Tech stack\*\* | React + HubSpot UI Extensions SDK + Supabase API |

| \*\*Auth\*\* | OAuth 2.0 via HubSpot private app (tokens stored encrypted in Supabase) |

| \*\*Data flow\*\* | Extension fetches user's progress/tasks from your Supabase backend using `hubspot\_user\_id` |

| \*\*Permissions\*\* | Respects HubSpot user roles + your platform's RLS policies |



\*\*Example UI in HubSpot\*\*:

```

\[Ops Solutions Panel]

✓ Welcome, Ahmed!  

🎓 Training: "Lead Qualification Basics" — 2/3 modules complete  

💡 Recommendation: Add "Company Size" property to this contact  

➕ Next Step: Update lifecycle stage → "Marketing Qualified"  

\[Complete Micro-Task] \[View Full Academy]

```



\*\*Effort\*\*: Medium (3-5 days for MVP extension)  

\*\*Impact\*\*: High — feels native, zero context-switching for users



🔗 Docs: \[HubSpot UI Extensions Guide](https://developers.hubspot.com/docs/ui-extensions)



\---



\### ✅ Option 2: HubSpot Tasks + Webhooks Sync (Fastest MVP)

\*\*What it is\*\*: Push guided steps from your platform → HubSpot Tasks object. When user completes task in HubSpot, webhook updates your system.



| Feature | Implementation |

|---------|---------------|

| \*\*Where it appears\*\* | HubSpot Tasks tab (native) |

| \*\*Tech stack\*\* | Supabase Edge Functions + HubSpot Tasks API + Webhooks |

| \*\*Auth\*\* | Same OAuth flow; no UI injection needed |

| \*\*Data flow\*\* | Your platform creates Task → HubSpot API → assigned to user → completion webhook → update Supabase |

| \*\*Permissions\*\* | Uses HubSpot's native task assignment + visibility |



\*\*Example Workflow\*\*:

1\. Ops employee flags: "Contact missing industry property"  

2\. Your system creates HubSpot Task: "Add industry to \[Contact Name]"  

3\. Agent sees task in their HubSpot inbox  

4\. Agent completes task → webhook triggers → your platform marks step complete + unlocks next training module



\*\*Effort\*\*: Low (1-2 days)  

\*\*Impact\*\*: Medium — leverages native UX, but less "wow" than embedded sidebar



🔗 Docs: \[HubSpot Tasks API](https://developers.hubspot.com/docs/api/crm/tasks)



\---



\### ⚙️ Option 3: Chrome Extension Companion (CRM-Agnostic)

\*\*What it is\*\*: Browser extension that detects HubSpot (or Salesforce/Zoho) URLs and overlays your guidance UI.



| Feature | Implementation |

|---------|---------------|

| \*\*Where it appears\*\* | Floating widget or sidebar overlay on CRM pages |

| \*\*Tech stack\*\* | React + Chrome Extensions Manifest V3 + Supabase API |

| \*\*Auth\*\* | Supabase session token stored in extension storage |

| \*\*Data flow\*\* | Extension reads URL → extracts record ID → fetches guidance from your backend |

| \*\*Permissions\*\* | Works across any CRM; no vendor approval needed |



\*\*Pros\*\*:  

\- Works for clients on Salesforce, Zoho, etc.  

\- No HubSpot app review process  

\- Can inject contextual tooltips/walkthroughs  



\*\*Cons\*\*:  

\- Requires user to install extension  

\- Slightly less "polished" than native extensions  



\*\*Effort\*\*: Medium-High (4-7 days)  

\*\*Impact\*\*: High for multi-CRM consultancies



\---



\### 🚫 Option 4: iFrame Embed via Custom Code (Not Recommended for Production)

\*\*What it is\*\*: Add your platform as an `<iframe>` in HubSpot via custom code module or page injection.



| Issue | Why Avoid |

|-------|-----------|

| \*\*Security\*\* | iFrames can be blocked by CSP policies; token leakage risk |

| \*\*UX\*\* | Clunky scrolling, mobile-unfriendly, no native styling |

| \*\*Maintenance\*\* | Breaks if HubSpot changes DOM structure |

| \*\*Approval\*\* | Won't pass HubSpot App Marketplace review |



→ Only use for internal prototyping, not client-facing.



\---



\## 🔄 Bidirectional Sync Architecture (Supabase + HubSpot)



```mermaid

graph LR

&#x20;   A\[Ops Solutions Platform] <--> B\[Supabase Edge Functions]

&#x20;   B <--> C\[HubSpot API]

&#x20;   C <--> D\[HubSpot UI: Tasks/Extensions]

&#x20;   

&#x20;   E\[User completes task in HubSpot] --> F\[Webhook to Edge Function]

&#x20;   F --> G\[Update Supabase: enrollment progress]

&#x20;   G --> H\[Trigger: unlock next module / notify manager]

&#x20;   

&#x20;   I\[Ops employee adds recommendation] --> J\[Create HubSpot Task via API]

&#x20;   J --> K\[Task appears in agent's HubSpot inbox]

```



\### 🔐 Critical Security Notes:

1\. \*\*Never expose Supabase keys to frontend\*\* — all HubSpot API calls go through Edge Functions

2\. \*\*Encrypt HubSpot tokens\*\* using `pgcrypto` in Supabase

3\. \*\*Validate record ownership\*\* — ensure user can only see guidance for records they own in HubSpot

4\. \*\*Rate limit API calls\*\* — HubSpot has strict limits (100 req/10s per app)



\---



\## 🧩 Sample Data Model Additions (Supabase)



```sql

\-- Link HubSpot users to your platform users

hubspot\_user\_mappings (

&#x20; id UUID PK,

&#x20; platform\_user\_id UUID FK REFERENCES users(id),

&#x20; hubspot\_user\_id TEXT, -- HubSpot's internal user ID

&#x20; hubspot\_portal\_id TEXT,

&#x20; oauth\_access\_token TEXT, -- encrypted

&#x20; oauth\_refresh\_token TEXT, -- encrypted

&#x20; token\_expires\_at TIMESTAMPTZ,

&#x20; UNIQUE(hubspot\_user\_id, hubspot\_portal\_id)

)



\-- Guidance steps that can be pushed to HubSpot

guidance\_steps (

&#x20; id UUID PK,

&#x20; company\_id UUID FK,

&#x20; title TEXT,

&#x20; description TEXT,

&#x20; hubspot\_object\_type TEXT CHECK (type IN ('contact', 'company', 'deal', 'ticket')),

&#x20; trigger\_condition JSONB, -- e.g., {property: "lifecyclestage", equals: "lead"}

&#x20; action\_type TEXT CHECK (action IN ('task', 'notification', 'training\_unlock')),

&#x20; training\_module\_id UUID FK REFERENCES modules(id),

&#x20; created\_at TIMESTAMPTZ

)



\-- Track completion of in-CRM guidance

guidance\_completions (

&#x20; id UUID PK,

&#x20; step\_id UUID FK,

&#x20; hubspot\_user\_id TEXT,

&#x20; hubspot\_record\_id TEXT, -- the contact/deal ID where action was taken

&#x20; completed\_at TIMESTAMPTZ,

&#x20; source TEXT CHECK (source IN ('hubspot\_task', 'ui\_extension', 'chrome\_extension'))

)

```

\## 💡 Pro Tips for Mostafa



1\. \*\*Start with Tasks sync\*\* — delivers immediate value with minimal code, validates the workflow with clients.

2\. \*\*Use your existing AI Diagnose App\*\* as the "brain" — feed HubSpot record data to it, return recommendations to display in-extension.

3\. \*\*White-label the extension\*\* — use the company's branding config (colors/logo) so it feels like their internal tool.

4\. \*\*Add Arabic support early\*\* — no major competitor offers in-CRM guidance in Arabic; huge differentiator for your MENA clients.

5\. \*\*Track "guidance adoption" as a KPI\*\* — measure how many recommended steps users complete → proves ROI to clients.

```
&#x20;     │              │              │
```

\## 👥 Role Matrix (Final)



| Role | Scope | Key Permissions | UI Access |

|------|-------|----------------|-----------|

| \*\*Super Admin\*\* (Mostafa) | Global | ✅ All companies/users/courses<br>✅ Impersonate any user<br>✅ Manage billing/plans<br>✅ View all analytics/logs | Full admin panel + all client views |

| \*\*Ops Employee\*\* | Assigned companies | ✅ View/edit assigned clients<br>✅ Post updates, audits, enhancements<br>✅ Upload training materials<br>❌ Cannot delete companies | Dashboard filtered to assigned companies |

| \*\*Customer Admin\*\* | Single company | ✅ Full dashboard + analytics<br>✅ Manage their employees<br>✅ Comment on updates<br>❌ Cannot edit HubSpot config | Branded client portal (white-label) |

| \*\*Customer Manager\*\* | Single company + team | ✅ View assigned employees' progress<br>✅ View team analytics<br>✅ Comment on updates<br>❌ Cannot invite users or change settings | Filtered portal view |

| \*\*Customer Employee\*\* | Single company + assigned content | ✅ Complete assigned courses<br>✅ View personal progress/certs<br>✅ View updates shared with them<br>❌ Cannot see analytics or other users | Minimal training + update view |

\## 🗄️ Core Database Schema (Supabase — Final)



\### 🏢 Companies + Users

```sql

companies (

&#x20; id UUID PK DEFAULT gen\_random\_uuid(),

&#x20; name TEXT NOT NULL,

&#x20; website TEXT,

&#x20; domain TEXT UNIQUE,

&#x20; industry TEXT,

&#x20; employee\_count TEXT, -- '1-10', '11-50', '51-200', '200+'

&#x20; country TEXT,

&#x20; region TEXT, -- 'MENA', 'NA', 'EMEA', 'APAC'

&#x20; logo\_url TEXT, -- auto-fetched

&#x20; plan TEXT DEFAULT 'basic' CHECK (plan IN ('basic','pro','enterprise')),

&#x20; hubspot\_portal\_id TEXT,

&#x20; hubspot\_access\_token TEXT, -- encrypted via pgcrypto

&#x20; hubspot\_refresh\_token TEXT, -- encrypted

&#x20; branding\_config JSONB DEFAULT '{"primary":"#425b76","secondary":"#333333","accent":"#ff7a59"}',

&#x20; language TEXT DEFAULT 'en' CHECK (language IN ('en','ar')),

&#x20; is\_rtl BOOLEAN DEFAULT false,

&#x20; created\_by UUID REFERENCES auth.users(id),

&#x20; created\_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT now()

);



profiles (

&#x20; id UUID PK REFERENCES auth.users(id),

&#x20; full\_name TEXT,

&#x20; email TEXT UNIQUE,

&#x20; avatar\_url TEXT,

&#x20; role TEXT NOT NULL CHECK (role IN ('super\_admin','ops\_employee','client\_admin','client\_manager','client\_employee')),

&#x20; company\_id UUID REFERENCES companies(id),

&#x20; manager\_id UUID REFERENCES profiles(id), -- for employee→manager link

&#x20; hubspot\_user\_id TEXT, -- HubSpot's internal user ID

&#x20; is\_active BOOLEAN DEFAULT true,

&#x20; seen\_intro BOOLEAN DEFAULT false, -- for first-login video

&#x20; created\_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT now()

);

```



\### 📊 Analytics + Funnel

```sql

funnel\_snapshots (

&#x20; id UUID PK,

&#x20; company\_id UUID FK,

&#x20; snapshot\_date DATE DEFAULT CURRENT\_DATE,

&#x20; stage TEXT CHECK (stage IN ('visitor','subscriber','lead','mql','sql','opportunity','customer')),

&#x20; count INT,

&#x20; conversion\_rate DECIMAL(5,2),

&#x20; avg\_time\_in\_stage\_hours INT,

&#x20; source TEXT CHECK (source IN ('hubspot','manual','scraped')),

&#x20; created\_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT now()

);



form\_tracking (

&#x20; id UUID PK,

&#x20; company\_id UUID FK,

&#x20; form\_name TEXT,

&#x20; form\_type TEXT CHECK (form\_type IN ('lead\_1','lead\_2','subscriber\_1','subscriber\_2','custom')),

&#x20; hubspot\_form\_id TEXT,

&#x20; total\_submissions INT DEFAULT 0,

&#x20; with\_owner INT DEFAULT 0,

&#x20; without\_owner INT DEFAULT 0,

&#x20; offline\_count INT DEFAULT 0,

&#x20; source\_breakdown JSONB, -- {"organic":45,"paid":30,"referral":15,"direct":10}

&#x20; last\_synced TIMESTAMPTZ,

&#x20; created\_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT now()

);



social\_metrics (

&#x20; id UUID PK,

&#x20; company\_id UUID FK,

&#x20; platform TEXT CHECK (platform IN ('linkedin','twitter','instagram','facebook')),

&#x20; profile\_url TEXT,

&#x20; followers\_count INT,

&#x20; posts\_count INT,

&#x20; avg\_engagement\_rate DECIMAL(5,2),

&#x20; last\_scraped TIMESTAMPTZ,

&#x20; source TEXT DEFAULT 'microlink' CHECK (source IN ('microlink','manual','puppeteer')),

&#x20; created\_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT now()

);

```



\### 🎓 Academy + Certificates

```sql

courses (

&#x20; id UUID PK,

&#x20; title TEXT NOT NULL,

&#x20; description TEXT,

&#x20; thumbnail\_url TEXT,

&#x20; order\_index INT DEFAULT 0,

&#x20; plan\_required TEXT DEFAULT 'basic',

&#x20; content\_type TEXT DEFAULT 'both' CHECK (content\_type IN ('doc','video','both')),

&#x20; is\_sequential BOOLEAN DEFAULT true,

&#x20; is\_published BOOLEAN DEFAULT false,

&#x20; created\_by UUID REFERENCES profiles(id),

&#x20; created\_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT now()

);



modules (

&#x20; id UUID PK,

&#x20; course\_id UUID FK,

&#x20; title TEXT NOT NULL,

&#x20; order\_index INT DEFAULT 0,

&#x20; doc\_url TEXT, -- Lovable academy doc link

&#x20; video\_url TEXT, -- Supabase Storage or external

&#x20; duration\_mins INT,

&#x20; is\_locked\_until\_prev\_complete BOOLEAN DEFAULT true,

&#x20; quiz\_questions JSONB, -- optional

&#x20; created\_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT now()

);



enrollments (

&#x20; id UUID PK,

&#x20; user\_id UUID FK,

&#x20; course\_id UUID FK,

&#x20; progress\_percent DECIMAL(5,2) DEFAULT 0,

&#x20; completed\_at TIMESTAMPTZ,

&#x20; UNIQUE(user\_id, course\_id)

);



module\_progress (

&#x20; id UUID PK,

&#x20; enrollment\_id UUID FK,

&#x20; module\_id UUID FK,

&#x20; completed BOOLEAN DEFAULT false,

&#x20; completed\_at TIMESTAMPTZ,

&#x20; time\_spent\_seconds INT,

&#x20; UNIQUE(enrollment\_id, module\_id)

);



certificate\_templates (

&#x20; id UUID PK,

&#x20; company\_id UUID FK,

&#x20; template\_name TEXT,

&#x20; background\_image\_url TEXT,

&#x20; gemini\_prompt\_template TEXT, -- for AI generation

&#x20; fields\_config JSONB DEFAULT '{"first\_name":true,"last\_name":true,"course\_name":true,"date":true,"signature":true}',

&#x20; is\_active BOOLEAN DEFAULT true,

&#x20; created\_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT now()

);



certificates (

&#x20; id UUID PK,

&#x20; enrollment\_id UUID FK,

&#x20; generated\_image\_url TEXT, -- Supabase Storage path

&#x20; share\_token TEXT UNIQUE DEFAULT gen\_random\_uuid()::text,

&#x20; shared\_on\_linkedin BOOLEAN DEFAULT false,

&#x20; generated\_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT now()

);

```

```sql
&#x20; description TEXT,

&#x20; before\_image\_url TEXT,

&#x20; after\_image\_url TEXT,

&#x20; visible\_to\_roles TEXT\[] DEFAULT ARRAY\['client\_admin','client\_manager'],

&#x20; visible\_to\_users UUID\[], -- granular user selection

&#x20; created\_by UUID REFERENCES profiles(id),

hubspot\_audits (

&#x20; status TEXT DEFAULT 'draft' CHECK (status IN ('draft','published','archived'))

);

```



\### 🔄 In-CRM Guidance (Arrows-Style)

```sql

lifecycle\_guidance (

&#x20; id UUID PK,

&#x20; stage TEXT NOT NULL CHECK (stage IN ('visitor','subscriber','lead','mql','sql','opportunity','customer')),

&#x20; title TEXT NOT NULL,

&#x20; description TEXT,

&#x20; action\_label TEXT, -- e.g., "Enroll in Welcome Sequence"

&#x20; action\_type TEXT CHECK (action\_type IN ('tip','task','sequence','alert','academy\_link')),

&#x20; academy\_module\_id UUID REFERENCES modules(id),

&#x20; hubspot\_property\_to\_update TEXT, -- optional: auto-update HubSpot on completion

&#x20; order\_index INT DEFAULT 0,

&#x20; plan\_required TEXT DEFAULT 'basic',

&#x20; is\_active BOOLEAN DEFAULT true,

&#x20; created\_by UUID REFERENCES profiles(id),

&#x20; created\_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT now()

);



guidance\_completions (

&#x20; id UUID PK,

&#x20; hubspot\_user\_id TEXT NOT NULL,

&#x20; hubspot\_record\_id TEXT NOT NULL, -- contact/deal ID

&#x20; guidance\_id UUID FK,

&#x20; company\_id UUID FK,

&#x20; completed\_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT now(),

&#x20; source TEXT CHECK (source IN ('ui\_extension','task\_sync','chrome\_extension')),

&#x20; UNIQUE(hubspot\_user\_id, hubspot\_record\_id, guidance\_id)

);



hubspot\_app\_installs (

&#x20; id UUID PK,

&#x20; company\_id UUID FK,

&#x20; hubspot\_portal\_id TEXT UNIQUE NOT NULL,

&#x20; access\_token TEXT, -- encrypted

&#x20; refresh\_token TEXT, -- encrypted

&#x20; token\_expires\_at TIMESTAMPTZ,

&#x20; installed\_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT now(),

&#x20; is\_active BOOLEAN DEFAULT true

);

```

```sql
&#x20; content TEXT, -- rich text (Tiptap JSON)

&#x20; visibility TEXT\[] DEFAULT ARRAY\['client\_admin'], -- role-based

&#x20; visible\_to\_users UUID\[], -- granular user selection (like HubSpot dashboard share)

&#x20; created\_by UUID REFERENCES profiles(id),

comments (

&#x20; update\_id UUID FK,

&#x20; user\_id UUID FK,

);
```

\### 🎯 Benchmarks + Recommendations

```sql

industry\_benchmarks (

&#x20; id UUID PK,

&#x20; industry TEXT NOT NULL,

&#x20; region TEXT, -- 'global', 'mena', 'na', 'emea', 'apac'

&#x20; stage TEXT,

&#x20; metric\_key TEXT, -- 'lead\_to\_mql', 'mql\_to\_sql', 'sql\_to\_close'

&#x20; benchmark\_value DECIMAL(5,2),

&#x20; source TEXT, -- 'internal', 'bizminer', 'databox', 'manual'

&#x20; sample\_size INT,

&#x20; updated\_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT now(),

&#x20; UNIQUE(industry, region, stage, metric\_key)

);



recommendations (

&#x20; id UUID PK,

&#x20; company\_id UUID FK,

&#x20; area TEXT, -- 'lead\_scoring', 'routing', 'nurture', 'reporting'

&#x20; issue TEXT,

&#x20; action TEXT,

&#x20; urgency TEXT CHECK (urgency IN ('low','medium','high')),

&#x20; linked\_guidance\_id UUID REFERENCES lifecycle\_guidance(id),

&#x20; linked\_module\_id UUID REFERENCES modules(id),

&#x20; is\_dismissed BOOLEAN DEFAULT false,

&#x20; created\_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT now()

);

```



\---



\## 🔐 Row Level Security (Critical — All Tables)



```sql

\-- Enable RLS on all tables

ALTER TABLE companies ENABLE ROW LEVEL SECURITY;

ALTER TABLE profiles ENABLE ROW LEVEL SECURITY;

\-- ... repeat for all tables with company\_id



\-- Companies: only visible to members of that company OR ops team

CREATE POLICY company\_isolation ON companies

&#x20; USING (

&#x20;   id IN (SELECT company\_id FROM profiles WHERE id = auth.uid())

&#x20;   OR EXISTS (

&#x20;     SELECT 1 FROM profiles 

&#x20;     WHERE id = auth.uid() AND role IN ('super\_admin','ops\_employee')

&#x20;   )

&#x20; );



\-- Profiles: users can only see teammates in their own company

CREATE POLICY profile\_isolation ON profiles

&#x20; USING (

&#x20;   company\_id IN (

&#x20;     SELECT company\_id FROM profiles WHERE id = auth.uid()

&#x20;   )

&#x20;   OR EXISTS (

&#x20;     SELECT 1 FROM profiles 

&#x20;     WHERE id = auth.uid() AND role IN ('super\_admin','ops\_employee')

&#x20;   )

&#x20; );



\-- Updates: filtered by visibility array OR specific users

CREATE POLICY update\_visibility ON updates

&#x20; FOR SELECT USING (

&#x20;   company\_id IN (

&#x20;     SELECT company\_id FROM profiles WHERE id = auth.uid()

&#x20;   )

&#x20;   AND (

&#x20;     'all' = ANY(visibility)

&#x20;     OR role = ANY(visibility)

&#x20;     OR auth.uid() = ANY(visible\_to\_users)

&#x20;     OR EXISTS (

&#x20;       SELECT 1 FROM profiles 

&#x20;       WHERE id = auth.uid() AND role IN ('super\_admin','ops\_employee')

&#x20;     )

&#x20;   )

&#x20; );



\-- Add similar RLS policies to: funnel\_snapshots, form\_tracking, 

\-- social\_metrics, courses, modules, enrollments, enhancements, etc.

```



\---



\## 🌐 HubSpot Integration Strategy



\### OAuth Flow (Secure + Per-Company)

```typescript

// lib/hubspot/oauth.ts

export async function initiateHubSpotOAuth(companyId: string) {

&#x20; // 1. Generate state token (company\_id + nonce)

&#x20; // 2. Redirect to: https://app.hubspot.com/oauth/authorize?

&#x20; //    client\_id=...\&redirect\_uri=...\&scope=...\&state=...

}



export async function handleHubSpotCallback(code: string, state: string) {

&#x20; // 1. Verify state matches company\_id

&#x20; // 2. Exchange code for tokens via POST /oauth/v1/token

&#x20; // 3. Encrypt tokens with pgcrypto: pgp\_sym\_encrypt(token, env.VAULT\_KEY)

&#x20; // 4. Store in hubspot\_app\_installs

&#x20; // 5. Schedule token refresh via pg\_cron (1 hour before expiry)

}

```



\### Token Refresh (Automated)

```sql

\-- Supabase pg\_cron job (runs hourly)

SELECT cron.schedule(

&#x20; 'refresh-hubspot-tokens',

&#x20; '0 \* \* \* \*', -- every hour

&#x20; $$

&#x20;   UPDATE hubspot\_app\_installs

&#x20;   SET access\_token = refresh\_token\_logic(access\_token, refresh\_token)

&#x20;   WHERE token\_expires\_at < NOW() + INTERVAL '2 hours'

&#x20;   AND is\_active = true;

&#x20; $$

);

```



\### Key API Endpoints Used

| Data | HubSpot Endpoint | Purpose |

|------|-----------------|---------|

| Contacts by stage | `GET /crm/v3/objects/contacts?properties=lifecyclestage` | Funnel analytics |

| Deals by stage | `GET /crm/v3/objects/deals` | Pipeline tracking |

| Forms list | `GET /marketing/v3/forms` | Form attribution |

| Form submissions | `GET /form-integrations/v1/submissions/forms/{id}` | Lead source tracking |

| Owners | `GET /crm/v3/owners` | Assignment analytics |

| Webhooks | `POST /webhooks/v3/subscriptions` | Real-time sync |

\## 🕷️ Social Scraper (No Meta API — Production Strategy)



```typescript

// lib/scrapers/socialScraper.ts

// Primary: Microlink.io (no API key for basic metadata)

// Fallback: Puppeteer + proxy rotation for complex pages



export async function scrapeSocialMetrics(domain: string, platform: string) {

&#x20; const platforms = {

&#x20;   linkedin: `https://www.linkedin.com/company/${domain}`,

&#x20;   twitter: `https://nitter.net/${domain}`, // no-auth Twitter alternative

&#x20;   instagram: `https://www.instagram.com/${domain}/embed/`,

&#x20;   facebook: `https://graph.facebook.com/${domain}?fields=fan\_count`

&#x20; };



&#x20; try {

&#x20;   // Primary: Microlink.io (free tier, no auth for public pages)

&#x20;   const response = await fetch(

&#x20;     `https://api.microlink.io?url=${encodeURIComponent(platforms\[platform])}`

&#x20;   );

&#x20;   const data = await response.json();

&#x20;   

&#x20;   return {

&#x20;     followers: data.data?.followers || null,

&#x20;     posts: data.data?.posts?.length || null,

&#x20;     engagement: calculateEngagement(data.data) || null

&#x20;   };

&#x20; } catch (error) {

&#x20;   // Fallback: Puppeteer with proxy (for rate-limited platforms)

&#x20;   return await scrapeWithPuppeteer(platforms\[platform]);

&#x20; }

}



// Schedule daily via Supabase Edge Function cron

```

\## 🎨 White-Label + Arabic Support

```typescript

// lib/theming.ts

export function getCompanyTheme(company: Company) {

&#x20; return {

&#x20;   '--color-primary': company.branding\_config.primary || '#425b76',

&#x20;   '--color-secondary': company.branding\_config.secondary || '#333333',

&#x20;   '--color-accent': company.branding\_config.acent || '#ff7a59',

&#x20;   '--direction': company.language === 'ar' ? 'rtl' : 'ltr',

&#x20;   '--font-family': company.language === 'ar' ? 'Tajawal, sans-serif' : 'DM Sans, sans-serif'

&#x20; };

}



// In layout.tsx

<html dir={company.language === 'ar' ? 'rtl' : 'ltr'}>

&#x20; <body style={getCompanyTheme(company)}>

&#x20;   {/\* App content \*/}

&#x20; </body>

</html>

```

```bash
&#x20;   defaultLocale: 'en',

}
```

\## 🎓 Academy + Certificate Engine (Final)



\### Sequential Learning Logic

```typescript

// lib/academy/progress.ts

export async function canAccessModule(userId: string, moduleId: string) {

&#x20; // 1. Get module's course + order\_index

&#x20; // 2. Check if all previous modules are completed

&#x20; // 3. Return boolean + reason if locked

}



// In ModulePlayer component

if (!await canAccessModule(user.id, module.id)) {

&#x20; return <LockedModule message="Complete previous module to unlock" />;

}

```



\### Certificate Generation (Gemini + Canvas)

```typescript

// supabase/functions/generate-certificate/index.ts

import { createCanvas, loadImage } from 'canvas';

import { GoogleGenerativeAI } from '@google/generative-ai';



export async function generateCertificate(enrollmentId: string) {

&#x20; // 1. Fetch enrollment + user + course + template

&#x20; // 2. Build Gemini prompt with user data

&#x20; const prompt = template.gemini\_prompt\_template

&#x20;   .replace('{{first\_name}}', user.first\_name)

&#x20;   .replace('{{last\_name}}', user.last\_name)

&#x20;   .replace('{{course\_name}}', course.title)

&#x20;   .replace('{{date}}', new Date().toLocaleDateString('en-US', { 

&#x20;     year: 'numeric', month: 'long', day: 'numeric' 

&#x20;   }));



&#x20; // 3. Generate image with Gemini (or use Canvas for deterministic output)

&#x20; const canvas = createCanvas(1200, 850);

&#x20; const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');

&#x20; 

&#x20; const bg = await loadImage(template.background\_image\_url);

&#x20; ctx.drawImage(bg, 0, 0, 1200, 850);

&#x20; 

&#x20; // Inject text with Arabic support if needed

&#x20; ctx.font = user.company.language === 'ar' 

&#x20;   ? 'bold 48px Tajawal' 

&#x20;   : 'bold 48px Sora';

&#x20; ctx.textAlign = 'center';

&#x20; ctx.fillText(`${user.first\_name} ${user.last\_name}`, 600, 420);

&#x20; 

&#x20; // 4. Upload to Supabase Storage

&#x20; const buffer = canvas.toBuffer('image/png');

&#x20; const { data } = await supabase.storage

&#x20;   .from('certificates')

&#x20;   .upload(`${company\_id}/${user\_id}/${course\_id}.png`, buffer);

&#x20; 

&#x20; // 5. Create shareable link + notify

&#x20; return { url: data.path, share\_token: generateShareToken() };

}

```

\## 🧭 Navigation Structure (Final)



\### SUPER ADMIN / OPS EMPLOYEE

```

🏠 Dashboard (company grid + KPIs)

🏢 Companies

&#x20; ├── Add Company (wizard: domain→logo→industry→plan)

&#x20; ├── \[Company] Detail (tabs: Overview|Team|Analytics|Updates|Enhancements|Academy)

&#x20; └── HubSpot Token Manager (OAuth flow + test connection)

👥 OPS Team

&#x20; ├── Invite Employee

&#x20; ├── Assign to Companies

&#x20; └── Activity Log

📣 Post Update (rich text + visibility selector + before/after images)

⚙️ Settings

&#x20; ├── Academy Content (courses/modules)

&#x20; ├── Certificate Templates (Gemini prompts + backgrounds)

&#x20; ├── Benchmarks (industry/region data)

&#x20; ├── Intro Video (first-login modal)

&#x20; └── White-Label Config (colors, logo, language)

```



\### CLIENT ADMIN

```

🏠 Overview (funnel summary + recent updates + quick actions)

📊 Analytics

&#x20; ├── Visitors (sessions, conversion rate, top pages)

&#x20; ├── Social (followers, posts, engagement — scraped)

&#x20; ├── Leads (form attribution, owner assignment, source breakdown)

&#x20; ├── MQL (conversion rate, benchmark comparison, recommendations)

&#x20; └── Pipeline (SQL→Opp→Customer, revenue metrics, leakage points)

📣 Updates (feed + comment + before/after gallery)

🛠 Enhancements (before/after visual comparisons by HubSpot area)

🎓 Academy (courses matching plan + progress tracking)

👥 Team (invite/manage employees + view their progress)

🏅 My Certificates (download + share on LinkedIn)

```



\### CLIENT MANAGER

```

📊 Analytics (limited to assigned team's data)

📣 Updates (filtered to visible updates)

🎓 Academy (assigned courses only)

👥 My Team (view assigned employees' progress)

🏅 Team Certificates (view/download team certs)

```



\### CLIENT EMPLOYEE

```

📣 Updates (personalized feed)

🎓 Academy (assigned courses + sequential player)

🏅 My Certificates (personal certs + share buttons)

✅ My Tasks (guidance steps from HubSpot extension)

```

\---



\## ⚠️ Critical Gaps Across All Plans



| Gap | Impact | Solution |

|-----|--------|----------|

| \*\*Arabic RTL UI + Localization\*\* | Blocks MENA client adoption | Add `next-i18next` + RTL CSS variables; store user language preference in `profiles` table |

| \*\*AI Diagnose App Integration\*\* | Missed synergy with existing tool | Embed as iframe in `/client/\[id]/diagnose` + API webhook to push findings to `recommendations` table |

| \*\*Offline Lead Tracking Workflow\*\* | Critical for clients with hybrid sales | Add `lead\_source` enum + manual upload CSV parser + deduplication logic against HubSpot contacts |

| \*\*Certificate Social Sharing (LinkedIn)\*\* | Reduces viral growth potential | Add Open Graph meta tags + LinkedIn Share API integration on certificate share page |

| \*\*Multi-Region Benchmark Data Source\*\* | Weakens recommendation engine | Seed `industry\_benchmarks` table with data from Bizminer API + allow OPS to upload custom benchmarks per client |

| \*\*Token Refresh Automation\*\* | Risk of HubSpot API failures | Supabase pg\_cron job to refresh tokens 1 hour before expiry + alert OPS on failure |

| \*\*Mobile Responsiveness\*\* | Limits field agent adoption | Add mobile-first breakpoints + PWA manifest for offline course viewing |

\*\*RLS Policy Pattern\*\* (Supabase):

```sql

\-- Example: updates table

CREATE POLICY "Updates isolation" ON updates

FOR SELECT USING (

&#x20; company\_id IN (

&#x20;   SELECT company\_id FROM profiles WHERE id = auth.uid()

&#x20; )

&#x20; OR EXISTS (

&#x20;   SELECT 1 FROM profiles 

&#x20;   WHERE id = auth.uid() 

&#x20;   AND role IN ('superadmin', 'ops\_employee')

&#x20; )

&#x20; OR auth.uid() = ANY(visible\_to\_users)

&#x20; OR role = ANY(visibility)

);

```



\---



\## 🗄️ Core Database Schema (Supabase PostgreSQL)



\### 🏢 Companies \& Auth

```sql

companies (

&#x20; id UUID PK DEFAULT gen\_random\_uuid(),

&#x20; name TEXT NOT NULL,

&#x20; website TEXT,

&#x20; domain TEXT UNIQUE,

&#x20; industry TEXT,

&#x20; employee\_count TEXT, -- '1-10', '11-50', '51-200', '200+'

&#x20; country TEXT,

&#x20; region TEXT, -- 'MENA', 'NA', 'EMEA', 'APAC'

&#x20; logo\_url TEXT,

&#x20; plan TEXT DEFAULT 'basic' CHECK (plan IN ('basic','pro','enterprise')),

&#x20; hubspot\_portal\_id TEXT,

&#x20; hubspot\_access\_token TEXT, -- encrypted via pgcrypto

&#x20; hubspot\_refresh\_token TEXT, -- encrypted

&#x20; token\_expires\_at TIMESTAMPTZ,

&#x20; branding\_config JSONB DEFAULT '{"primary":"#425b76","secondary":"#333333","accent":"#ff7a59"}',

&#x20; language TEXT DEFAULT 'en' CHECK (language IN ('en','ar')),

&#x20; created\_by UUID REFERENCES auth.users(id),

&#x20; created\_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT now(),

&#x20; updated\_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT now()

);



profiles (

&#x20; id UUID PK REFERENCES auth.users(id),

&#x20; full\_name TEXT NOT NULL,

&#x20; email TEXT UNIQUE NOT NULL,

&#x20; avatar\_url TEXT,

&#x20; role TEXT NOT NULL CHECK (role IN ('superadmin','ops\_employee','client\_admin','client\_manager','client\_employee')),

&#x20; company\_id UUID REFERENCES companies(id),

&#x20; manager\_id UUID REFERENCES profiles(id), -- for employee → manager link

&#x20; hubspot\_user\_id TEXT, -- HubSpot's internal user ID for extension auth

&#x20; is\_active BOOLEAN DEFAULT true,

&#x20; seen\_intro BOOLEAN DEFAULT false,

&#x20; created\_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT now()

);

```



\### 📊 Analytics \& Funnel

```sql

funnel\_metrics (

&#x20; id UUID PK,

&#x20; company\_id UUID FK,

&#x20; snapshot\_date DATE DEFAULT CURRENT\_DATE,

&#x20; stage TEXT CHECK (stage IN ('visitor','subscriber','lead','mql','sql','opportunity','customer')),

&#x20; count INT DEFAULT 0,

&#x20; conversion\_rate DECIMAL(5,2),

&#x20; avg\_time\_in\_stage\_hours DECIMAL(8,2),

&#x20; source TEXT CHECK (source IN ('hubspot','manual','scraper')),

&#x20; created\_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT now()

);



form\_tracking (

&#x20; id UUID PK,

&#x20; company\_id UUID FK,

&#x20; form\_name TEXT NOT NULL,

&#x20; form\_type TEXT CHECK (form\_type IN ('lead\_1','lead\_2','subscriber\_1','subscriber\_2','custom')),

&#x20; hubspot\_form\_id TEXT,

&#x20; total\_submissions INT DEFAULT 0,

&#x20; with\_owner INT DEFAULT 0,

&#x20; without\_owner INT DEFAULT 0,

&#x20; offline\_submissions INT DEFAULT 0,

&#x20; source\_breakdown JSONB, -- {"organic":45,"paid":30,"referral":15,"direct":10}

&#x20; last\_synced TIMESTAMPTZ,

&#x20; created\_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT now()

);



social\_metrics (

&#x20; id UUID PK,

&#x20; company\_id UUID FK,

&#x20; platform TEXT CHECK (platform IN ('linkedin','twitter','instagram','facebook')),

&#x20; profile\_url TEXT,

&#x20; followers\_count INT,

&#x20; posts\_count INT,

&#x20; avg\_engagement\_rate DECIMAL(5,2),

&#x20; last\_scraped TIMESTAMPTZ,

&#x20; scraper\_source TEXT CHECK (scraper\_source IN ('microlink','puppeteer','manual')),

&#x20; created\_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT now()

);

```



\### 🎓 Academy \& Certificates

```sql

courses (

&#x20; id UUID PK,

&#x20; title TEXT NOT NULL,

&#x20; description TEXT,

&#x20; thumbnail\_url TEXT,

&#x20; order\_index INT DEFAULT 0,

&#x20; plan\_required TEXT DEFAULT 'basic',

&#x20; content\_type TEXT DEFAULT 'both' CHECK (content\_type IN ('doc','video','both')),

&#x20; is\_sequential BOOLEAN DEFAULT true,

&#x20; is\_published BOOLEAN DEFAULT false,

&#x20; created\_by UUID REFERENCES profiles(id),

&#x20; created\_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT now()

);



course\_modules (

&#x20; id UUID PK,

&#x20; course\_id UUID FK REFERENCES courses(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,

&#x20; title TEXT NOT NULL,

&#x20; order\_index INT DEFAULT 0,

&#x20; doc\_url TEXT, -- Lovable academy doc link

&#x20; video\_url TEXT, -- Supabase Storage signed URL

&#x20; duration\_mins INT,

&#x20; is\_locked\_until\_prev BOOLEAN DEFAULT true,

&#x20; quiz\_json JSONB, -- optional quiz questions

&#x20; created\_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT now()

);



course\_progress (

&#x20; id UUID PK,

&#x20; user\_id UUID FK REFERENCES profiles(id),

&#x20; course\_id UUID FK,

&#x20; module\_id UUID FK REFERENCES course\_modules(id),

&#x20; company\_id UUID FK,

&#x20; completed BOOLEAN DEFAULT false,

&#x20; completed\_at TIMESTAMPTZ,

&#x20; time\_spent\_seconds INT DEFAULT 0,

&#x20; UNIQUE(user\_id, module\_id)

);



certificate\_templates (

&#x20; id UUID PK,

&#x20; company\_id UUID FK,

&#x20; template\_name TEXT,

&#x20; background\_image\_url TEXT, -- Supabase Storage

&#x20; gemini\_prompt\_template TEXT,

&#x20; fields\_config JSONB DEFAULT '{"first\_name":true,"last\_name":true,"course\_name":true,"date":true,"signature":true}',

&#x20; is\_active BOOLEAN DEFAULT true,

&#x20; created\_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT now()

);



certificates (

&#x20; id UUID PK,

&#x20; enrollment\_id UUID FK REFERENCES course\_progress(id),

&#x20; generated\_image\_url TEXT, -- Supabase Storage

&#x20; share\_token TEXT UNIQUE DEFAULT gen\_random\_uuid()::text,

&#x20; shared\_on\_linkedin BOOLEAN DEFAULT false,

&#x20; generated\_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT now()

);

```

```sql
);
```

\---



\## 🔄 HubSpot Integration Strategy



\### OAuth Flow (Supabase Edge Function)

```typescript

// /api/hubspot/oauth/install

1\. Redirect to: https://app.hubspot.com/oauth/authorize?client\_id=...\&scope=...

2\. User approves → HubSpot redirects to /api/hubspot/oauth/callback with code

3\. Exchange code for tokens → encrypt with pgcrypto → store in hubspot\_app\_installs

4\. Fetch portal info → match to company by domain or manual selection

5\. Redirect to success page

```



\### Key API Endpoints Used

| Data | HubSpot Endpoint | Sync Frequency |

|------|-----------------|----------------|

| Contacts by lifecycle | `GET /crm/v3/objects/contacts?properties=lifecyclestage` | Every 4h |

| Deals by stage | `GET /crm/v3/objects/deals` | Every 4h |

| Forms list | `GET /marketing/v3/forms` | Daily |

| Form submissions | `GET /form-integrations/v1/submissions/forms/{id}` | Every 2h |

| Traffic analytics | `GET /analytics/v2/reports/totals/daily` | Daily |

| Owners list | `GET /crm/v3/owners` | Weekly |



\### Token Management

\- Encrypt tokens at rest: `pgcrypto` with project-level secret

\- Auto-refresh: Supabase pg\_cron job runs hourly to refresh tokens expiring in <2h

\- Alert OPS on failure: Send email via Resend API if refresh fails 3x



\---



\## 🕷️ Social Scraper Strategy (No Meta API)



\### Primary: Microlink.io (Free Tier)

```typescript

// lib/scrapers/socialScraper.ts

export async function scrapeSocialProfile(platform: string, handle: string) {

&#x20; const url = `https://api.microlink.io?url=https://${platform}.com/${handle}`;

&#x20; const res = await fetch(url, { headers: { 'x-api-key': process.env.MICROLINK\_API\_KEY } });

&#x20; const data = await res.json();

&#x20; 

&#x20; return {

&#x20;   followers: data.data.social?.followers || null,

&#x20;   posts: data.data.social?.posts || null,

&#x20;   engagement: data.data.social?.engagement\_rate || null

&#x20; };

}

```



\### Fallback: Puppeteer Edge Function (for LinkedIn)

```typescript

// Supabase Edge Function (Deno)

import { launch } from 'https://deno.land/x/puppeteer@16.2.0/mod.ts';



export async function scrapeLinkedInCompany(domain: string) {

&#x20; const browser = await launch({ args: \['--no-sandbox'] });

&#x20; const page = await browser.newPage();

&#x20; await page.goto(`https://www.linkedin.com/company/${domain}`, { waitUntil: 'networkidle2' });

&#x20; 

&#x20; const followers = await page.$eval('.followers-count', el => el.textContent);

&#x20; const posts = await page.$$eval('.update-components-actor\_\_container', els => els.length);

&#x20; 

&#x20; await browser.close();

&#x20; return { followers: parseInt(followers), posts };

}

```



\### Rate Limiting \& Caching

\- Max 1 scrape per company per platform per 24h

\- Cache results in `social\_metrics` table with `last\_scraped` timestamp

\- If scraper fails, fall back to manual entry by OPS team

\## 🎓 Academy Engine: Sequential Learning + Certificates



\### Course Player Logic (Frontend)

```typescript

// components/academy/ModulePlayer.tsx

const ModulePlayer = ({ moduleId, userId, companyId }) => {

&#x20; const {  progress } = useCourseProgress(userId, moduleId);

&#x20; const {  module } = useModule(moduleId);

&#x20; const { data: company } = useCompany(companyId);

&#x20; 

&#x20; // Plan-based content gating

&#x20; if (company.plan === 'basic' \&\& module.content\_type === 'video') {

&#x20;   return <UpgradePrompt plan="pro" feature="Video lessons" />;

&#x20; }

&#x20; 

&#x20; // Sequential lock

&#x20; if (module.is\_locked\_until\_prev \&\& !progress.prevModuleCompleted) {

&#x20;   return <LockedModule message="Complete previous module to unlock" />;

&#x20; }

&#x20; 

&#x20; // Render content

&#x20; return module.content\_type === 'video' 

&#x20;   ? <VideoPlayer src={module.video\_url} onProgress={markProgress} />

&#x20;   : <DocViewer src={module.doc\_url} onProgress={markProgress} />;

};

```



\### Certificate Generation (Supabase Edge Function)

```typescript

// /api/certificates/generate

import { createCanvas, loadImage } from 'canvas';

import { GoogleGenerativeAI } from '@google/generative-ai';



export async function generateCertificate(enrollmentId: string) {

&#x20; // 1. Fetch enrollment + user + course + template

&#x20; // 2. Build Gemini prompt for personalized text overlay

&#x20; const genAI = new GoogleGenerativeAI(process.env.GEMINI\_API\_KEY);

&#x20; const model = genAI.getGenerativeModel({ model: "gemini-pro-vision" });

&#x20; 

&#x20; const prompt = `

&#x20;   Generate a professional certificate image with:

&#x20;   - Name: ${user.full\_name}

&#x20;   - Course: ${course.title}

&#x20;   - Date: ${new Date().toLocaleDateString('en-US', { year:'numeric', month:'long', day:'numeric' })}

&#x20;   - Signature: Mostafa Ali, RevOps Consultant

&#x20;   - Style: Corporate, navy blue (#425b76) and orange (#ff7a59) accents

&#x20;   - Include Ops Solutions logo: ${company.logo\_url}

&#x20; `;

&#x20; 

&#x20; // 3. Generate image with Gemini + overlay on template

&#x20; const result = await model.generateContent(\[prompt, template.background\_image\_url]);

&#x20; const imageBuffer = await result.response.image();

&#x20; 

&#x20; // 4. Upload to Supabase Storage

&#x20; const { data } = await supabase.storage

&#x20;   .from('certificates')

&#x20;   .upload(`${company\_id}/${user\_id}/${course\_id}.png`, imageBuffer, { contentType: 'image/png' });

&#x20; 

&#x20; // 5. Create shareable link

&#x20; const shareToken = crypto.randomUUID();

&#x20; await supabase.from('certificates').insert({

&#x20;   enrollment\_id: enrollmentId,

&#x20;   generated\_image\_url: data.path,

&#x20;   share\_token: shareToken

&#x20; });

&#x20; 

&#x20; // 6. Send notifications

&#x20; await sendCompletionNotifications(company\_id, user\_id, course\_id);

&#x20; 

&#x20; return { certificate\_url: data.path, share\_link: `/share/certificate/${shareToken}` };

}

```



\### Certificate Share Page (Public)

```

/share/certificate/\[share\_token]

\- Displays generated certificate image

\- "Download PNG" button

\- "Share on LinkedIn" button (pre-filled post text)

\- No company-sensitive data exposed

\- Rate-limited to prevent abuse

```

\## 📊 Analytics Dashboard: 5-Stage Funnel



\### Stage Breakdown + Metrics

| Stage | Key Metrics | Data Source | Visualization |

|-------|------------|-------------|---------------|

| \*\*1. Visitor\*\* | Sessions, Unique Users, Bounce Rate, Top Pages | HubSpot Traffic Analytics / GA4 embed | Line chart (30/60/90d) + KPI cards |

| \*\*2. Subscriber\*\* | Social followers, Post count, Avg engagement | Social scraper + manual override | Platform cards (LinkedIn/Twitter/IG) |

| \*\*3. Lead\*\* | Form submissions, With/without owner, Source breakdown | HubSpot Forms API + manual CSV upload | Bar chart + donut chart + table |

| \*\*4. MQL\*\* | MQL count, Lead→MQL rate, By source/channel | HubSpot lifecyclestage property + benchmarks | Funnel step + benchmark comparison |

| \*\*5. Pipeline\*\* | SQL→Opp→Customer rates, Avg cycle time, Revenue | HubSpot Deals API + custom properties | Horizontal funnel + revenue projection |



\### Benchmark Overlay Logic

```typescript

// lib/utils/benchmarks.ts

export function getBenchmarkComparison(metrics: FunnelMetrics, industry: string, region: string) {

&#x20; const benchmarks = industry\_benchmarks

&#x20;   .filter(b => b.industry === industry \&\& b.region === region);

&#x20; 

&#x20; return metrics.map(m => ({

&#x20;   ...m,

&#x20;   benchmark\_value: benchmarks.find(b => b.stage === m.stage \&\& b.metric\_key === m.metric\_key)?.value,

&#x20;   variance\_percent: ((m.value - benchmark.value) / benchmark.value \* 100).toFixed(1),

&#x20;   status: m.value >= benchmark.value ? 'above' : 'below'

&#x20; }));

}

```



\### Recommendation Engine (Rule-Based MVP)

```typescript

// lib/utils/recommendations.ts

export function generateRecommendations(metrics: CompanyMetrics, benchmarks: Benchmark\[]) {

&#x20; const recs = \[];

&#x20; 

&#x20; if (metrics.leadToMqlRate < benchmarks.leadToMqlRate \* 0.8) {

&#x20;   recs.push({

&#x20;     area: 'Lead Qualification',

&#x20;     issue: `Lead→MQL rate (${metrics.leadToMqlRate}%) is 20%+ below industry avg (${benchmarks.leadToMqlRate}%)`,

&#x20;     action: 'Review lead scoring criteria; add firmographic filters',

&#x20;     urgency: 'high',

&#x20;     linkedModule: 'lead-scoring-basics' // academy module ID

&#x20;   });

&#x20; }

&#x20; 

&#x20; if (metrics.formsWithoutOwnerPct > 0.3) {

&#x20;   recs.push({

&#x20;     area: 'Lead Routing',

&#x20;     issue: `${Math.round(metrics.formsWithoutOwnerPct\*100)}% of form submissions have no owner`,

&#x20;     action: 'Set up round-robin workflow in HubSpot; assign default owner',

&#x20;     urgency: 'medium',

&#x20;     linkedModule: 'lead-routing-setup'

&#x20;   });

&#x20; }

&#x20; 

&#x20; return recs.sort((a,b) => (a.urgency === 'high' ? -1 : 1));

}

```

\## 🔐 Security \& Compliance Checklist



| Area | Implementation |

|------|---------------|

| \*\*Data Isolation\*\* | RLS on every table with `company\_id`; test with `anon` and `authenticated` roles |

| \*\*Token Security\*\* | HubSpot tokens encrypted via `pgcrypto`; decrypted only in Edge Functions |

| \*\*Auth\*\* | Supabase Auth + JWT; optional SSO for enterprise clients |

| \*\*File Storage\*\* | Supabase Storage with signed URLs; virus scan on upload (ClamAV Edge Function) |

| \*\*Certificate Privacy\*\* | Share links contain only name/course/date; no company data exposed |

| \*\*Audit Logs\*\* | Log all admin actions (token changes, user invites) to `audit\_logs` table |

| \*\*GDPR/CCPA\*\* | Data export/delete endpoints per user; cookie consent banner |

| \*\*Rate Limiting\*\* | HubSpot API calls capped at 100 req/10s per app; scraper calls limited to 1/company/day |

\## 🚀 Ready-to-Code Starter Commands



```bash

\# 1. Initialize Next.js project

npx create-next-app@latest ops-client-os --typescript --tailwind --eslint --app --src-dir=false

cd ops-client-os



\# 2. Install core dependencies

npm install @supabase/supabase-js @supabase/ssr

npm install @radix-ui/react-dialog @radix-ui/react-dropdown-menu

npm install react-hook-form zod @hookform/resolvers

npm install recharts lucide-react clsx tailwind-merge

npm install canvas @google/generative-ai  # for certificates

npm install next-i18next  # for Arabic support



\# 3. Install shadcn/ui

npx shadcn-ui@latest init

npx shadcn-ui@latest add button card dialog dropdown-menu input label table



\# 4. Set up Supabase

npx supabase init

npx supabase link --project-ref your-project-id

npx supabase db push  # apply migrations



\# 5. Add environment variables (.env.local)

NEXT\_PUBLIC\_SUPABASE\_URL=your\_url

NEXT\_PUBLIC\_SUPABASE\_ANON\_KEY=your\_anon\_key

SUPABASE\_SERVICE\_ROLE\_KEY=your\_service\_key

NEXT\_PUBLIC\_LOGO\_DEV\_TOKEN=your\_token

MICROLINK\_API\_KEY=your\_key

GEMINI\_API\_KEY=your\_key

NEXT\_PUBLIC\_APP\_URL=https://app.opsolutionss.com

```

\## 2. Database Schema



\### supabase/migrations/001\_initial\_schema.sql

```sql

\-- Enable UUID extension

CREATE EXTENSION IF NOT EXISTS "uuid-ossp";



\-- Enable pgcrypto for encryption

CREATE EXTENSION IF NOT EXISTS "pgcrypto";



\-- Companies table

CREATE TABLE companies (

&#x20; id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen\_random\_uuid(),

&#x20; name TEXT NOT NULL,

&#x20; website TEXT,

&#x20; domain TEXT UNIQUE,

&#x20; industry TEXT,

&#x20; employee\_count TEXT,

&#x20; country TEXT,

&#x20; region TEXT,

&#x20; logo\_url TEXT,

&#x20; plan TEXT DEFAULT 'basic' CHECK (plan IN ('basic','pro','enterprise')),

&#x20; hubspot\_portal\_id TEXT,

&#x20; hubspot\_access\_token TEXT,

&#x20; hubspot\_refresh\_token TEXT,

&#x20; token\_expires\_at TIMESTAMPTZ,

&#x20; branding\_config JSONB DEFAULT '{"primary":"#425b76","secondary":"#333333","accent":"#ff7a59"}',

&#x20; language TEXT DEFAULT 'en' CHECK (language IN ('en','ar')),

&#x20; created\_by UUID REFERENCES auth.users(id),

&#x20; created\_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT now(),

&#x20; updated\_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT now()

);



\-- Profiles table (extends auth.users)

CREATE TABLE profiles (

&#x20; id UUID PRIMARY KEY REFERENCES auth.users(id),

&#x20; full\_name TEXT NOT NULL,

&#x20; email TEXT UNIQUE NOT NULL,

&#x20; avatar\_url TEXT,

&#x20; role TEXT NOT NULL CHECK (role IN ('superadmin','ops\_employee','client\_admin','client\_manager','client\_employee')),

&#x20; company\_id UUID REFERENCES companies(id),

&#x20; manager\_id UUID REFERENCES profiles(id),

&#x20; hubspot\_user\_id TEXT,

&#x20; is\_active BOOLEAN DEFAULT true,

&#x20; seen\_intro BOOLEAN DEFAULT false,

&#x20; created\_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT now()

);



\-- Funnel metrics

CREATE TABLE funnel\_metrics (

&#x20; id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen\_random\_uuid(),

&#x20; company\_id UUID REFERENCES companies(id),

&#x20; snapshot\_date DATE DEFAULT CURRENT\_DATE,

&#x20; stage TEXT CHECK (stage IN ('visitor','subscriber','lead','mql','sql','opportunity','customer')),

&#x20; count INT DEFAULT 0,

&#x20; conversion\_rate DECIMAL(5,2),

&#x20; avg\_time\_in\_stage\_hours DECIMAL(8,2),

&#x20; source TEXT CHECK (source IN ('hubspot','manual','scraper')),

&#x20; created\_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT now()

);



\-- Form tracking

CREATE TABLE form\_tracking (

&#x20; id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen\_random\_uuid(),

&#x20; company\_id UUID REFERENCES companies(id),

&#x20; form\_name TEXT NOT NULL,

&#x20; form\_type TEXT CHECK (form\_type IN ('lead\_1','lead\_2','subscriber\_1','subscriber\_2','custom')),

&#x20; hubspot\_form\_id TEXT,

&#x20; total\_submissions INT DEFAULT 0,

&#x20; with\_owner INT DEFAULT 0,

&#x20; without\_owner INT DEFAULT 0,

&#x20; offline\_submissions INT DEFAULT 0,

&#x20; source\_breakdown JSONB,

&#x20; last\_synced TIMESTAMPTZ,

&#x20; created\_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT now()

);



\-- Social metrics

CREATE TABLE social\_metrics (

&#x20; id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen\_random\_uuid(),

&#x20; company\_id UUID REFERENCES companies(id),

&#x20; platform TEXT CHECK (platform IN ('linkedin','twitter','instagram','facebook')),

&#x20; profile\_url TEXT,

&#x20; followers\_count INT,

&#x20; posts\_count INT,

&#x20; avg\_engagement\_rate DECIMAL(5,2),

&#x20; last\_scraped TIMESTAMPTZ,

&#x20; scraper\_source TEXT CHECK (scraper\_source IN ('microlink','puppeteer','manual')),

&#x20; created\_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT now()

);



\-- Courses

CREATE TABLE courses (

&#x20; id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen\_random\_uuid(),

&#x20; title TEXT NOT NULL,

&#x20; description TEXT,

&#x20; thumbnail\_url TEXT,

&#x20; order\_index INT DEFAULT 0,

&#x20; plan\_required TEXT DEFAULT 'basic',

&#x20; content\_type TEXT DEFAULT 'both' CHECK (content\_type IN ('doc','video','both')),

&#x20; is\_sequential BOOLEAN DEFAULT true,

&#x20; is\_published BOOLEAN DEFAULT false,

&#x20; created\_by UUID REFERENCES profiles(id),

&#x20; created\_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT now()

);



\-- Course modules

CREATE TABLE course\_modules (

&#x20; id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen\_random\_uuid(),

&#x20; course\_id UUID REFERENCES courses(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,

&#x20; title TEXT NOT NULL,

&#x20; order\_index INT DEFAULT 0,

&#x20; doc\_url TEXT,

&#x20; video\_url TEXT,

&#x20; duration\_mins INT,

&#x20; is\_locked\_until\_prev BOOLEAN DEFAULT true,

&#x20; quiz\_json JSONB,

&#x20; created\_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT now()

);



\-- Course progress

CREATE TABLE course\_progress (

&#x20; id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen\_random\_uuid(),

&#x20; user\_id UUID REFERENCES profiles(id),

&#x20; course\_id UUID REFERENCES courses(id),

&#x20; module\_id UUID REFERENCES course\_modules(id),

&#x20; company\_id UUID REFERENCES companies(id),

&#x20; completed BOOLEAN DEFAULT false,

&#x20; completed\_at TIMESTAMPTZ,

&#x20; time\_spent\_seconds INT DEFAULT 0,

&#x20; UNIQUE(user\_id, module\_id)

);



\-- Certificate templates

CREATE TABLE certificate\_templates (

&#x20; id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen\_random\_uuid(),

&#x20; company\_id UUID REFERENCES companies(id),

&#x20; template\_name TEXT,

&#x20; background\_image\_url TEXT,

&#x20; gemini\_prompt\_template TEXT,

&#x20; fields\_config JSONB DEFAULT '{"first\_name":true,"last\_name":true,"course\_name":true,"date":true,"signature":true}',

&#x20; is\_active BOOLEAN DEFAULT true,

&#x20; created\_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT now()

);



\-- Certificates

CREATE TABLE certificates (

&#x20; id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen\_random\_uuid(),

&#x20; enrollment\_id UUID REFERENCES course\_progress(id),

&#x20; generated\_image\_url TEXT,

&#x20; share\_token TEXT UNIQUE DEFAULT gen\_random\_uuid()::text,

&#x20; shared\_on\_linkedin BOOLEAN DEFAULT false,

&#x20; generated\_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT now()

);



\-- Enhancements (before/after)

CREATE TABLE enhancements (

&#x20; id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen\_random\_uuid(),

&#x20; company\_id UUID REFERENCES companies(id),

&#x20; area TEXT CHECK (area IN ('workflows','pipelines','properties','reports','sequences','custom')),

&#x20; title TEXT NOT NULL,

&#x20; description TEXT,

&#x20; before\_image\_url TEXT,

&#x20; after\_image\_url TEXT,

&#x20; impact\_metric TEXT,

&#x20; visible\_to\_roles TEXT\[] DEFAULT ARRAY\['client\_admin','client\_manager'],

&#x20; created\_by UUID REFERENCES profiles(id),

&#x20; created\_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT now()

);



\-- HubSpot audits

CREATE TABLE hubspot\_audits (

&#x20; id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen\_random\_uuid(),

&#x20; company\_id UUID REFERENCES companies(id),

&#x20; audited\_by UUID REFERENCES profiles(id),

&#x20; audit\_date TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT now(),

&#x20; findings JSONB,

&#x20; recommendations JSONB,

&#x20; status TEXT DEFAULT 'draft' CHECK (status IN ('draft','published','archived'))

);



\-- Updates

CREATE TABLE updates (

&#x20; id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen\_random\_uuid(),

&#x20; company\_id UUID REFERENCES companies(id),

&#x20; title TEXT NOT NULL,

&#x20; content TEXT,

&#x20; category TEXT CHECK (category IN ('hubspot','process','training','general')),

&#x20; visibility TEXT\[] DEFAULT ARRAY\['client\_admin'],

&#x20; visible\_to\_users UUID\[],

&#x20; before\_image\_url TEXT,

&#x20; after\_image\_url TEXT,

&#x20; created\_by UUID REFERENCES profiles(id),

&#x20; created\_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT now()

);



\-- Comments

CREATE TABLE comments (

&#x20; id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen\_random\_uuid(),

&#x20; update\_id UUID REFERENCES updates(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,

&#x20; user\_id UUID REFERENCES profiles(id),

&#x20; content TEXT NOT NULL,

&#x20; is\_internal BOOLEAN DEFAULT false,

&#x20; created\_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT now()

);



\-- Lifecycle guidance (for HubSpot UI Extension)

CREATE TABLE lifecycle\_guidance (

&#x20; id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen\_random\_uuid(),

&#x20; stage TEXT NOT NULL CHECK (stage IN ('visitor','subscriber','lead','mql','sql','opportunity','customer')),

&#x20; title TEXT NOT NULL,

&#x20; description TEXT,

&#x20; action\_label TEXT,

&#x20; action\_type TEXT CHECK (action\_type IN ('tip','task','sequence','alert','academy\_link')),

&#x20; academy\_module\_id UUID REFERENCES course\_modules(id),

&#x20; order\_index INT DEFAULT 0,

&#x20; plan\_required TEXT DEFAULT 'basic',

&#x20; is\_active BOOLEAN DEFAULT true,

&#x20; created\_by UUID REFERENCES profiles(id),

&#x20; created\_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT now()

);



\-- Guidance completions

CREATE TABLE guidance\_completions (

&#x20; id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen\_random\_uuid(),

&#x20; hubspot\_user\_id TEXT NOT NULL,

&#x20; hubspot\_record\_id TEXT NOT NULL,

&#x20; guidance\_id UUID REFERENCES lifecycle\_guidance(id),

&#x20; company\_id UUID REFERENCES companies(id),

&#x20; completed\_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT now(),

&#x20; UNIQUE(hubspot\_user\_id, hubspot\_record\_id, guidance\_id)

);



\-- HubSpot app installs

CREATE TABLE hubspot\_app\_installs (

&#x20; id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen\_random\_uuid(),

&#x20; company\_id UUID REFERENCES companies(id),

&#x20; hubspot\_portal\_id TEXT UNIQUE NOT NULL,

&#x20; access\_token TEXT,

&#x20; refresh\_token TEXT,

&#x20; token\_expires\_at TIMESTAMPTZ,

&#x20; installed\_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT now(),

&#x20; is\_active BOOLEAN DEFAULT true

);



\-- Industry benchmarks

CREATE TABLE industry\_benchmarks (

&#x20; id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen\_random\_uuid(),

&#x20; industry TEXT,

&#x20; region TEXT,

&#x20; stage TEXT,

&#x20; metric\_key TEXT,

&#x20; benchmark\_value NUMERIC,

&#x20; source TEXT,

&#x20; updated\_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT now()

);



\-- Enable Row Level Security

ALTER TABLE companies ENABLE ROW LEVEL SECURITY;

ALTER TABLE profiles ENABLE ROW LEVEL SECURITY;

ALTER TABLE funnel\_metrics ENABLE ROW LEVEL SECURITY;

ALTER TABLE form\_tracking ENABLE ROW LEVEL SECURITY;

ALTER TABLE social\_metrics ENABLE ROW LEVEL SECURITY;

ALTER TABLE courses ENABLE ROW LEVEL SECURITY;

ALTER TABLE course\_modules ENABLE ROW LEVEL SECURITY;

ALTER TABLE course\_progress ENABLE ROW LEVEL SECURITY;

ALTER TABLE certificates ENABLE ROW LEVEL SECURITY;

ALTER TABLE enhancements ENABLE ROW LEVEL SECURITY;

ALTER TABLE updates ENABLE ROW LEVEL SECURITY;

ALTER TABLE comments ENABLE ROW LEVEL SECURITY;



\-- RLS Policies



\-- Companies: Users can only see their own company or all if they're ops

CREATE POLICY company\_isolation ON companies

&#x20; FOR SELECT

&#x20; USING (

&#x20;   id IN (SELECT company\_id FROM profiles WHERE id = auth.uid())

&#x20;   OR EXISTS (

&#x20;     SELECT 1 FROM profiles 

&#x20;     WHERE id = auth.uid() 

&#x20;     AND role IN ('superadmin','ops\_employee')

&#x20;   )

&#x20; );



CREATE POLICY company\_insert\_ops ON companies

&#x20; FOR INSERT

&#x20; WITH CHECK (

&#x20;   EXISTS (

&#x20;     SELECT 1 FROM profiles 

&#x20;     WHERE id = auth.uid() 

&#x20;     AND role IN ('superadmin','ops\_employee')

&#x20;   )

&#x20; );



CREATE POLICY company\_update\_ops ON companies

&#x20; FOR UPDATE

&#x20; USING (

&#x20;   EXISTS (

&#x20;     SELECT 1 FROM profiles 

&#x20;     WHERE id = auth.uid() 

&#x20;     AND role IN ('superadmin','ops\_employee')

&#x20;   )

&#x20; );



\-- Profiles: Users can see teammates in their company

CREATE POLICY profiles\_isolation ON profiles

&#x20; FOR SELECT

&#x20; USING (

&#x20;   company\_id IN (

&#x20;     SELECT company\_id FROM profiles WHERE id = auth.uid()

&#x20;   )

&#x20;   OR EXISTS (

&#x20;     SELECT 1 FROM profiles 

&#x20;     WHERE id = auth.uid() 

&#x20;     AND role IN ('superadmin','ops\_employee')

&#x20;   )

&#x20; );



\-- Updates: Filtered by visibility and company

CREATE POLICY updates\_isolation ON updates

&#x20; FOR SELECT

&#x20; USING (

&#x20;   company\_id IN (

&#x20;     SELECT company\_id FROM profiles WHERE id = auth.uid()

&#x20;   )

&#x20;   AND (

&#x20;     role = ANY(visibility)

&#x20;     OR auth.uid() = ANY(visible\_to\_users)

&#x20;     OR EXISTS (

&#x20;       SELECT 1 FROM profiles 

&#x20;       WHERE id = auth.uid() 

&#x20;       AND role IN ('superadmin','ops\_employee')

&#x20;     )

&#x20;   )

&#x20; );



\-- Enhancements: Based on roles

CREATE POLICY enhancements\_isolation ON enhancements

&#x20; FOR SELECT

&#x20; USING (

&#x20;   company\_id IN (

&#x20;     SELECT company\_id FROM profiles WHERE id = auth.uid()

&#x20;   )

&#x20;   AND (

&#x20;     role = ANY(visible\_to\_roles)

&#x20;     OR EXISTS (

&#x20;       SELECT 1 FROM profiles 

&#x20;       WHERE id = auth.uid() 

&#x20;       AND role IN ('superadmin','ops\_employee')

&#x20;     )

&#x20;   )

&#x20; );



\-- Course progress: Users can only see their own progress

CREATE POLICY course\_progress\_isolation ON course\_progress

&#x20; FOR SELECT

&#x20; USING (

&#x20;   user\_id = auth.uid()

&#x20;   OR EXISTS (

&#x20;     SELECT 1 FROM profiles 

&#x20;     WHERE id = auth.uid() 

&#x20;     AND role IN ('superadmin','ops\_employee','client\_admin','client\_manager')

&#x20;     AND company\_id = course\_progress.company\_id

&#x20;   )

&#x20; );



\-- Create indexes for performance

CREATE INDEX idx\_companies\_domain ON companies(domain);

CREATE INDEX idx\_profiles\_company\_id ON profiles(company\_id);

CREATE INDEX idx\_profiles\_role ON profiles(role);

CREATE INDEX idx\_funnel\_metrics\_company\_date ON funnel\_metrics(company\_id, snapshot\_date);

CREATE INDEX idx\_form\_tracking\_company ON form\_tracking(company\_id);

CREATE INDEX idx\_social\_metrics\_company ON social\_metrics(company\_id);

CREATE INDEX idx\_course\_progress\_user ON course\_progress(user\_id);

CREATE INDEX idx\_updates\_company ON updates(company\_id);

CREATE INDEX idx\_enhancements\_company ON enhancements(company\_id);

CREATE INDEX idx\_guidance\_stage ON lifecycle\_guidance(stage);



\-- Create updated\_at trigger

CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION update\_updated\_at\_column()

RETURNS TRIGGER AS $$

BEGIN

&#x20; NEW.updated\_at = now();

&#x20; RETURN NEW;

END;

$$ LANGUAGE plpgsql;



CREATE TRIGGER update\_companies\_updated\_at

&#x20; BEFORE UPDATE ON companies

&#x20; FOR EACH ROW

&#x20; EXECUTE FUNCTION update\_updated\_at\_column();

```

```typescript
import { createBrowserClient } from '@supabase/ssr';

import { Database } from '@/types/supabase';



export function createClient() {

&#x20; return createBrowserClient<Database>(

&#x20;   process.env.NEXT\_PUBLIC\_SUPABASE\_URL!,

&#x20;   process.env.NEXT\_PUBLIC\_SUPABASE\_ANON\_KEY!

&#x20; );

}
```

\### lib/supabase/server.ts

```typescript

import { createServerClient } from '@supabase/ssr';

import { cookies } from 'next/headers';

import { Database } from '@/types/supabase';



export function createClient() {

&#x20; const cookieStore = cookies();



&#x20; return createServerClient<Database>(

&#x20;   process.env.NEXT\_PUBLIC\_SUPABASE\_URL!,

&#x20;   process.env.NEXT\_PUBLIC\_SUPABASE\_ANON\_KEY!,

&#x20;   {

&#x20;     cookies: {

&#x20;       getAll() {

&#x20;         return cookieStore.getAll();

&#x20;       },

&#x20;       setAll(cookiesToSet) {

&#x20;         try {

&#x20;           cookiesToSet.forEach(({ name, value, options }) =>

&#x20;             cookieStore.set(name, value, options)

&#x20;           );

&#x20;         } catch {

&#x20;           // The `setAll` method was called from a Server Component.

&#x20;           // This can be ignored if you have middleware refreshing

&#x20;           // user sessions.

&#x20;         }

&#x20;       },

&#x20;     },

&#x20;   }

&#x20; );

}

```



\### lib/hubspot/client.ts

```typescript

import { Client } from '@hubspot/api-client';

import { createClient as createSupabaseClient } from '@/lib/supabase/server';



export async function getHubSpotClient(companyId: string) {

&#x20; const supabase = createSupabaseClient();

&#x20; 

&#x20; const { data: company } = await supabase

&#x20;   .from('companies')

&#x20;   .select('hubspot\_access\_token')

&#x20;   .eq('id', companyId)

&#x20;   .single();



&#x20; if (!company?.hubspot\_access\_token) {

&#x20;   throw new Error('HubSpot token not found');

&#x20; }



&#x20; return new Client({

&#x20;   accessToken: company.hubspot\_access\_token,

&#x20; });

}



export async function refreshHubSpotToken(companyId: string) {

&#x20; const supabase = createSupabaseClient();

&#x20; 

&#x20; const { data: company } = await supabase

&#x20;   .from('companies')

&#x20;   .select('hubspot\_refresh\_token, hubspot\_portal\_id')

&#x20;   .eq('id', companyId)

&#x20;   .single();



&#x20; if (!company?.hubspot\_refresh\_token) {

&#x20;   throw new Error('Refresh token not found');

&#x20; }



&#x20; // Exchange refresh token for new access token

&#x20; const response = await fetch('https://api.hubapi.com/oauth/v1/token', {

&#x20;   method: 'POST',

&#x20;   headers: {

&#x20;     'Content-Type': 'application/x-www-form-urlencoded',

&#x20;   },

&#x20;   body: new URLSearchParams({

&#x20;     grant\_type: 'refresh\_token',

&#x20;     client\_id: process.env.HUBSPOT\_CLIENT\_ID!,

&#x20;     client\_secret: process.env.HUBSPOT\_CLIENT\_SECRET!,

&#x20;     refresh\_token: company.hubspot\_refresh\_token,

&#x20;   }),

&#x20; });



&#x20; const data = await response.json();



&#x20; if (data.access\_token) {

&#x20;   await supabase

&#x20;     .from('companies')

&#x20;     .update({

&#x20;       hubspot\_access\_token: data.access\_token,

&#x20;       token\_expires\_at: new Date(Date.now() + data.expires\_in \* 1000),

&#x20;     })

&#x20;     .eq('id', companyId);



&#x20;   return data.access\_token;

&#x20; }



&#x20; throw new Error('Failed to refresh token');

}

```



\### lib/scrapers/socialScraper.ts

```typescript

export async function scrapeSocialProfile(platform: string, handle: string) {

&#x20; const apiKey = process.env.MICROLINK\_API\_KEY;

&#x20; 

&#x20; try {

&#x20;   const url = `https://api.microlink.io?url=https://${platform}.com/${handle}`;

&#x20;   const response = await fetch(url, {

&#x20;     headers: {

&#x20;       'x-api-key': apiKey || '',

&#x20;     },

&#x20;   });



&#x20;   const data = await response.json();



&#x20;   return {

&#x20;     followers: data.data.social?.followers || null,

&#x20;     posts: data.data.social?.posts || null,

&#x20;     engagement: data.data.social?.engagement\_rate || null,

&#x20;   };

&#x20; } catch (error) {

&#x20;   console.error(`Error scraping ${platform}:`, error);

&#x20;   return null;

&#x20; }

}

&#x20; // This would be implemented as a Supabase Edge Function with Puppeteer

&#x20; // For now, return null and rely on manual entry or Microlink

&#x20; return null;

}
```

\### lib/scrapers/logoFetcher.ts

```typescript

export async function fetchCompanyLogo(domain: string): Promise<string | null> {

&#x20; const strategies = \[

&#x20;   () => `https://img.logo.dev/${domain}?token=${process.env.NEXT\_PUBLIC\_LOGO\_DEV\_TOKEN}\&size=128`,

&#x20;   () => `https://logo.clearbit.com/${domain}`,

&#x20;   () => `https://www.google.com/s2/favicons?domain=${domain}\&sz=128`,

&#x20; ];



&#x20; for (const getUrl of strategies) {

&#x20;   const url = getUrl();

&#x20;   try {

&#x20;     const response = await fetch(url, { method: 'HEAD' });

&#x20;     if (response.ok) {

&#x20;       return url;

&#x20;     }

&#x20;   } catch {

&#x20;     continue;

&#x20;   }

&#x20; }



&#x20; return null;

}

```



\### lib/certificates/generateCertificate.ts

```typescript

import { createCanvas, loadImage } from 'canvas';

import { GoogleGenerativeAI } from '@google/generative-ai';



interface CertificateData {

&#x20; firstName: string;

&#x20; lastName: string;

&#x20; courseName: string;

&#x20; completionDate: string;

&#x20; templateUrl: string;

&#x20; signatureUrl?: string;

&#x20; logoUrl?: string;

}



export async function generateCertificate(data: CertificateData): Promise<Buffer> {

&#x20; const canvas = createCanvas(1200, 850);

&#x20; const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');



&#x20; // Load template background

&#x20; const template = await loadImage(data.templateUrl);

&#x20; ctx.drawImage(template, 0, 0, 1200, 850);



&#x20; // Set fonts and colors

&#x20; ctx.font = 'bold 52px Sora';

&#x20; ctx.fillStyle = '#425b76';

&#x20; ctx.textAlign = 'center';



&#x20; // Inject name

&#x20; ctx.fillText(`${data.firstName} ${data.lastName}`, 600, 420);



&#x20; // Inject course name

&#x20; ctx.font = '28px DM Sans';

&#x20; ctx.fillStyle = '#333333';

&#x20; ctx.fillText(data.courseName, 600, 490);



&#x20; // Inject date

&#x20; ctx.font = '22px DM Sans';

&#x20; ctx.fillStyle = '#8a9bb0';

&#x20; ctx.fillText(data.completionDate, 600, 540);



&#x20; // Load and draw signature if provided

&#x20; if (data.signatureUrl) {

&#x20;   const signature = await loadImage(data.signatureUrl);

&#x20;   ctx.drawImage(signature, 500, 650, 200, 80);

&#x20; }



&#x20; // Load and draw logo if provided

&#x20; if (data.logoUrl) {

&#x20;   const logo = await loadImage(data.logoUrl);

&#x20;   ctx.drawImage(logo, 50, 50, 150, 50);

&#x20; }



&#x20; return canvas.toBuffer('image/png');

}



export async function generateCertificateWithGemini(data: CertificateData): Promise<Buffer> {

&#x20; const genAI = new GoogleGenerativeAI(process.env.GEMINI\_API\_KEY!);

&#x20; const model = genAI.getGenerativeModel({ model: 'gemini-pro-vision' });



&#x20; const prompt = `

&#x20;   Generate a professional certificate design with:

&#x20;   - Recipient Name: ${data.firstName} ${data.lastName}

&#x20;   - Course: ${data.courseName}

&#x20;   - Completion Date: ${data.completionDate}

&#x20;   - Issued by: Mostafa Ali - RevOps Consultant

&#x20;   - Style: Corporate, professional

&#x20;   - Colors: Navy blue (#425b76) and orange (#ff7a59) accents

&#x20;   - Include space for signature and logo

&#x20; `;



&#x20; // Note: Gemini image generation is still in development

&#x20; // For now, use the canvas approach above

&#x20; return generateCertificate(data);

}

```



\### lib/utils/roleHelpers.ts

```typescript

export type UserRole = 'superadmin' | 'ops\_employee' | 'client\_admin' | 'client\_manager' | 'client\_employee';



export const roleHierarchy: Record<UserRole, number> = {

&#x20; superadmin: 5,

&#x20; ops\_employee: 4,

&#x20; client\_admin: 3,

&#x20; client\_manager: 2,

&#x20; client\_employee: 1,

};



export function canInvite(inviterRole: UserRole, inviteeRole: UserRole): boolean {

&#x20; return roleHierarchy\[inviterRole] > roleHierarchy\[inviteeRole];

}



export function canViewAnalytics(viewerRole: UserRole, targetRole?: UserRole): boolean {

&#x20; if (viewerRole === 'superadmin' || viewerRole === 'ops\_employee') return true;

&#x20; if (viewerRole === 'client\_admin') return true;

&#x20; if (viewerRole === 'client\_manager' \&\& targetRole === 'client\_employee') return true;

&#x20; return false;

}



export function getPlanFeatures(plan: 'basic' | 'pro' | 'enterprise') {

&#x20; const features = {

&#x20;   basic: {

&#x20;     guidanceSteps: 1,

&#x20;     contentTypes: \['doc'],

&#x20;     analytics: 'basic',

&#x20;   },

&#x20;   pro: {

&#x20;     guidanceSteps: 5,

&#x20;     contentTypes: \['doc', 'video'],

&#x20;     analytics: 'advanced',

&#x20;   },

&#x20;   enterprise: {

&#x20;     guidanceSteps: 999,

&#x20;     contentTypes: \['doc', 'video'],

&#x20;     analytics: 'full',

&#x20;   },

&#x20; };



&#x20; return features\[plan];

}

```



\### lib/utils/benchmarks.ts

```typescript

export interface CompanyMetrics {

&#x20; leadToMqlRate: number;

&#x20; mqlToSqlRate: number;

&#x20; sqlToOppRate: number;

&#x20; oppToCustomerRate: number;

&#x20; formsWithoutOwnerPct: number;

}



export interface Benchmark {

&#x20; industry: string;

&#x20; region: string;

&#x20; stage: string;

&#x20; metric\_key: string;

&#x20; benchmark\_value: number;

}



export function getBenchmarkComparison(

&#x20; metrics: CompanyMetrics,

&#x20; benchmarks: Benchmark\[],

&#x20; industry: string,

&#x20; region: string

) {

&#x20; const industryBenchmarks = benchmarks.filter(

&#x20;   (b) => b.industry === industry \&\& b.region === region

&#x20; );



&#x20; return {

&#x20;   leadToMql: {

&#x20;     value: metrics.leadToMqlRate,

&#x20;     benchmark: industryBenchmarks.find((b) => b.stage === 'lead' \&\& b.metric\_key === 'conversion\_rate')?.benchmark\_value || 0,

&#x20;   },

&#x20;   mqlToSql: {

&#x20;     value: metrics.mqlToSqlRate,

&#x20;     benchmark: industryBenchmarks.find((b) => b.stage === 'mql' \&\& b.metric\_key === 'conversion\_rate')?.benchmark\_value || 0,

&#x20;   },

&#x20; };

}



export function generateRecommendations(metrics: CompanyMetrics, benchmarks: Benchmark\[]) {

&#x20; const recommendations = \[];



&#x20; if (metrics.leadToMqlRate < 15) {

&#x20;   recommendations.push({

&#x20;     area: 'Lead Qualification',

&#x20;     issue: `Lead→MQL rate (${metrics.leadToMqlRate}%) is below industry average`,

&#x20;     action: 'Review lead scoring criteria; add firmographic filters',

&#x20;     urgency: 'high' as const,

&#x20;   });

&#x20; }



&#x20; if (metrics.formsWithoutOwnerPct > 0.3) {

&#x20;   recommendations.push({

&#x20;     area: 'Lead Routing',

&#x20;     issue: `${Math.round(metrics.formsWithoutOwnerPct \* 100)}% of form submissions have no owner`,

&#x20;     action: 'Set up round-robin workflow in HubSpot; assign default owner',

&#x20;     urgency: 'medium' as const,

&#x20;   });

&#x20; }



&#x20; if (metrics.mqlToSqlRate < 20) {

&#x20;   recommendations.push({

&#x20;     area: 'Sales Engagement',

&#x20;     issue: `MQL→SQL rate (${metrics.mqlToSqlRate}%) needs improvement`,

&#x20;     action: 'Implement faster follow-up sequences; improve sales enablement',

&#x20;     urgency: 'high' as const,

&#x20;   });

&#x20; }



&#x20; return recommendations.sort((a, b) => (a.urgency === 'high' ? -1 : 1));

}

```

```typescript

export type UserRole = 'superadmin' | 'ops\_employee' | 'client\_admin' | 'client\_manager' | 'client\_employee';

export interface Company {

&#x20; id: string;

&#x20; website?: string;

}
```
