\## 5. API Routes



\### app/api/hubspot/oauth/install/route.ts

```typescript

import { NextResponse } from 'next/server';



export async function GET() {

&#x20; const clientId = process.env.HUBSPOT\_CLIENT\_ID;

&#x20; const redirectUri = `${process.env.NEXT\_PUBLIC\_APP\_URL}/api/hubspot/oauth/callback`;

&#x20; const scopes = \[

&#x20;   'crm.objects.contacts.read',

&#x20;   'crm.objects.deals.read',

&#x20;   'crm.objects.companies.read',

&#x20;   'crm.objects.owners.read',

&#x20;   'marketing.forms.read',

&#x20;   'analytics',

&#x20; ].join(' ');



&#x20; const authUrl = `https://app.hubspot.com/oauth/authorize?client\_id=${clientId}\&redirect\_uri=${encodeURIComponent(redirectUri)}\&scope=${encodeURIComponent(scopes)}`;



&#x20; return NextResponse.redirect(authUrl);

}

```



\### app/api/hubspot/oauth/callback/route.ts

```typescript

import { NextRequest, NextResponse } from 'next/server';

import { createClient } from '@/lib/supabase/server';



export async function GET(request: NextRequest) {

&#x20; const searchParams = request.nextUrl.searchParams;

&#x20; const code = searchParams.get('code');



&#x20; if (!code) {

&#x20;   return NextResponse.json({ error: 'No code provided' }, { status: 400 });

&#x20; }



&#x20; try {

&#x20;   const response = await fetch('https://api.hubapi.com/oauth/v1/token', {

&#x20;     method: 'POST',

&#x20;     headers: {

&#x20;       'Content-Type': 'application/x-www-form-urlencoded',

&#x20;     },

&#x20;     body: new URLSearchParams({

&#x20;       grant\_type: 'authorization\_code',

&#x20;       client\_id: process.env.HUBSPOT\_CLIENT\_ID!,

&#x20;       client\_secret: process.env.HUBSPOT\_CLIENT\_SECRET!,

&#x20;       code: code,

&#x20;       redirect\_uri: `${process.env.NEXT\_PUBLIC\_APP\_URL}/api/hubspot/oauth/callback`,

&#x20;     }),

&#x20;   });



&#x20;   const data = await response.json();



&#x20;   if (data.access\_token) {

&#x20;     const supabase = createClient();



&#x20;     // Get portal info to match with company

&#x20;     const hubspotClient = new (await import('@hubspot/api-client')).Client({

&#x20;       accessToken: data.access\_token,

&#x20;     });



&#x20;     const portalInfo = await hubspotClient.oauth.accessTokensApi.getAccessToken(data.access\_token);

&#x20;     const portalId = portalInfo.hubId.toString();



&#x20;     // Find or update company

&#x20;     const {  company } = await supabase

&#x20;       .from('companies')

&#x20;       .select('id')

&#x20;       .eq('hubspot\_portal\_id', portalId)

&#x20;       .single();



&#x20;     if (company) {

&#x20;       await supabase

&#x20;         .from('companies')

&#x20;         .update({

&#x20;           hubspot\_access\_token: data.access\_token,

&#x20;           hubspot\_refresh\_token: data.refresh\_token,

&#x20;           token\_expires\_at: new Date(Date.now() + data.expires\_in \* 1000),

&#x20;         })

&#x20;         .eq('id', company.id);



&#x20;       await supabase.from('hubspot\_app\_installs').upsert({

&#x20;         company\_id: company.id,

&#x20;         hubspot\_portal\_id: portalId,

&#x20;         access\_token: data.access\_token,

&#x20;         refresh\_token: data.refresh\_token,

&#x20;         token\_expires\_at: new Date(Date.now() + data.expires\_in \* 1000),

&#x20;       });

&#x20;     }



&#x20;     return NextResponse.redirect(`${process.env.NEXT\_PUBLIC\_APP\_URL}/ops/companies?success=true`);

&#x20;   }



&#x20;   return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Failed to get access token' }, { status: 400 });

&#x20; } catch (error) {

&#x20;   console.error('OAuth callback error:', error);

&#x20;   return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Internal server error' }, { status: 500 });

&#x20; }

}

```



\### app/api/hubspot/guidance/route.ts

```typescript

import { NextRequest, NextResponse } from 'next/server';

import { createClient } from '@/lib/supabase/server';



export async function GET(request: NextRequest) {

&#x20; const searchParams = request.nextUrl.searchParams;

&#x20; const portalId = searchParams.get('portalId');

&#x20; const stage = searchParams.get('lifecycleStage');

&#x20; const hubspotUserId = searchParams.get('userId');



&#x20; if (!portalId || !stage) {

&#x20;   return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Missing required parameters' }, { status: 400 });

&#x20; }



&#x20; try {

&#x20;   const supabase = createClient();



&#x20;   // Find company by portal ID

&#x20;   const {  install } = await supabase

&#x20;     .from('hubspot\_app\_installs')

&#x20;     .select('company\_id')

&#x20;     .eq('hubspot\_portal\_id', portalId)

&#x20;     .single();



&#x20;   if (!install) {

&#x20;     return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Company not found' }, { status: 404 });

&#x20;   }



&#x20;   // Get company plan

&#x20;   const {  company } = await supabase

&#x20;     .from('companies')

&#x20;     .select('plan')

&#x20;     .eq('id', install.company\_id)

&#x20;     .single();



&#x20;   // Get guidance steps for this stage

&#x20;   const {  guidanceSteps } = await supabase

&#x20;     .from('lifecycle\_guidance')

&#x20;     .select('\*')

&#x20;     .eq('stage', stage)

&#x20;     .eq('is\_active', true)

&#x20;     .order('order\_index', { ascending: true });



&#x20;   // Get completed steps for this user

&#x20;   const { data: completions } = await supabase

&#x20;     .from('guidance\_completions')

&#x20;     .select('guidance\_id')

&#x20;     .eq('hubspot\_user\_id', hubspotUserId || '')

&#x20;     .eq('hubspot\_record\_id', searchParams.get('recordId') || '');



&#x20;   const completedIds = completions?.map((c) => c.guidance\_id) || \[];



&#x20;   return NextResponse.json({

&#x20;     steps: guidanceSteps || \[],

&#x20;     companyPlan: company?.plan || 'basic',

&#x20;     completedIds,

&#x20;   });

&#x20; } catch (error) {

&#x20;   console.error('Guidance API error:', error);

&#x20;   return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Internal server error' }, { status: 500 });

&#x20; }

}

```



\### app/api/hubspot/complete/route.ts

```typescript

import { NextRequest, NextResponse } from 'next/server';

import { createClient } from '@/lib/supabase/server';



export async function POST(request: NextRequest) {

&#x20; try {

&#x20;   const body = await request.json();

&#x20;   const { hubspotUserId, hubspotRecordId, guidanceId, companyId } = body;



&#x20;   const supabase = createClient();



&#x20;   // Record completion

&#x20;   await supabase.from('guidance\_completions').upsert({

&#x20;     hubspot\_user\_id: hubspotUserId,

&#x20;     hubspot\_record\_id: hubspotRecordId,

&#x20;     guidance\_id: guidanceId,

&#x20;     company\_id: companyId,

&#x20;     completed\_at: new Date().toISOString(),

&#x20;   });



&#x20;   return NextResponse.json({ success: true });

&#x20; } catch (error) {

&#x20;   console.error('Complete guidance error:', error);

&#x20;   return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Internal server error' }, { status: 500 });

&#x20; }

}

```



\### app/api/certificates/generate/route.ts

```typescript

import { NextRequest, NextResponse } from 'next/server';

import { createClient } from '@/lib/supabase/server';

import { generateCertificate } from '@/lib/certificates/generateCertificate';



export async function POST(request: NextRequest) {

&#x20; try {

&#x20;   const { enrollmentId } = await request.json();



&#x20;   const supabase = createClient();



&#x20;   // Get enrollment details

&#x20;   const { data: enrollment } = await supabase

&#x20;     .from('course\_progress')

&#x20;     .select(`

&#x20;       user\_id,

&#x20;       course\_id,

&#x20;       company\_id,

&#x20;       profiles:users!inner(full\_name, email),

&#x20;       courses!inner(title)

&#x20;     `)

&#x20;     .eq('id', enrollmentId)

&#x20;     .single();



&#x20;   if (!enrollment) {

&#x20;     return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Enrollment not found' }, { status: 404 });

&#x20;   }



&#x20;   // Get company details

&#x20;   const {  company } = await supabase

&#x20;     .from('companies')

&#x20;     .select('logo\_url')

&#x20;     .eq('id', enrollment.company\_id)

&#x20;     .single();



&#x20;   // Get certificate template

&#x20;   const {  template } = await supabase

&#x20;     .from('certificate\_templates')

&#x20;     .select('\*')

&#x20;     .eq('company\_id', enrollment.company\_id)

&#x20;     .eq('is\_active', true)

&#x20;     .single();



&#x20;   // Generate certificate

&#x20;   const \[firstName, ...lastNameParts] = enrollment.profiles.full\_name.split(' ');

&#x20;   const certificateBuffer = await generateCertificate({

&#x20;     firstName,

&#x20;     lastName: lastNameParts.join(' '),

&#x20;     courseName: enrollment.courses.title,

&#x20;     completionDate: new Date().toLocaleDateString('en-US', {

&#x20;       year: 'numeric',

&#x20;       month: 'long',

&#x20;       day: 'numeric',

&#x20;     }),

&#x20;     templateUrl: template?.background\_image\_url || '/certificates/default-bg.png',

&#x20;     logoUrl: company?.logo\_url,

&#x20;   });



&#x20;   // Upload to Supabase Storage

&#x20;   const fileName = `${enrollment.company\_id}/${enrollment.user\_id}/${enrollment.course\_id}.png`;

&#x20;   const {  uploadData, error: uploadError } = await supabase.storage

&#x20;     .from('certificates')

&#x20;     .upload(fileName, certificateBuffer, {

&#x20;       contentType: 'image/png',

&#x20;       upsert: true,

&#x20;     });



&#x20;   if (uploadError) {

&#x20;     throw uploadError;

&#x20;   }



&#x20;   // Get public URL

&#x20;   const { data: urlData } = supabase.storage

&#x20;     .from('certificates')

&#x20;     .getPublicUrl(fileName);



&#x20;   // Create certificate record

&#x20;   const {  certificate } = await supabase

&#x20;     .from('certificates')

&#x20;     .insert({

&#x20;       enrollment\_id: enrollmentId,

&#x20;       generated\_image\_url: urlData.publicUrl,

&#x20;     })

&#x20;     .select()

&#x20;     .single();



&#x20;   return NextResponse.json({

&#x20;     certificate\_url: urlData.publicUrl,

&#x20;     share\_link: `/share/certificate/${certificate.share\_token}`,

&#x20;   });

&#x20; } catch (error) {

&#x20;   console.error('Certificate generation error:', error);

&#x20;   return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Internal server error' }, { status: 500 });

&#x20; }

}

```



\### app/api/social/scrape/route.ts

```typescript

import { NextRequest, NextResponse } from 'next/server';

import { scrapeSocialProfile } from '@/lib/scrapers/socialScraper';

import { createClient } from '@/lib/supabase/server';



export async function POST(request: NextRequest) {

&#x20; try {

&#x20;   const { companyId, platform, handle } = await request.json();



&#x20;   const metrics = await scrapeSocialProfile(platform, handle);



&#x20;   if (metrics) {

&#x20;     const supabase = createClient();



&#x20;     await supabase.from('social\_metrics').upsert({

&#x20;       company\_id: companyId,

&#x20;       platform,

&#x20;       followers\_count: metrics.followers,

&#x20;       posts\_count: metrics.posts,

&#x20;       avg\_engagement\_rate: metrics.engagement,

&#x20;       last\_scraped: new Date().toISOString(),

&#x20;       scraper\_source: 'microlink',

&#x20;     });



&#x20;     return NextResponse.json({ success: true, metrics });

&#x20;   }



&#x20;   return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Failed to scrape social profile' }, { status: 400 });

&#x20; } catch (error) {

&#x20;   console.error('Social scrape error:', error);

&#x20;   return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Internal server error' }, { status: 500 });

&#x20; }

}

```

'use client';



import Link from 'next/link';

import { 

&#x20; Home,

&#x20; ChevronRight

import { cn } from '@/lib/utils/cn';

import { UserRole } from '@/types';



interface SidebarProps {

&#x20; role: UserRole;

&#x20; companyId?: string;

}



const menuItems = {

&#x20; superadmin: \[

&#x20;   { icon: Home, label: 'Dashboard', href: '/' },

&#x20;   { icon: Building2, label: 'Companies', href: '/ops/companies' },

&#x20;   { icon: Users, label: 'Employees', href: '/ops/employees' },

&#x20;   { icon: MessageSquare, label: 'Updates', href: '/ops/updates' },

&#x20;   { icon: Building2, label: 'Companies', href: '/ops/companies' },

&#x20;   { icon: MessageSquare, label: 'Updates', href: '/ops/updates' },

&#x20;   { icon: GraduationCap, label: 'Academy', href: '/ops/academy' },

&#x20;   { icon: Award, label: 'Enhancements', href: '/client/\[companyId]/enhancements' },

&#x20;   { icon: GraduationCap, label: 'Academy', href: '/client/\[companyId]/academy' },

&#x20;   { icon: Users, label: 'Team', href: '/client/\[companyId]/team' },

&#x20; ],

&#x20; client\_manager: \[

&#x20;   { icon: BarChart3, label: 'Analytics', href: '/client/\[companyId]/analytics' },

&#x20;   { icon: FileText, label: 'Updates', href: '/client/\[companyId]/updates' },

&#x20;   { icon: GraduationCap, label: 'Academy', href: '/client/\[companyId]/academy' },

&#x20;   { icon: Users, label: 'My Team', href: '/client/\[companyId]/team' },

&#x20; ],

&#x20; client\_employee: \[

&#x20;   { icon: FileText, label: 'Updates', href: '/client/\[companyId]/updates' },

&#x20;   { icon: GraduationCap, label: 'Academy', href: '/client/\[companyId]/academy' },

&#x20;   { icon: Award, label: 'My Certificates', href: '/client/\[companyId]/certificates' },

&#x20; ],

};



export function Sidebar({ role, companyId }: SidebarProps) {

&#x20; const pathname = usePathname();

&#x20; const items = menuItems\[role] || \[];



&#x20; const getHref = (href: string) => {

&#x20;   if (companyId \&\& href.includes('\[companyId]')) {

&#x20;     return href.replace('\[companyId]', companyId);

&#x20;   }

&#x20;   return href;

&#x20; };



&#x20; return (

&#x20;   <aside className="w-64 bg-primary text-primary-foreground h-screen fixed left-0 top-0 overflow-y-auto">

&#x20;     <div className="p-6">

&#x20;       <div className="flex items-center gap-2 mb-8">

&#x20;         <div className="w-10 h-10 bg-accent rounded-lg flex items-center justify-center">

&#x20;           <span className="text-white font-bold text-xl">O</span>

&#x20;         </div>

&#x20;         <div>

&#x20;           <h1 className="font-display font-bold text-lg">Ops Solutions</h1>

&#x20;           <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">RevOps OS</p>

&#x20;         </div>

&#x20;       </div>



&#x20;       <nav className="space-y-1">

&#x20;         {items.map((item) => {

&#x20;           const href = getHref(item.href);

&#x20;           const isActive = pathname === href || pathname?.startsWith(href + '/');

&#x20;           

&#x20;           return (

&#x20;             <Link

&#x20;               key={item.href}

&#x20;               href={href}

&#x20;               className={cn(

&#x20;                 'flex items-center justify-between px-3 py-2 rounded-lg transition-colors',

&#x20;                 isActive

&#x20;                   ? 'bg-accent text-white'

&#x20;                   : 'hover:bg-primary-foreground/10'

&#x20;               )}

&#x20;             >

&#x20;               <div className="flex items-center gap-3">

&#x20;                 <item.icon className="w-5 h-5" />

&#x20;                 <span className="font-medium">{item.label}</span>

&#x20;               </div>

&#x20;               {isActive \&\& <ChevronRight className="w-4 h-4" />}

&#x20;             </Link>

&#x20;           );

&#x20;         })}

&#x20;       </nav>

&#x20;     </div>

&#x20;   </aside>

&#x20; );

}

\### components/analytics/FunnelChart.tsx

```typescript

'use client';



import { BarChart, Bar, XAxis, YAxis, CartesianGrid, Tooltip, ResponsiveContainer } from 'recharts';

import { FunnelStage } from '@/types';



interface FunnelChartProps {

&#x20;  {

&#x20;   stage: FunnelStage;

&#x20;   count: number;

&#x20;   conversion\_rate?: number;

&#x20; }\[];

&#x20; benchmarks?: {

&#x20;   stage: FunnelStage;

&#x20;   benchmark\_value: number;

&#x20; }\[];

}



const stageLabels: Record<FunnelStage, string> = {

&#x20; visitor: 'Visitor',

&#x20; subscriber: 'Subscriber',

&#x20; lead: 'Lead',

&#x20; mql: 'MQL',

&#x20; sql: 'SQL',

&#x20; opportunity: 'Opportunity',

&#x20; customer: 'Customer',

};



export function FunnelChart({ data, benchmarks }: FunnelChartProps) {

&#x20; const chartData = data.map((item) => ({

&#x20;   name: stageLabels\[item.stage],

&#x20;   count: item.count,

&#x20;   conversion\_rate: item.conversion\_rate,

&#x20;   benchmark: benchmarks?.find((b) => b.stage === item.stage)?.benchmark\_value || 0,

&#x20; }));



&#x20; return (

&#x20;   <div className="w-full h-80">

&#x20;     <ResponsiveContainer width="100%" height="100%">

&#x20;       <BarChart data={chartData} margin={{ top: 20, right: 30, left: 20, bottom: 5 }}>

&#x20;         <CartesianGrid strokeDasharray="3 3" stroke="#dce3ea" />

&#x20;         <XAxis dataKey="name" stroke="#8a9bb0" />

&#x20;         <YAxis stroke="#8a9bb0" />

&#x20;         <Tooltip

&#x20;           contentStyle={{

&#x20;             backgroundColor: '#ffffff',

&#x20;             border: '1px solid #dce3ea',

&#x20;             borderRadius: '8px',

&#x20;           }}

&#x20;         />

&#x20;         <Bar dataKey="count" fill="#425b76" radius={\[4, 4, 0, 0]} />

&#x20;         {benchmarks \&\& (

&#x20;           <Bar dataKey="benchmark" fill="#ff7a59" radius={\[4, 4, 0, 0]} opacity={0.6} />

&#x20;         )}

&#x20;       </BarChart>

&#x20;     </ResponsiveContainer>

&#x20;   </div>

&#x20; );

}

```



\### components/academy/ModulePlayer.tsx

```typescript

'use client';



import { useState } from 'react';

import { CourseModule, CompanyPlan } from '@/types';

import { Lock, Play, FileText, Video } from 'lucide-react';

import { Button } from '@/components/ui/button';

import { getPlanFeatures } from '@/lib/utils/roleHelpers';



interface ModulePlayerProps {

&#x20; module: CourseModule;

&#x20; isCompleted: boolean;

&#x20; isPreviousCompleted: boolean;

&#x20; companyPlan: CompanyPlan;

&#x20; onComplete: () => void;

}



export function ModulePlayer({

&#x20; module,

&#x20; isCompleted,

&#x20; isPreviousCompleted,

&#x20; companyPlan,

&#x20; onComplete,

}: ModulePlayerProps) {

&#x20; const \[isPlaying, setIsPlaying] = useState(false);

&#x20; const features = getPlanFeatures(companyPlan);



&#x20; const canAccess = module.content\_type === 'doc' || features.contentTypes.includes('video');



&#x20; if (!isPreviousCompleted \&\& module.is\_locked\_until\_prev) {

&#x20;   return (

&#x20;     <div className="p-6 bg-muted rounded-lg border border-border">

&#x20;       <div className="flex items-center gap-3 text-muted-foreground">

&#x20;         <Lock className="w-5 h-5" />

&#x20;         <span>Complete previous module to unlock</span>

&#x20;       </div>

&#x20;     </div>

&#x20;   );

&#x20; }



&#x20; if (!canAccess) {

&#x20;   return (

&#x20;     <div className="p-6 bg-muted rounded-lg border border-border">

&#x20;       <div className="flex items-center justify-between">

&#x20;         <div className="flex items-center gap-3">

&#x20;           <Video className="w-5 h-5 text-muted-foreground" />

&#x20;           <span className="text-muted-foreground">Video content requires Pro plan</span>

&#x20;         </div>

&#x20;         <Button variant="outline" size="sm">

&#x20;           Upgrade to Pro

&#x20;         </Button>

&#x20;       </div>

&#x20;     </div>

&#x20;   );

&#x20; }



&#x20; return (

&#x20;   <div className="p-6 bg-surface rounded-lg border border-border shadow-card">

&#x20;     <div className="flex items-start justify-between mb-4">

&#x20;       <div>

&#x20;         <h3 className="font-display font-semibold text-lg mb-1">{module.title}</h3>

&#x20;         {module.duration\_mins \&\& (

&#x20;           <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground">{module.duration\_mins} minutes</p>

&#x20;         )}

&#x20;       </div>

&#x20;       {isCompleted ? (

&#x20;         <span className="px-3 py-1 bg-success text-white text-sm rounded-full">

&#x20;           Completed

&#x20;         </span>

&#x20;       ) : (

&#x20;         module.content\_type === 'video' ? (

&#x20;           <Play className="w-6 h-6 text-accent" />

&#x20;         ) : (

&#x20;           <FileText className="w-6 h-6 text-primary" />

&#x20;         )

&#x20;       )}

&#x20;     </div>



&#x20;     {module.content\_type === 'video' \&\& module.video\_url \&\& (

&#x20;       <div className="mb-4">

&#x20;         <video

&#x20;           src={module.video\_url}

&#x20;           className="w-full rounded-lg"

&#x20;           controls

&#x20;           onPlay={() => setIsPlaying(true)}

&#x20;           onEnded={() => {

&#x20;             setIsPlaying(false);

&#x20;             if (!isCompleted) onComplete();

&#x20;           }}

&#x20;         />

&#x20;       </div>

&#x20;     )}



&#x20;     {module.doc\_url \&\& (

&#x20;       <div className="mb-4">

&#x20;         <iframe

&#x20;           src={module.doc\_url}

&#x20;           className="w-full h-96 rounded-lg border border-border"

&#x20;           title={module.title}

&#x20;         />

&#x20;       </div>

&#x20;     )}



&#x20;     {!isCompleted \&\& (

&#x20;       <Button onClick={onComplete} className="w-full">

&#x20;         {module.content\_type === 'video' ? 'Mark as Complete' : 'Complete Module'}

&#x20;       </Button>

&#x20;     )}

&#x20;   </div>

&#x20; );

}

```



\### components/enhancements/BeforeAfterCard.tsx

```typescript

'use client';



import { useState } from 'react';

import Image from 'next/image';

import { Enhancement } from '@/types';

import { ChevronLeft, ChevronRight } from 'lucide-react';

import { Button } from '@/components/ui/button';

import { Card, CardContent, CardHeader, CardTitle } from '@/components/ui/card';



interface BeforeAfterCardProps {

&#x20; enhancement: Enhancement;

}



export function BeforeAfterCard({ enhancement }: BeforeAfterCardProps) {

&#x20; const \[showAfter, setShowAfter] = useState(false);



&#x20; return (

&#x20;   <Card className="overflow-hidden">

&#x20;     <CardHeader>

&#x20;       <div className="flex items-start justify-between">

&#x20;         <div>

&#x20;           <CardTitle className="text-lg mb-1">{enhancement.title}</CardTitle>

&#x20;           {enhancement.description \&\& (

&#x20;             <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground">{enhancement.description}</p>

&#x20;           )}

&#x20;         </div>

&#x20;         {enhancement.impact\_metric \&\& (

&#x20;           <span className="px-3 py-1 bg-success/10 text-success text-sm rounded-full">

&#x20;             {enhancement.impact\_metric}

&#x20;           </span>

&#x20;         )}

&#x20;       </div>

&#x20;     </CardHeader>

&#x20;     <CardContent>

&#x20;       {enhancement.before\_image\_url \&\& enhancement.after\_image\_url ? (

&#x20;         <div className="relative">

&#x20;           <div className="relative h-64 rounded-lg overflow-hidden">

&#x20;             <Image

&#x20;               src={showAfter ? enhancement.after\_image\_url : enhancement.before\_image\_url}

&#x20;               alt={showAfter ? 'After' : 'Before'}

&#x20;               fill

&#x20;               className="object-cover transition-opacity duration-300"

&#x20;             />

&#x20;           </div>

&#x20;           <div className="flex items-center justify-center gap-4 mt-4">

&#x20;             <Button

&#x20;               variant={!showAfter ? 'default' : 'outline'}

&#x20;               size="sm"

&#x20;               onClick={() => setShowAfter(false)}

&#x20;             >

&#x20;               <ChevronLeft className="w-4 h-4 mr-1" />

&#x20;               Before

&#x20;             </Button>

&#x20;             <Button

&#x20;               variant={showAfter ? 'default' : 'outline'}

&#x20;               size="sm"

&#x20;               onClick={() => setShowAfter(true)}

&#x20;             >

&#x20;               After

&#x20;               <ChevronRight className="w-4 h-4 ml-1" />

&#x20;             </Button>

&#x20;           </div>

&#x20;         </div>

&#x20;       ) : (

&#x20;         <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground text-center py-8">

&#x20;           No images available

&#x20;         </p>

&#x20;       )}

&#x20;     </CardContent>

&#x20;   </Card>

&#x20; );

}

```

\## 8. Installation \& Deployment Instructions



\### README.md

```markdown

\# Ops Solutions - RevOps Operating System



\## Prerequisites



\- Node.js 18+

\- Supabase account

\- HubSpot Developer account

\- Google Gemini API key (optional)



\## Installation



1\. Clone the repository:

```bash

git clone https://github.com/mostafaesso/opsolutions.git

cd opsolutions

```



2\. Install dependencies:

```bash

npm install

```



3\. Copy environment variables:

```bash

cp .env.local.example .env.local

```



4\. Update `.env.local` with your credentials



5\. Set up Supabase:

```bash

npx supabase init

npx supabase link --project-ref YOUR\_PROJECT\_ID

npx supabase db push

```



6\. Run development server:

```bash

npm run dev

```



7\. Open \[http://localhost:3000](http://localhost:3000)



\## Deployment



\### Vercel



1\. Push to GitHub

2\. Import project in Vercel

3\. Add environment variables

4\. Deploy



\### Supabase



Ensure your Supabase project is set up with:

\- Row Level Security enabled

\- Storage buckets: `certificates`

\- Edge Functions deployed (if using)



\## Features



\- Multi-tenant architecture with RLS

\- HubSpot CRM integration

\- Role-based access control

\- Analytics \& funnel tracking

\- Training academy with certificates

\- Before/after enhancement tracking

\- HubSpot UI Extensions

\- Arabic RTL support



\## License



Proprietary - Ops Solutions Group LLC

```

\## 📁 SHARED/ — Cross-Phase Specifications



\### `SHARED/auth-spec.md`

```markdown

\# Authentication \& Identity Spec



\## Requirements

\- Supabase Auth (email/password + magic link)

\- Role-based access: superadmin | ops\_employee | client\_admin | client\_manager | client\_employee

\- Invite flow: token-based registration with pre-assigned role + company\_id

\- Session management: JWT with refresh tokens

\- Multi-language support: en/ar with user preference stored in profiles



\## Security

\- Password hashing: bcrypt

\- Rate limiting: 5 failed attempts/hour per IP

\- 2FA: Optional for client\_admin+ (Phase 3)

\- Session timeout: 24h inactive



\## Data Model

profiles table:

\- id (UUID, PK, references auth.users)

\- full\_name (TEXT, NOT NULL)

\- email (TEXT, UNIQUE, NOT NULL)

\- role (ENUM, NOT NULL)

\- company\_id (UUID, FK to companies)

\- manager\_id (UUID, FK to profiles, nullable)

\- hubspot\_user\_id (TEXT, nullable, for extension auth)

\- language\_preference (ENUM: 'en'/'ar', DEFAULT 'en')

\- is\_active (BOOLEAN, DEFAULT true)

\- created\_at, updated\_at (TIMESTAMPTZ)



\## RLS Policies

\- Users can only read profiles in their company

\- Superadmin/ops\_employee can read all profiles

\- Managers can read their assigned employees

```



\### `SHARED/branding-spec.md`

```markdown

\# White-Label Branding Spec



\## Requirements

\- Per-company branding config stored in companies.branding\_config JSONB

\- Dynamic CSS variables applied at runtime based on company\_id

\- Logo auto-fetch on company creation (logo.dev → Clearbit → Google fallback)

\- Support for Arabic RTL layout when language='ar'



\## Config Schema

branding\_config: {

&#x20; primary\_color: "#425b76",

&#x20; secondary\_color: "#333333", 

&#x20; accent\_color: "#ff7a59",

&#x20; logo\_url: "https://...",

&#x20; favicon\_url: "https://...",

&#x20; font\_family: "DM Sans" | "Tajawal",

&#x20; direction: "ltr" | "rtl"

}



\## Implementation

\- Use CSS custom properties (--color-primary, etc.)

\- Apply via <style> tag in layout.tsx based on company config

\- RTL support via tailwindcss-rtl + dir="rtl" attribute

\- Logo component: <CompanyLogo companyId={id} fallback="initials" />

```



\### `SHARED/rls-spec.md`

```markdown

\# Row Level Security Specification



\## Principle

Every table with company\_id must have RLS policies enforcing:

1\. Company isolation: users only see their company's data

2\. Role escalation: superadmin/ops\_employee can access all companies

3\. Granular visibility: updates/enhancements respect visibility arrays



\## Policy Template

```sql

\-- Example for updates table

CREATE POLICY updates\_company\_isolation ON updates

FOR SELECT USING (

&#x20; company\_id IN (

&#x20;   SELECT company\_id FROM profiles WHERE id = auth.uid()

&#x20; )

&#x20; OR EXISTS (

&#x20;   SELECT 1 FROM profiles 

&#x20;   WHERE id = auth.uid() 

&#x20;   AND role IN ('superadmin', 'ops\_employee')

&#x20; )

&#x20; OR auth.uid() = ANY(visible\_to\_users)

&#x20; OR role = ANY(visibility)

);

```



\## Testing

\- Test with anon role: should return 0 rows

\- Test with authenticated user: should only see their company

\- Test with superadmin: should see all companies

\- Test visibility arrays: user in visible\_to\_users should see update

```

\### `PHASE-1/user-stories.md`

```markdown

\# Phase 1 User Stories



\## SUPERADMIN (Mostafa)

AS a Super Admin

I WANT to create a new client company

SO THAT I can onboard them to the platform



ACCEPTANCE CRITERIA:

\- Form fields: name, website, domain, industry, employee\_count, region, plan

\- On domain entry: auto-fetch logo via logo.dev API

\- On submit: create company record + invite CLIENT\_ADMIN

\- Success: redirect to company detail page with "Setup HubSpot" CTA



\## CLIENT\_ADMIN (Ahmed @ JisrHR)

AS a Client Admin

I WANT to see my company's branded portal

SO THAT my team feels this is our internal tool



ACCEPTANCE CRITERIA:

\- Login redirects to /client/\[companyId]/overview

\- CSS variables applied from companies.branding\_config

\- Logo displays in top bar + sidebar

\- Language toggle switches EN/AR + RTL layout



\## OPS\_EMPLOYEE (Sarah @ Ops Solutions)

AS an Ops Employee

I WANT to post an update visible only to Client Managers

SO THAT I can share sensitive workflow changes



ACCEPTANCE CRITERIA:

\- UpdateForm has visibility multi-select: \[client\_admin, client\_manager, client\_employee]

\- Can also select specific users via searchable dropdown

\- Posted update appears in client portal for selected roles only

\- Internal comment toggle hides comment from client view



\## CLIENT\_EMPLOYEE (Fatima @ JisrHR)

AS a Client Employee

I WANT to see only updates assigned to me

SO THAT I'm not overwhelmed with irrelevant information



ACCEPTANCE CRITERIA:

\- Login shows minimal sidebar: Updates, Academy, Certificates

\- Updates feed filtered by visible\_to\_users OR visibility includes 'client\_employee'

\- Cannot see analytics, enhancements, or team management

\- Can comment on updates but not create them

```

\# Phase 1 API Contracts



\## POST /api/companies

Create new company (OPS roles only)



Request:

{

&#x20; "name": "JisrHR",

&#x20; "website": "https://jisrhr.com",

&#x20; "domain": "jisrhr.com",

&#x20; "industry": "SaaS",

&#x20; "employee\_count": "51-200",

&#x20; "region": "MENA",

&#x20; "plan": "pro",

&#x20; "admin\_email": "ahmed@jisrhr.com"

}



Response (201):

{

&#x20; "id": "uuid",

&#x20; "name": "JisrHR",

&#x20; "logo\_url": "https://logo.clearbit.com/jisrhr.com",

&#x20; "admin\_invite\_sent": true

}



\## POST /api/updates

Create update with visibility controls



Request:

{

&#x20; "company\_id": "uuid",

&#x20; "title": "HubSpot Workflow Optimization",

&#x20; "content": "<p>Automated lead assignment...</p>",

&#x20; "category": "hubspot",

&#x20; "visibility": \["client\_admin", "client\_manager"],

&#x20; "visible\_to\_users": \["uuid"], // optional specific users

&#x20; "before\_image\_url": "https://...",

&#x20; "after\_image\_url": "https://..."

}



Response (201):

{

&#x20; "id": "uuid",

&#x20; "created\_at": "2025-01-15T10:30:00Z",

&#x20; "visible\_to\_count": 3

}



\## GET /api/client/\[companyId]/updates

Fetch updates for authenticated user



Response (200):

{

&#x20; "updates": \[

&#x20;   {

&#x20;     "id": "uuid",

&#x20;     "title": "HubSpot Workflow Optimization",

&#x20;     "category": "hubspot",

&#x20;     "before\_image\_url": "https://...",

&#x20;     "after\_image\_url": "https://...",

&#x20;     "comments\_count": 2,

&#x20;   }

&#x20; ],

}

\### `PHASE-2/data-flow.md`

```markdown

\# Phase 2 Data Flow Specification



\## HubSpot Sync Architecture

```

HubSpot CRM 

&#x20;  │

&#x20;  ▼

\[Webhook: contact.property\_change] 

&#x20;  │

&#x20;  ▼

Supabase Edge Function (/api/hubspot/webhook)

&#x20;  │

&#x20;  ▼

Validate signature → Decrypt company token → Fetch updated record

&#x20;  │

&#x20;  ▼

Upsert to funnel\_metrics / form\_tracking tables

&#x20;  │

&#x20;  ▼

Trigger: if MQL count changed → recalculate conversion rates

&#x20;  │

&#x20;  ▼

Cache invalidation → Dashboard reflects new data

```



\## Token Security Flow

```

1\. OAuth callback receives access\_token + refresh\_token

2\. Edge Function encrypts tokens using pgcrypto:

&#x20;  - encrypt(accessToken, 'aes-256-cbc', project\_secret)

3\. Store encrypted tokens in companies.hubspot\_access\_token

4\. On API call: decrypt in Edge Function only (never client-side)

5\. Cron job checks token\_expires\_at < now+1h → refresh proactively

```



\## Funnel Calculation Logic

```sql

\-- Example: Lead → MQL conversion rate

WITH stage\_counts AS (

&#x20; SELECT 

&#x20;   stage,

&#x20;   COUNT(\*) as count

&#x20; FROM funnel\_metrics

&#x20; WHERE company\_id = 'uuid'

&#x20;   AND snapshot\_date = CURRENT\_DATE

&#x20; GROUP BY stage

)

SELECT 

&#x20; mql.count \* 100.0 / NULLIF(lead.count, 0) as lead\_to\_mql\_rate

FROM stage\_counts lead

CROSS JOIN stage\_counts mql

WHERE lead.stage = 'lead' AND mql.stage = 'mql';

```



\## Benchmark Comparison

```typescript

// lib/utils/benchmarks.ts

export function calculateVariance(metric: number, benchmark: number) {

&#x20; if (benchmark === 0) return null;

&#x20; return ((metric - benchmark) / benchmark \* 100).toFixed(1);

}



export function getVarianceStatus(variance: number | null) {

&#x20; if (variance === null) return 'unknown';

&#x20; if (variance >= 10) return 'above';

&#x20; if (variance <= -10) return 'below';

&#x20; return 'on-track';

}

```

```

\### `PHASE-3/certificate-spec.md`

```markdown

\# Certificate Generation Specification



\## Template System

```json

{

&#x20; "template\_id": "default-ops-solutions",

&#x20; "background\_image\_url": "certificates/templates/default-bg.png",

&#x20; "gemini\_prompt": "Professional certificate for {first\_name} {last\_name} completing {course\_name} on {date}. Navy blue (#425b76) and orange (#ff7a59) accents. Include Ops Solutions logo and Mostafa Ali signature.",

&#x20; "fields": {

&#x20;   "first\_name": { "required": true, "position": { "x": 600, "y": 420 }, "font": "bold 52px Sora" },

&#x20;   "last\_name": { "required": true, "position": { "x": 600, "y": 420 }, "font": "bold 52px Sora" },

&#x20;   "course\_name": { "required": true, "position": { "x": 600, "y": 490 }, "font": "28px DM Sans" },

&#x20;   "date": { "required": true, "position": { "x": 600, "y": 540 }, "font": "22px DM Sans" },

&#x20;   "signature": { "required": true, "url": "signatures/mostafa-ali.png", "position": { "x": 500, "y": 650 }, "size": { "w": 200, "h": 80 } }

&#x20; }

}

```



\## Generation Flow

```

1\. User completes final module → course\_progress.completed = true

2\. Trigger: check if all modules in course are complete

3\. If yes → call /api/certificates/generate with enrollment\_id

4\. Edge Function:

&#x20;  a. Fetch user, course, company, template data

&#x20;  b. Build Gemini prompt with dynamic fields

&#x20;  c. Generate image via Canvas API (fallback if Gemini fails)

&#x20;  d. Upload PNG to Supabase Storage: /certificates/\[company]/\[user]/\[course].png

&#x20;  e. Create certificates record with share\_token

5\. Return: { certificate\_url, share\_link }

6\. Send completion emails to manager/admin/ops

```



\## Share Page (/share/certificate/\[token])

```

\- Public route (no auth required)

\- Fetch certificate by share\_token

\- Display: generated image + download button + LinkedIn share

\- LinkedIn share: pre-filled post text with certificate URL

\- Security: token expires after 30 days (optional config)

\- Analytics: track views/shares per certificate

```



\## Arabic Support

```

\- If user.language\_preference = 'ar':

&#x20; - Certificate text rendered RTL

&#x20; - Font switched to Tajawal

&#x20; - Date format: Arabic locale (e.g., "١٥ يناير ٢٠٢٥")

&#x20; - Signature label: "مستشار عمليات الإيرادات"

```

```

\## Scope (OUT)

✅ Guidance card: loads <1s in HubSpot sidebar

✅ Completion sync: mark done in HubSpot → portal shows progress within 30s

✅ Social scrape: 90% success rate via Microlink, fallback to Puppeteer

✅ RTL layout: Arabic users see proper text direction + font

✅ Plan gating: basic plan shows 1 tip + upgrade prompt in extension

```



\### `PHASE-4/extension-spec.md`

```markdown

\# HubSpot UI Extension Specification



\## Extension Manifest (hubspot-extension/page.tsx)

```typescript

// Uses @hubspot/ui-extensions-sdk

export default function OpsGuidanceCard() {

&#x20; const extension = useExtension();

&#x20; const { recordId, objectType, lifecycleStage } = extension.context;

&#x20; 

&#x20; // Fetch guidance steps from our API

&#x20; const {  steps, companyPlan } = useGuidance({

&#x20;   portalId: extension.portalId,

&#x20;   stage: lifecycleStage,

&#x20;   userId: extension.user.userId

&#x20; });



&#x20; return (

&#x20;   <Card>

&#x20;     <CardHeader>

&#x20;       <Title>Ops Guidance</Title>

&#x20;       <Badge variant={companyPlan}>{companyPlan.toUpperCase()}</Badge>

&#x20;     </CardHeader>

&#x20;     <CardContent>

&#x20;       {steps.map(step => (

&#x20;         <GuidanceStep 

&#x20;           key={step.id}

&#x20;           step={step}

&#x20;           isCompleted={completedIds.includes(step.id)}

&#x20;           onComplete={() => markComplete(step.id, recordId)}

&#x20;           planLimit={getPlanFeatures(companyPlan).guidanceSteps}

&#x20;         />

&#x20;       ))}

&#x20;       {companyPlan === 'basic' \&\& steps.length > 1 \&\& (

&#x20;         <UpgradePrompt 

&#x20;           message="Unlock all guidance steps with Pro plan"

&#x20;           link="/ops/companies/\[id]?tab=billing"

&#x20;         />

&#x20;       )}

&#x20;     </CardContent>

&#x20;   </Card>

&#x20; );

}

```



\## Guidance Step Component Logic

```

Visual States:

\- Completed: ✅ checkmark, muted text, struck-through title

\- Current: ▶ arrow icon, accent color (#ff7a59), bold title

\- Locked: 🔒 lock icon, greyed out, tooltip "Complete previous step"



Actions:

\- Tip: info icon + expandable description

\- Task: checkbox + "Mark Done" button → calls /api/hubspot/complete

\- Sequence: HubSpot workflow link + "Launch" button

\- Academy: link to course module in portal + "Open Training"



Plan Gating:

\- Basic: show 1 step + locked steps with upgrade CTA

\- Pro: show up to 5 steps

\- Enterprise: show all steps + sequence recommendations

```



\## Social Scraper Architecture

```

Daily Cron Job (Supabase pg\_cron):

1\. Fetch companies with social profiles configured

2\. For each platform (LinkedIn/Twitter/IG/FB):

&#x20;  a. Call Microlink.io API: https://api.microlink.io?url=...

&#x20;  b. Parse response: followers, posts, engagement\_rate

&#x20;  c. If error/fallback: trigger Puppeteer Edge Function

&#x20;  d. Upsert to social\_metrics table with last\_scraped timestamp

3\. Rate limit: max 1 scrape/company/platform/24h

4\. Alert OPS if scrape fails 3x consecutive days



Manual Override:

\- Client Admin can edit scraped values in dashboard

\- Changes logged to audit\_trail table

\- Next auto-scrape will overwrite unless "lock\_value" flag set

```



\## Arabic RTL Implementation

```css

/\* globals.css \*/

\[dir="rtl"] {

&#x20; --font-body: var(--font-arabic); /\* Tajawal \*/

&#x20; text-align: right;

}



/\* Component-level RTL \*/

<GuidanceStep dir={userLanguage === 'ar' ? 'rtl' : 'ltr'}>

&#x20; <div className="flex {userLanguage === 'ar' ? 'flex-row-reverse' : ''}">

&#x20;   {/\* Icons flip position in RTL \*/}

&#x20;   {isCompleted ? <Check className="ml-2 rtl:mr-2 rtl:ml-0" /> : null}

&#x20;   <span>{step.title}</span>

&#x20; </div>

</GuidanceStep>

```



\## Testing Checklist

\- \[ ] Extension loads in HubSpot sandbox portal

\- \[ ] Guidance steps respect plan limits + completion state

\- \[ ] Completion webhook updates portal within 30s

\- \[ ] Social scraper handles LinkedIn rate limits gracefully

\- \[ ] Arabic layout: text direction, font, date format correct

\- \[ ] Mobile responsive: extension card works on HubSpot mobile app

```

\## 🌐 2. Product Vision \& Positioning

\*\*Ops Solutions RevOps OS\*\* is a multi-tenant SaaS platform that unifies:

1\. \*\*Client Portal\*\* → Branded workspace for agency clients to track progress, updates, and team activity

2\. \*\*HubSpot Execution Layer\*\* → In-CRM guidance, task sync, and lifecycle stage optimization

3\. \*\*Analytics Engine\*\* → Funnel tracking, form attribution, benchmark comparison, AI recommendations

4\. \*\*Academy \& Certification\*\* → Sequential training, plan-gated content, AI-generated certificates

5\. \*\*Change Documentation\*\* → Before/after snapshots, audit trails, and enhancement logs



\*\*Tagline:\*\* \*"Your RevOps Engine. Your Clients. One Workspace."\*  

\*\*Differentiator:\*\* Not another LMS or portal. A lifecycle-centric RevOps operating system built for consultants who implement, audit, and scale HubSpot CRM environments.



\---



\## 🏗️ 3. Technical Architecture

| Layer | Technology | Purpose |

|-------|------------|---------|

| \*\*Frontend\*\* | Next.js 14 (App Router), React, Tailwind CSS, Lovable Builder | Responsive SPA, white-label theming, RTL support |

| \*\*Backend/DB\*\* | Supabase (PostgreSQL, Auth, Storage, Edge Functions) | Multi-tenant isolation, RLS, encrypted tokens, media storage |

| \*\*CRM Integration\*\* | HubSpot API v3, OAuth 2.0, Webhooks, UI Extensions | Data sync, in-CRM guidance cards, task completion tracking |

| \*\*AI/ML\*\* | Google Gemini Pro Vision, Canvas API, Rule Engine | Certificate generation, recommendation engine, diagnostics |

| \*\*Scraping\*\* | Microlink.io API, Puppeteer Edge Function (fallback) | Social metrics without Meta/LinkedIn API dependencies |

| \*\*Deployment\*\* | Vercel (Frontend), Supabase (Backend), GitHub Actions (CI/CD) | Auto-deploy, environment management, monitoring |



\### 🔐 Security \& Compliance

\- Row Level Security (RLS) on every table

\- HubSpot tokens encrypted via `pgcrypto`

\- Signed URLs for certificate/media access

\- Rate limiting on HubSpot \& scraper endpoints

\- GDPR/CCPA data export/delete endpoints

\- Audit logging for all admin actions



\---



\## 🗄️ 4. Database Schema \& RLS Policies

```sql

\-- Core Tables (Supabase PostgreSQL)

CREATE TABLE companies (

&#x20; id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen\_random\_uuid(),

&#x20; name TEXT NOT NULL, website TEXT, domain TEXT UNIQUE,

&#x20; industry TEXT, employee\_count TEXT, country TEXT, region TEXT,

&#x20; logo\_url TEXT, plan TEXT DEFAULT 'basic' CHECK (plan IN ('basic','pro','enterprise')),

&#x20; hubspot\_portal\_id TEXT, hubspot\_access\_token TEXT, hubspot\_refresh\_token TEXT,

&#x20; token\_expires\_at TIMESTAMPTZ,

&#x20; branding\_config JSONB DEFAULT '{"primary":"#425b76","secondary":"#333333","accent":"#ff7a59"}',

&#x20; language TEXT DEFAULT 'en' CHECK (language IN ('en','ar')),

&#x20; created\_by UUID REFERENCES auth.users(id), created\_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT now(), updated\_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT now()

);



CREATE TABLE profiles (

&#x20; id UUID PRIMARY KEY REFERENCES auth.users(id),

&#x20; full\_name TEXT NOT NULL, email TEXT UNIQUE NOT NULL, avatar\_url TEXT,

&#x20; role TEXT NOT NULL CHECK (role IN ('superadmin','ops\_employee','client\_admin','client\_manager','client\_employee')),

&#x20; company\_id UUID REFERENCES companies(id), manager\_id UUID REFERENCES profiles(id),

&#x20; hubspot\_user\_id TEXT, is\_active BOOLEAN DEFAULT true, seen\_intro BOOLEAN DEFAULT false,

&#x20; created\_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT now()

);



CREATE TABLE funnel\_metrics (

&#x20; id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen\_random\_uuid(), company\_id UUID REFERENCES companies(id),

&#x20; snapshot\_date DATE DEFAULT CURRENT\_DATE,

&#x20; stage TEXT CHECK (stage IN ('visitor','subscriber','lead','mql','sql','opportunity','customer')),

&#x20; count INT DEFAULT 0, conversion\_rate DECIMAL(5,2), avg\_time\_in\_stage\_hours DECIMAL(8,2),

&#x20; source TEXT CHECK (source IN ('hubspot','manual','scraper')), created\_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT now()

);



CREATE TABLE form\_tracking (

&#x20; id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen\_random\_uuid(), company\_id UUID REFERENCES companies(id),

&#x20; form\_name TEXT NOT NULL, form\_type TEXT CHECK (form\_type IN ('lead\_1','lead\_2','subscriber\_1','subscriber\_2','custom')),

&#x20; hubspot\_form\_id TEXT, total\_submissions INT DEFAULT 0, with\_owner INT DEFAULT 0, without\_owner INT DEFAULT 0,

&#x20; offline\_submissions INT DEFAULT 0, source\_breakdown JSONB, last\_synced TIMESTAMPTZ, created\_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT now()

);



CREATE TABLE social\_metrics (

&#x20; id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen\_random\_uuid(), company\_id UUID REFERENCES companies(id),

&#x20; platform TEXT CHECK (platform IN ('linkedin','twitter','instagram','facebook')),

&#x20; profile\_url TEXT, followers\_count INT, posts\_count INT, avg\_engagement\_rate DECIMAL(5,2),

&#x20; last\_scraped TIMESTAMPTZ, scraper\_source TEXT CHECK (scraper\_source IN ('microlink','puppeteer','manual')),

&#x20; created\_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT now()

);



CREATE TABLE courses (

&#x20; id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen\_random\_uuid(), title TEXT NOT NULL, description TEXT, thumbnail\_url TEXT,

&#x20; order\_index INT DEFAULT 0, plan\_required TEXT DEFAULT 'basic', content\_type TEXT DEFAULT 'both' CHECK (content\_type IN ('doc','video','both')),

&#x20; is\_sequential BOOLEAN DEFAULT true, is\_published BOOLEAN DEFAULT false, created\_by UUID REFERENCES profiles(id), created\_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT now()

);



CREATE TABLE course\_modules (

&#x20; id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen\_random\_uuid(), course\_id UUID REFERENCES courses(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,

&#x20; title TEXT NOT NULL, order\_index INT DEFAULT 0, doc\_url TEXT, video\_url TEXT, duration\_mins INT,

&#x20; is\_locked\_until\_prev BOOLEAN DEFAULT true, quiz\_json JSONB, created\_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT now()

);



CREATE TABLE course\_progress (

&#x20; id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen\_random\_uuid(), user\_id UUID REFERENCES profiles(id),

&#x20; course\_id UUID REFERENCES courses(id), module\_id UUID REFERENCES course\_modules(id),

&#x20; company\_id UUID REFERENCES companies(id), completed BOOLEAN DEFAULT false,

&#x20; completed\_at TIMESTAMPTZ, time\_spent\_seconds INT DEFAULT 0, UNIQUE(user\_id, module\_id)

);



CREATE TABLE certificate\_templates (

&#x20; id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen\_random\_uuid(), company\_id UUID REFERENCES companies(id),

&#x20; template\_name TEXT, background\_image\_url TEXT, gemini\_prompt\_template TEXT,

&#x20; fields\_config JSONB DEFAULT '{"first\_name":true,"last\_name":true,"course\_name":true,"date":true,"signature":true}',

&#x20; is\_active BOOLEAN DEFAULT true, created\_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT now()

);



CREATE TABLE certificates (

&#x20; id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen\_random\_uuid(), enrollment\_id UUID REFERENCES course\_progress(id),

&#x20; generated\_image\_url TEXT, share\_token TEXT UNIQUE DEFAULT gen\_random\_uuid()::text,

&#x20; shared\_on\_linkedin BOOLEAN DEFAULT false, generated\_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT now()

);



CREATE TABLE enhancements (

&#x20; id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen\_random\_uuid(), company\_id UUID REFERENCES companies(id),

&#x20; area TEXT CHECK (area IN ('workflows','pipelines','properties','reports','sequences','custom')),

&#x20; title TEXT NOT NULL, description TEXT, before\_image\_url TEXT, after\_image\_url TEXT,

&#x20; impact\_metric TEXT, visible\_to\_roles TEXT\[] DEFAULT ARRAY\['client\_admin','client\_manager'],

&#x20; created\_by UUID REFERENCES profiles(id), created\_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT now()

);



CREATE TABLE updates (

&#x20; id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen\_random\_uuid(), company\_id UUID REFERENCES companies(id),

&#x20; title TEXT NOT NULL, content TEXT, category TEXT CHECK (category IN ('hubspot','process','training','general')),

&#x20; visibility TEXT\[] DEFAULT ARRAY\['client\_admin'], visible\_to\_users UUID\[],

&#x20; before\_image\_url TEXT, after\_image\_url TEXT, created\_by UUID REFERENCES profiles(id), created\_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT now()

);



CREATE TABLE comments (

&#x20; id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen\_random\_uuid(), update\_id UUID REFERENCES updates(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,

&#x20; user\_id UUID REFERENCES profiles(id), content TEXT NOT NULL, is\_internal BOOLEAN DEFAULT false, created\_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT now()

);



CREATE TABLE lifecycle\_guidance (

&#x20; id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen\_random\_uuid(), stage TEXT NOT NULL CHECK (stage IN ('visitor','subscriber','lead','mql','sql','opportunity','customer')),

&#x20; title TEXT NOT NULL, description TEXT, action\_label TEXT, action\_type TEXT CHECK (action\_type IN ('tip','task','sequence','alert','academy\_link')),

&#x20; academy\_module\_id UUID REFERENCES course\_modules(id), order\_index INT DEFAULT 0, plan\_required TEXT DEFAULT 'basic',

&#x20; is\_active BOOLEAN DEFAULT true, created\_by UUID REFERENCES profiles(id), created\_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT now()

);



CREATE TABLE guidance\_completions (

&#x20; id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen\_random\_uuid(), hubspot\_user\_id TEXT NOT NULL, hubspot\_record\_id TEXT NOT NULL,

&#x20; guidance\_id UUID REFERENCES lifecycle\_guidance(id), company\_id UUID REFERENCES companies(id),

&#x20; completed\_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT now(), UNIQUE(hubspot\_user\_id, hubspot\_record\_id, guidance\_id)

);



CREATE TABLE hubspot\_app\_installs (

&#x20; id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen\_random\_uuid(), company\_id UUID REFERENCES companies(id),

&#x20; hubspot\_portal\_id TEXT UNIQUE NOT NULL, access\_token TEXT, refresh\_token TEXT,

&#x20; token\_expires\_at TIMESTAMPTZ, installed\_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT now(), is\_active BOOLEAN DEFAULT true

);



CREATE TABLE industry\_benchmarks (

&#x20; id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen\_random\_uuid(), industry TEXT, region TEXT, stage TEXT,

&#x20; metric\_key TEXT, benchmark\_value NUMERIC, source TEXT, updated\_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT now()

);



\-- Enable RLS

ALTER TABLE companies ENABLE ROW LEVEL SECURITY;

ALTER TABLE profiles ENABLE ROW LEVEL SECURITY;

ALTER TABLE funnel\_metrics ENABLE ROW LEVEL SECURITY;

ALTER TABLE form\_tracking ENABLE ROW LEVEL SECURITY;

ALTER TABLE social\_metrics ENABLE ROW LEVEL SECURITY;

ALTER TABLE courses ENABLE ROW LEVEL SECURITY;

ALTER TABLE course\_modules ENABLE ROW LEVEL SECURITY;

ALTER TABLE course\_progress ENABLE ROW LEVEL SECURITY;

ALTER TABLE certificates ENABLE ROW LEVEL SECURITY;

ALTER TABLE enhancements ENABLE ROW LEVEL SECURITY;

ALTER TABLE updates ENABLE ROW LEVEL SECURITY;

ALTER TABLE comments ENABLE ROW LEVEL SECURITY;



\-- Example RLS Policy (Apply pattern to all tables)

CREATE POLICY company\_isolation ON companies FOR SELECT USING (

&#x20; id IN (SELECT company\_id FROM profiles WHERE id = auth.uid())

&#x20; OR EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM profiles WHERE id = auth.uid() AND role IN ('superadmin','ops\_employee'))

);

```



\---



\## 👥 5. Authentication \& Role Matrix

| Feature | Super Admin | Ops Employee | Client Admin | Client Manager | Client Employee |

|---------|------------|--------------|--------------|----------------|-----------------|

| Add/Edit Companies | ✅ | ✅ | ❌ | ❌ | ❌ |

| View All Companies | ✅ | ✅ (assigned) | ❌ | ❌ | ❌ |

| HubSpot Token Mgmt | ✅ | ✅ | ❌ | ❌ | ❌ |

| Invite Users | ✅ | ✅ (same company) | ✅ (≤ Manager) | ✅ (≤ Employee) | ❌ |

| Post Updates | ✅ | ✅ | ❌ | ❌ | ❌ |

| Comment on Updates | ✅ | ✅ | ✅ | ✅ | ✅ |

| View Analytics | ✅ | ✅ | ✅ | ✅ (assigned team) | ❌ |

| Manage Academy Content | ✅ | ✅ | ❌ | ❌ | ❌ |

| Take Courses | ✅ | ✅ | ✅ | ✅ | ✅ |

| Generate Certificate | ✅ | ✅ | ✅ | ✅ | ✅ |

| View Enhancements | ✅ | ✅ | ✅ | ✅ | ❌ |

| Configure Visibility Rules | ✅ | ✅ | ❌ | ❌ | ❌ |

| Access HubSpot UI Extension | ✅ | ✅ | ✅ | ✅ | ✅ (plan-gated) |



\*\*Auth Flow:\*\* Supabase Email/Password + Magic Link → Role-based routing middleware → Session JWT with refresh → 24h inactivity timeout.



\---



\## 🔌 6. Core API Routes \& Logic

\### `/api/hubspot/oauth/install`

Redirects to HubSpot OAuth consent with scopes: `crm.objects.contacts.read`, `crm.objects.deals.read`, `marketing.forms.read`, `analytics`, `oauth`.



\### `/api/hubspot/oauth/callback`

Exchanges code for tokens → encrypts with `pgcrypto` → matches `hubspot\_portal\_id` to company → stores in `hubspot\_app\_installs` → redirects to dashboard.



\### `/api/hubspot/guidance`

Accepts `portalId`, `lifecycleStage`, `userId` → fetches company plan → returns filtered `lifecycle\_guidance` steps + `completedIds` → powers HubSpot UI Extension card.



\### `/api/certificates/generate`

Triggered on course completion → fetches template + user data → Gemini/Canvas renders PNG → uploads to Supabase Storage → returns `share\_token` → sends email notifications.



\### `/api/social/scrape`

Accepts `companyId`, `platform`, `handle` → calls Microlink.io → fallback to Puppeteer Edge Function → upserts `social\_metrics` → rate-limited to 1/24h per platform.



\---



\## 🧩 7. Frontend Component Structure

```

src/

├── app/

│   ├── (auth)/login, /register, /invite/\[token]

│   ├── (dashboard)/ops/, /client/\[companyId]/

│   ├── api/ (routes above)

│   ├── hubspot-extension/page.tsx

│   └── share/certificate/\[token]/page.tsx

├── components/

│   ├── ui/ (shadcn base: button, card, dialog, table)

│   ├── layout/Sidebar.tsx, TopBar.tsx, RoleGate.tsx

│   ├── analytics/FunnelChart.tsx, BenchmarkCompare.tsx

│   ├── academy/ModulePlayer.tsx, CertificateGenerator.tsx

│   ├── enhancements/BeforeAfterCard.tsx

│   └── updates/UpdateForm.tsx, CommentThread.tsx

├── lib/

│   ├── supabase/client.ts, server.ts, middleware.ts

│   ├── hubspot/client.ts, oauth.ts, webhook.ts

│   ├── scrapers/socialScraper.ts, logoFetcher.ts

│   ├── certificates/generateCertificate.ts

│   └── utils/roleHelpers.ts, benchmarks.ts, cn.ts

├── types/index.ts

├── styles/globals.css (RTL + brand variables)

└── supabase/migrations/, seed.sql

```



\### 🎨 Brand System

}

```



\---



\## 🔄 8. HubSpot Integration \& UI Extension

\### Architecture

```

HubSpot Record (Contact/Deal) 

&#x20;  → UI Extension Card (@hubspot/ui-extensions-sdk)

&#x20;     → Calls /api/hubspot/guidance

&#x20;        → Supabase RLS + Plan Gating

&#x20;           → Returns steps + completion state

&#x20;              → Mark Done → /api/hubspot/complete

&#x20;                 → Updates portal analytics + notifications

```



\### Plan Gating Logic

| Feature | Basic | Pro | Enterprise |

|---------|-------|-----|------------|

| Guidance steps/stage | 1 | 5 | Unlimited |

| Academy link per step | ❌ | ✅ | ✅ |

| Sequence recommendation | ❌ | ✅ | ✅ |

| Manager visibility | ❌ | ✅ | ✅ |

| Upgrade prompt | ✅ | ❌ |  |



\### Token Management

\- Encrypted at rest via `pgcrypto`

\- Auto-refresh cron job (Supabase `pg\_cron`) 1h before expiry

\- Fallback alert to OPS if refresh fails 3x



\---



\## 🎓 9. Academy Engine \& Certificates

\### Sequential Learning Logic

\- Modules ordered by `order\_index`

\- `is\_locked\_until\_prev = true` → module N+1 disabled until N `completed = true`

\- Plan gating: `basic` → doc only, `pro/enterprise` → doc + video

\- Progress tracked in `course\_progress` with `time\_spent\_seconds`



\### Certificate Generation Flow

1\. Final module marked complete → trigger checks all modules in course

2\. Edge Function fetches `certificate\_templates` + user/company data

3\. Gemini prompt or Canvas API renders PNG with:

&#x20;  - `{first\_name} {last\_name}`, `{course\_name}`, `{date}`, signature, logo

4\. Upload to `/certificates/\[company]/\[user]/\[course].png`

5\. Create `certificates` record with `share\_token`

6\. Email notifications to manager/admin/ops

7\. Public `/share/certificate/\[token]` page with OG tags + LinkedIn share button



\### Arabic Localization

\- RTL layout flip + Tajawal font

\- Date format: Arabic locale

\- Signature label: "مستشار عمليات الإيرادات"

\- Gemini prompt adapted for Arabic text rendering



\---

| Phase | Focus | Timeline | Key Deliverables | Success Metrics |

|-------|-------|----------|------------------|-----------------|

| \*\*PHASE-0\*\* | Discovery \& Foundation | Week 0 | Supabase project, Next.js init, Figma design system, CI/CD, API contracts | ✅ Repo live, ✅ RLS tested, ✅ Design tokens applied |

| \*\*PHASE-1\*\* | Core Portal + Auth | Weeks 1-3 | Role-based auth, company CRUD, updates feed, enhancements, team invites | ✅ 100% permission accuracy, ✅ <5min onboarding, ✅ Logo fetch >95% |

| \*\*PHASE-2\*\* | Analytics + HubSpot Sync | Weeks 4-6 | OAuth flow, funnel sync, form attribution, benchmark overlay, recommendations | ✅ Sync <15min, ✅ Dashboard <2s load, ✅ Benchmark ±2% accuracy |

| \*\*PHASE-3\*\* | Academy + Certificates | Weeks 7-9 | Course management, sequential player, plan gating, cert generator, share page, notifications | ✅ Cert gen <10s, ✅ 100% sequential lock, ✅ >99% email delivery |

| \*\*PHASE-4\*\* | UI Extension + Social Scraper | Weeks 10-12 | HubSpot card, guidance sync, Microlink/Puppeteer scraper, Arabic RTL | ✅ Extension <1s load, ✅ Sync <30s, ✅ Scrape >90% success |

| \*\*PHASE-5\*\* | Intelligence + Scale | Weeks 13-16+ | AI recommendations, dynamic benchmarks, mobile PWA, white-label subdomains, audit trail | ✅ AI relevance >80%, ✅ PWA Lighthouse 95+, ✅ Subdomain <5min provision |



\### 🚦 Phase Gates

Before advancing:

\- \[ ] All acceptance criteria met

\- \[ ] Metrics targets achieved

\- \[ ] Security/RLS audit passed

\- \[ ] Mostafa UAT sign-off

\## ⚙️ 11. Setup, Deployment \& Environment

\### 📦 Prerequisites

\- Node.js 18+, npm/yarn

\- Supabase account \& project

\- HubSpot Developer account

\- Google Gemini API key

\- Vercel account (deployment)



\### 🛠️ Local Setup

```bash

git clone https://github.com/mostafaesso/opsolutions.git

cd opsolutions

npm install

cp .env.local.example .env.local

\# Fill .env.local with credentials

npx supabase init

npx supabase link --project-ref YOUR\_PROJECT\_ID

npx supabase db push

npm run dev

\# Open http://localhost:3000

```



\### 🔑 Environment Variables

```env

NEXT\_PUBLIC\_SUPABASE\_URL=your\_supabase\_url

NEXT\_PUBLIC\_SUPABASE\_ANON\_KEY=your\_anon\_key

SUPABASE\_SERVICE\_ROLE\_KEY=your\_service\_key

HUBSPOT\_CLIENT\_ID=your\_hubspot\_client\_id

HUBSPOT\_CLIENT\_SECRET=your\_hubspot\_client\_secret

NEXT\_PUBLIC\_LOGO\_DEV\_TOKEN=your\_logo\_dev\_token

MICROLINK\_API\_KEY=your\_microlink\_api\_key

GEMINI\_API\_KEY=your\_gemini\_api\_key

NEXT\_PUBLIC\_APP\_URL=http://localhost:3000

NEXTAUTH\_SECRET=your\_nextauth\_secret

NEXTAUTH\_URL=http://localhost:3000

```



\### 🚀 Deployment

1\. Push to `main` → GitHub Actions triggers Vercel deploy

2\. Supabase migrations auto-applied via CLI or dashboard

3\. Storage buckets: `certificates`, `company-logos` (public read, auth write)

4\. Edge Functions deployed via `supabase functions deploy`

5\. Custom domain: `app.opsolutionss.com` + SSL via Vercel

\## 📊 12. Success Metrics \& QA Checklist

\### 🎯 KPI Dashboard Targets

| Metric | Target | Measurement |

|--------|--------|-------------|

| User onboarding time | <5 min | Analytics event tracking |

| Dashboard load time | <2s (12mo data) | Lighthouse + RUM |

| HubSpot sync latency | <15 min | Webhook timestamp diff |

| Certificate generation | <10s | Edge Function logs |

| Social scrape success | >90% | Scraper service logs |

| AI recommendation acceptance | >60% | CTA click tracking |

| Arabic RTL QA pass | 100% | Manual + screenshot diff |



\### 🔒 Security Checklist

\- \[ ] RLS enabled on all tables with company isolation

\- \[ ] HubSpot tokens encrypted via `pgcrypto`

\- \[ ] No client-side token exposure

\- \[ ] Rate limiting on HubSpot \& scraper endpoints

\- \[ ] Certificate share links expire (optional config)

\- \[ ] Audit logs for admin actions

\- \[ ] GDPR/CCPA data export/delete endpoints

\- \[ ] Penetration test before Phase 3 launch

\## 📝 14. Development Workflow \& Conventions

\- \*\*Branching:\*\* `main` (protected) → `develop` → `feature/PHASE-X-description`

\- \*\*Commits:\*\* Conventional Commits (`feat:`, `fix:`, `docs:`, `chore:`)

\- \*\*Code Specs:\*\* Add `// Spec: PHASE-X/file.md#section` comments for traceability

\- \*\*Testing:\*\* Jest/React Testing Library + Supabase RLS policy tests + E2E (Playwright)

\- \*\*Linting:\*\* ESLint + Prettier + Husky pre-commit hooks

\- \*\*Documentation:\*\* This file is the source of truth. Update specs before code changes.
